# 4.1 Flow Control on F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U

## 4.1.0-1 Flow Control on F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U Document Owner SriRadhaKrishna P &#115;&#114;&#105;&#114;&#97;&#100;&#104;&#97;&#107;&#114;&#105;&#115;&#104;&#110;&#97;&#46;&#112;&#64;&#110;&#111;&#107;&#105;&#97;&#46;&#99;&#111;&#109; (ID: 11217602)

## 4.1.1 Common

### 4.1.1.0-1 Common Flow control - PDCP SN length configuration (ID: 11217612)

**4.1.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11217637`)

Common
5G-L2-HI shall support flow control over F1-U interface for,

* DRBs configured with 18 bits PDCP SN length with
* RLC AM mode using 18 bit RLC SN OR 12 bit RLC SN.
* RLC UM mode using 12 bit RLC SN
* DRBs configured with 12 bits PDCP SN length (NOTE: Flow control procedure remains the same).
* RLC AM mode using 12 bit RLC SN.
* [CB008963-B] RLC UM mode using 12 bit RLC SN [End CB008963-B]

The table below represents flow control support for different bearer types and PDCP SN sizes:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| PDCP SN Length | Flow control Support |  |  |  |
| RLC AM Mode |  | RLC UM Mode |  |  |
| Non-GBR | GBR (Non-VoNR) | Non GBR | GBR (Non-VoNR) |  |
| 18 Bit | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |
| 12 Bit | Yes | [Before CB008963-B] No [CB008963-B] Yes [End CB008963-B] | No | [Before CB008963-B] No [CB008963-B] Yes [End CB008963-B] |

---

### 4.1.1.0-2 Common Enabling flow control over F1-U. (ID: 11217645)

**4.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11217652`)

Common
5G-L2-HI shall on receiving Bearer Modify with DL F1-U TEID

* Set f1DataSendSuspended = false.

5G-L2-HI shall start monitoring the inactivity for the bearer as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6204\_replaced([11228392](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyhx8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 4.1.1.0-3 Common Handling of Flow control timer expiry (ID: 11217660)

**4.1.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11217664`)

Common
In case when  dlFlowControlAlgo is set to 3gppFlowControl

5G-L2-HI shall perform the following actions  defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5596\_replaced([11219830](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

### 4.1.1.0-5 Common Flow control disabled specific action. (ID: 11217732)

**4.1.1.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11217750`)

Common
5G-L2-HI shall disable flow control when dlFlowControlAlgo is set to None.

When flow control is disabled,

* PDCP PDU is sent as soon as it is received:
* SN is assigned using the TX\_NEXT variable according to 5G\_UP\_IF\_3535\_replaced([11531151](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWfpJ_v1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G-L2-HI shall use the SN to generate the PDCP Header and create PDCP PDU.
* Header compression using ROHC shall be performed according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5956\_replaced([11223173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kx_mafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* If Integrity Protection is enabled for the DRB, integrity protection of the PDCP SDU is performed according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11595\_replaced([11223772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyDQx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Ciphering of the PDCP SDU is performed according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6216\_replaced([11223741](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyDQwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* In case when  PDCP and RLC entities are co-located, send PDCP PDU over F1-U interface as defined in 5G\_L2\_6995\_replaced([11222994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_n_AfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Otherwise send PDCP PDU over F1-U interface as defined in 5G\_L2\_6992\_replaced([11222970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_nX_fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* If PDCP and RLC entities of 5G-L2-HI are co-located and if DRB is 5QI-1, [CB008118-A-UPD010]5QI 65 or 66[End CB008118-A-UPD010]
* PDCP PDUs shall be released upon reception of DDDS (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6474\_replaced([11217803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxgePPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Else,

* PDCP PDUs shall be released immediately after transmission over F1-U interface.

---

### 4.1.1.0-6 Common Initial DL data routing after the bearer setup (ID: 11217757)

**4.1.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11217768`)

Common
5G-L2-HI shall start sending the initial DL PDCP PDUs over F1-U or X2-U [CB008490-B] / Xn-U [End CB008490-B]  based on the vendor specific configurable parameter initialDLTrafficRouting.

---

### 4.1.1.0-7 Common UL Data Split Mode Indication (ID: 11217774)

**4.1.1.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11217779`)

Common
In case when  DDDS is received over F1-U with cause value IE = 3 (UL RADIO LINK OUTAGE),

* PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI shall send indication to informing about the UL RL OUTAGE to C-Plane.

In case when  DDDS is received over F1-U with cause value IE = 5 (UL RADIO LINK RESUME),

* PDCP entity of 5G-L2-HI shall send indication to informing about the UL RL RESUME to C-Plane.

Upon sending indication about UL RLC OUTAGE or UL RL RESUME to C-plane, L2-HI shall start UlSplitAckWaitTimer of duration **[Before PR666690] rdUlSplitWaitTimerDuration** [PR666690] rdUlSplitAckWaitTimerDuration **[End PR666690] [5G\_UP\_ALG\_3356\_replaced([11151756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksbw8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] for the bearer.**\*\*\*\*

L2-HI CU shall not take any action on receiving any subsequent DDDS over F1-U with cause value IE = 3 (UL RADIO LINK OUTAGE) or 5 (UL RADIO LINK RESUME) for the bearer while UlSplitAckWaitTimer is running. Upon receiving acknowledged by CPlane, 5G-L2-HI shall stop UlSplitAckWaitTimer.

**[Before PR666690] rdUlSplitWaitTimerDuration is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5353\_replaced([11218336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxjhkvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** [End PR66690]\*\*\*\*

**[PR666690] rdUlSplitAckWaitTimerDuration is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5353\_replaced([11218336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxjhkvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**[End PR666690]\*\*\*\*

---

### 4.1.1.0-8 Common ICMP/PING identification (ID: 11217785)

**4.1.1.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11217792`)

Common
5G-L2-HI shall identify the PDCP SDU as “ICMP” packet when below conditions are met

 Version is 4 AND Protocol is 1

OR

 Version is 6 AND Next Header is 58

The PDCP SDU is assumed to be IP packet.

The IP packet format is described in RFC 791 for IPv4 and RFC 2460 for IPV6

---

### 4.1.1.1 DDDS Handling

#### 4.1.1.1.0-1 DDDS Handling Handling of DDDS message (ID: 11217803)

**4.1.1.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11217831`)

DDDS Handling
Upon receiving Downlink Data Delivery Status (DDDS) indication over the F1-U or Secondary link,

gNB-CU-UP shall stop the corresponding timer tMaxPollingResp if running.

gNB-CU-UP shall perform the below actions:

1)   Check DDDS validity as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5308\_replaced([11217839](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhFQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If DDDS is not valid, skip the below step and exit handling the current DDDS.

2) Check and handle First F1-U DDDS as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5309\_replaced([11217853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhFQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3) Check and handle F1-U Final Frame Indication as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5310\_replaced([11217891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhFS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and exit the procedure.

3a)  In case of 5QI-1 [CB008118-A-UPD010], 5QI65 or 5QI66[End CB008118-A-UPD010] DRB,

* Peform the procedure specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14326\_replaced([11218152](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6cfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and skip the below steps.

4) Check and handle UL RL Outage/Resume for ENDC Split bearer as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5312\_replaced([11217902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhFTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5) Check and handle DL RLF Outage and RL Resume for:

a. Split bearer as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5315\_replaced([11217915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhFT_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

b. SA bearer as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5324\_replaced([11217978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: Split Bearer above is referred to both ENDC SN Split bearer and NR DC Split Bearer types

6) If "Lost Packet Report" IE is set to 1 (refer NOTE),

* Update the PDCP PDU lost counters.
* In case when  dlFlowControlAlgo is set to 3gppFlowControl, perform the procedure specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

7)  Update the flow control variables accordingly for F1-U or Xx-U as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5328\_replaced([11218096](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

8)  Check and handle Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Indication as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5325\_replaced([11217991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

8a) Check and handle Delivered Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6517\_replaced([11218123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTbPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

9) In case when  PDCP PDU(s) discarding is needed due to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5325\_replaced([11217991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), send discard indication as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6531\_replaced([11220543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

10) In case when  dlFlowControlAlgo is set to 3gppFlowControl, PDCP PDUs marked for retransmission shall be handled as defined in,

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7815\_replaced([11219186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpBEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if the DDDS is received over F1-U interface.
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7817\_replaced([11219584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxrdUvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if the DDDS is received over Xx-U interface.

NOTE:

1. Lost packet report should be handled before,
2. Flow control variables are updated.
3. "Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Indication" - to ensure the lost packets are marked for retransmission and not released based on "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number".
4. Steps 6 and 10 are not applicable as retransmissions for Intra gNB NR DC split bearers are not supported.
5. Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. For NR DC bearers, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Glossary.

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-2 DDDS Handling DDDS validity (ID: 11217839)

**4.1.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11217844`)

DDDS Handling
The below table show when the received DDDS is considered to be invalid.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Previous Highest Transmitted | Previous Highest Delivered | Current Highest Transmitted | Current Highest Delivered |
| Current Highest Transmitted | Greater | Greater | N/A | Greater |
|  | Less | Less | N/A | Less |
|  | Equal | Equal | N/A | Equal |
| Current Highest Delivered | Greater | Greater | Greater | N/A |
|  | Less | Less | Less | N/A |
|  | Equal | Equal | Equal | N/A |
|  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  | Valid DDDS |  |  |
|  |  | Invalid DDDS |  |  |

[5GC001354-A]

The below table show when the received DDDS is considered to be invalid for Retransmission IEs.

NOTE: NR-U SNs are compared corresponding to PDCP SNs in the IE.

The followng table is available in: <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/CFAMs/5GC1200-5GC1399/5GC001354%20Flow%20control%20fast%20retransmission/DDDS_table_5G_UP_%20ALG_5308.xlsx?d=wfffb6340b9de4858a6ae4f14d225d9bf&csf=1&web=1&e=4PKLe8>

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Retx IEs | Previous  Retransmitted | Previous successfully Delivered Retransmitted | Current  Retransmitted | Current successfully Delivered Retransmitted |
| Current  Retransmitted | Greater | Greater | N/A | Greater |
|  | Less | Less | N/A | Less |
|  | Equal | Equal | N/A | Equal |
| Current successfully Delivered Retransmitted | Greater | Greater | Greater | N/A |
|  | Less | Less | Less | N/A |
|  | Equal | Equal | Equal | N/A |
|  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  | Valid DDDS |  |  |
|  |  | Invalid DDDS |  |  |

[End 5GC001354-A]

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-3 DDDS Handling First F1-U DDDS Handling (ID: 11217853)

**4.1.1.1.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11217883`)

DDDS Handling
If it is the first F1-U DDDS message received by the bearer, 5G-L2-HI shall perform the following if "Final Frame Indication" (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5310\_replaced([11217891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhFS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not set to '1':

 Get "UeIdCu" from bearer index

 Send indication to CPlane informing reception of the first F1-U DDDS, only for the MCG link.

If DDDS is received on Primary

* Set firstDDDSreceivedOnPrimary to TRUE

Else if DDDS is received on Secondary

 Set firstDDDSreceivedOnSecondary to TRUE

[Before CB008490-D]

Note: Interworking of CNI-97376 with NR-DC is not supported. Support shall be added in a later sub-feature of CB008490.

[End CB008490-D]

Rationale:

While first DDDS is received (which means the UE RACH is successful), send indication to CPlane indicating successful RACH.

However, there is no need to send the indication to CPlane if FFI=1 since it indicates mobility is in progress.

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-4 DDDS Handling F1-U Final Frame Indication Handling (ID: 11217891)

**4.1.1.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11217896`)

DDDS Handling
In case when  F1-U DDDS contains "Final Frame Indication" IE = 1, 5G-L2-HI shall:

 Set f1DataSendSuspended = true.

 Ignore any new DDDS that is received on the F1-U link on which the DDDS with FFI = 1 is received.

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-5 DDDS Handling Uplink RL Outage/Resume handling for ENDC split bearer (ID: 11217902)

**4.1.1.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11217909`)

DDDS Handling
F1-U Uplink Radio Link Outage handling for Split Bearer

In case when all the conditions listed below are met:

 f1DataSendSuspended = false

 f1RlOutage = false

 F1-U DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 and "Cause value" IE = 3 (UL RADIO LINK OUTAGE)

 bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer

5G-L2-HI shall:

 Send UL Data Split Mode Indication to C-Plane as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5302\_replaced([11217774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxgeN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

F1-U Uplink Radio Link Resume handling for Split Bearer

In case when all the conditions listed below are met:

 f1DataSendSuspended = false

 f1RlOutage = false

 F1-U DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 and "Cause value" IE = 5 (UL RADIO LINK RESUME)

 bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer

5G-L2-HI shall:

 Send UL Data Split Mode Indication to C-Plane as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5302\_replaced([11217774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxgeN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-6 DDDS Handling RLF Outage and RL Resume handling for Split bearer (ID: 11217915)

**4.1.1.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11217928`)

DDDS Handling
 RLF outage and RL resume of the F1 interface shall be executed as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5318\_replaced([11217936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before CB008717-E]

 RLF outage and RL resume of the X2 interface shall be executed as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5321\_replaced([11217955](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008717-E]

[CB008717-E]

 RLF outage and RL resume of the secondary link shall be executed as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5321\_replaced([11217955](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: For NR DC Split Bearers, the handling for SCG F1-U is as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5321\_replaced([11217955](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008717-E]

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-7 DDDS Handling Handling of RLF outage and RL Resume for F1-U interface (ID: 11217936)

**4.1.1.1.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11217948`)

DDDS Handling
F1-U RLF Outage:

In case when all the conditions listed below are met:

f1DataSendSuspended = false AND xxDataSendSuspended= false

· f1RlOutage = false

· F1-U DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 and ("Cause value" IE = 1 OR 4)

[Before CB008717-E]

· bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer

[End CB008717-E]

[CB008717-E]

· bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer or NR DC Split Bearer

[End CB008717-E]

· pdcpKeyChangeOngoing = FALSE (Please refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6739\_replaced([11226634](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyWyyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

· dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U

5G-L2-HI shall:

· Stop transmission of DL PDCP PDUs over F1-U interface by setting f1RlOutage = true.

· In case dlFlowControlAlgo is set to 3gppFlowControl,

* For the PDCP PDUs that are not yet indicated as transmitted (derived from the IEs "Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" and "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") via DDDS message received over F1-U interface.

[Before CB008717-E]

* Mark the PDCP PDUs for retransmission over X2-U interface.

[End CB008717-E]

[CB008717-E]

* Mark the PDCP PDUs for retransmission over secondary link.

[End CB008717-E]

F1-U RL Resume:

In case when all the conditions listed below are met:

· f1RlOutage = true

· f1DataSendSuspended = false

· F1-U DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 and ("Cause value" IE = 2 OR 6)

[Before CB008717-E]

· bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer

[End CB008717-E]

[CB008717-E]

· bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer or NR DC Split Bearer

[End CB008717-E]

· pdcpKeyChangeOngoing = FALSE (Please refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6739\_replaced([11226634](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyWyyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

· dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U

5G-L2-HI shall:

· Set f1RlOutage = false

Rationale:

For SgNB initiated RLF case (DL RL Outage via DDDS)], Only the first DDDS shall be processed i.e. when F1-U is not yet suspended, or data is not yet switched to [Before CB008717-E]X2[End CB008717-E][CB008717-E]Secondary link[End CB008717-E].

Subsequent DDDS messages will be ignored since f1DataSendSuspended is set to TRUE and xxDataSendSuspended will be set to FALSE when data is switched.

Note:

1. Refer to 5G\_UP\_IF\_4031\_replaced([11535527](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tXMzxvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Cause Value details

2. Downlink Radio Link Outage via DDDS

a. Only DL RL Outage shall be considered for the RLF outage handling.

b. UL/DL RL Outage/Resume during intra/inter MeNB mobility is ignored as the F1-U and X2-U  tunnel are changing.

c. F1-U UL/DL RL Outage/Resume during PsCell Change is ignored as the F1-U and X2-U tunnel are changing.

[Before CB008717-DA]

3. dlDataSplitMode is a NIDD parameter. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008717-DA]

3. dlDataSplitMode is an algorithm parameter specific for EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent parameter is dlDataSplitModeNrDc. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008717-DA]

4. This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

5.   [CB008717-E] For NR DC Split Bearers, the f1RlOutage and f1DataSendSuspended flags refer to the MCG F1-U link [End CB008717-E]

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-8 DDDS Handling Handling of RLF outage and RL Resume for X2-U or Xn-U interface (ID: 11217955)

**4.1.1.1.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11217972`)

DDDS Handling
Secondary Link RLF Outage:

In case when all the conditions listed below are met:

· xxDataSendSuspended= false OR (xxDataSendSuspended = true AND tMaxDDDSWaitTimer is running)

· xxRlOutage = false

·           pdcpKeyChangeOngoing = FALSE (Please refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6739\_replaced([11226634](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyWyyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[Before CB008717-E]

· X2-U DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 AND ("Cause value" IE = 1 OR 3 OR 4)

·       bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer

5G-L2-HI shall

· Stop transmission of DL PDCP PDUs over X2-U interface by setting xxRlOutage = true.

[End CB008717-E]

[CB008717-E]

· Secondary link DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 AND ("Cause value" IE = 1 OR 3 OR 4)

·       bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer or NR DC Split Bearer

5G-L2-HI shall

· Stop transmission of DL PDCP PDUs over secondary link by setting xxRlOutage = true.

[End CB008717-E]

· In case dlFlowControlAlgo is set to 3gppFlowControl,

* For the PDCP PDUs that are not yet indicated as transmitted (derived from the IEs "Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" and "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") via DDDS message received over X2-U interface.
* Mark the PDCP PDUs for retransmission over F1-U interface.

Secondary Link RL Resume:

In case when all the conditions listed below are met:

· xxDataSendSuspended = false OR (xxDataSendSuspended= true AND tMaxDDDSWaitTimer is running)

· xxRlOutage = true

· pdcpKeyChangeOngoing = FALSE (Please refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6739\_replaced([11226634](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyWyyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[Before CB008717-E]

· bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer

· X2-U DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 and ("Cause value" IE = 2 OR 5 OR 6)

5G-L2-HI shall:

· Set xxRlOutage = false

· If xxDataSendSuspended = false, Initialise the X2-U flow control parameters.

Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008717-E]

[CB008717-E]

· bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer or NR DC Split Bearer

· Secondary link DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 and ("Cause value" IE = 2 OR 5 OR 6)

5G-L2-HI shall:

· Set xxRlOutage = false

· If xxDataSendSuspended = false, Initialise the Secondary link flow control parameters.

Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008717-E]

Note:

a.   Refer to 5G\_UP\_IF\_4031\_replaced([11535527](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tXMzxvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Cause Value details

b. X2-U RLF Outage/RL Resume Handling:

· RL Outage/Resume during intra/inter MeNB mobility is ignored as the F1-U and X2-U tunnel are changing.

· RL Outage/Resume during intra SgNB mobility, RL Outage/Resume will be handled as X2-U tunnel is not changing.

c.  This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

[CB008717-E]

d.   The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[End CB008717-E]

#### 4.1.1.1.0-9 DDDS Handling RLF Outage and RL Resume handling for SA Bearer (ID: 11217978)

**4.1.1.1.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11217983`)

DDDS Handling
F1-U RLF Outage:

In case when all theconditions listed below are met:

 f1DataSendSuspended = false

 f1RlOutage = false

 F1-U DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 and ("Cause value" IE = 1)

 Bearer Type = StandAlone Bearer

5G-L2-HI shall

 Suspend transmission of DL PDCP PDUs over F1-U interface by setting f1RlOutage = true.

F1-U RL Resume:

In case when all the conditions listed below are met:

 f1RlOutage = true

 f1DataSendSuspended = false

 F1-U DDDS contain "Cause report" IE = 1 and ("Cause value" IE = 2)

 Bearer Type = StandAlone Bearer

5G-L2-HI shall:

 Set f1RlOutage = false

#### 4.1.1.1.0-10 DDDS Handling Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Ind handling (ID: 11217991)

**4.1.1.1.0-10.0-3**  (ID: `11218014`)

DDDS Handling
For a non-GBR bearer with RLC AM mode

After receiving of Downlink Data Delivery Status (DDDS) indication over the F1-U or Secondary link (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6474\_replaced([11217803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxgePPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-CU-UP shall do the following:

IF the bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer

If Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

For each PDCP PDU (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the buffer with PDCP SN <= "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" IE received in F1-U DDDS message or Xx-U DDDS message accordingly taking into account the PDCP PDU sent over F1-U or Xx-U respectively, perform the following:

- IF the PDCP PDU is NOT marked for retransmission due to lost packet report (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15062\_replaced([11218021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) NOTE 5), perform the following:

• Update the data on flight as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8895\_replaced([11218035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

• If Data on Flight is decremented in above step, perform the following:

In case when the PDCP PDU is marked as duplicated,

• In case when the current DDDS is received over Xx-U, store the PDCP SN of the PDCP PDU for discarding over the F1-U interface. (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15062\_replaced([11218021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) NOTE 3 and 4)

Otherwise,

• Store the PDCP SN of the PDCP PDU for discarding over the other interface link. (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15062\_replaced([11218021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) NOTE 3)

• Perform the procedure specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the PDCP PDU.

• Release the PDCP PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15062\_replaced([11218021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) NOTE 1).

END

IF the bearerType = SA bearer

If Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

For each PDCP PDU (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the buffer with PDCP SN <= "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" IE received in F1-U DDDS message, perform the following:

- IF the PDCP PDU is NOT marked for retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

• Release the PDCP PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15062\_replaced([11218021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) NOTE 1)

END

IF the bearerType = SA Bearer with additional link configured (NR DC Split bearer) [CB008490-D]Refer to Note[End CB008490-D]

If Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Ind = 1 in either of the MCG or SCG F1-U DDDS message,

For each PDCP PDU in the buffer with PDCP SN <= "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" IE received in MCG F1-U DDDS message or SCG F1-U DDDS message accordingly taking into account the PDCP PDU sent over MCG F1-U or SCG F1-U respectively, perform the following:

 Release the PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15062\_replaced([11218021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) NOTE 1)

END

[CB008490-D]

NOTE:

For NR DC bearers, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

#### 4.1.1.1.0-11 DDDS Handling NOTE section for Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Ind handling (ID: 11218021)

**4.1.1.1.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11218027`)

DDDS Handling
NOTE section of 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5325\_replaced([11217991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Ind handling) is as follows:

[Before 5GC001354-C-UPD003]

1) For implementation of releasing PDCP PDUs, refer to 5G\_L2\_3938\_replaced([11226964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2__ycPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Duplicate PDCP PDU could be indicated as delivered via both the interface. It is always released when indicated as delivered for the first time on any given interface and delivered status from the other interface is ignored thereafter.

[End 5GC001354-C-UPD003]

[5GC001354-C-UPD003]

1) For implementation of releasing PDCP PDUs, refer to 5G\_L2\_3938\_replaced([11226964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2__ycPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Duplicate PDCP data PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8910\_replaced([11220484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or the PDCP data PDU retransmitted due to delay threshold based criteria (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7509\_replaced([11220415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuy_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) could be indicated as delivered via both the interface. It is always released when indicated as delivered for the first time on any given interface and delivered status from the other interface is ignored thereafter.

[End 5GC001354-C-UPD003]

[Before 5GC001354-C]

2) Since the PDCP PDU is duplicate, it is accounted in data on flight (dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx) on both interfaces. Hence when such packet is indicated as delivered on X2-U interface and is not yet indicated as transmitted (via DDDS) on the F1-U interface,  Data on Flight needs to be decremented on the F1-U interface.

[End 5GC001354-C]

[Before PR669984] [5GC001354-C]

2) If the PDCP PDU is sent (i.e. transmitted, retransmitted or duplicated) on both the interface links, it is accounted in data on flight (dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx) on both interfaces. Hence when such packet is indicated as delivered over one interface and is not yet indicated as transmitted (via DDDS) on the other interface,  Data on Flight needs to be decremented for the other interface since the PDCP PDU will be discarded.

[End 5GC001354-C] [End PR669984]

[PR669984]

2) If the PDCP PDU is sent (i.e. transmitted, retransmitted or duplicated) on both the interface links, it is accounted in data on flight (dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx) on both interfaces. Hence when such packet is indicated as delivered (derived from the IEs

"Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" or "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number")

via DDDS over one of the interface and is not yet indicated as transmitted (derived from the IEs

"Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" or "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") via DDDS

on the other interface, Data on Flight needs to be decremented for the other interface since the PDCP PDU will be discarded.

[End PR669984]

3) Since the PDCP PDU will be released in below steps, 5G-L2-HI should remember the PDCP SN.

4) Duplicated PDCP PDU is not requested to be discarded over X2-U when the PDU is delivered over F1-U to avoid eNB buffer becoming empty and causing additional duplication.

5) [5GC001354-A] gNB-DU may not consider PDCP PDUs lost over the interface while computing "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number", hence gNB-CU should check if PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission before releasing the PDU buffer. [End 5GC001354-A]

[5GC001354-C]

6) PDCP PDU may be sent over the other link due to duplication (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5599\_replaced([11219850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or when the Threshold 1 or 2 monitoring exceeds (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End 5GC001354-C]

#### 4.1.1.1.0-12 DDDS Handling Data on Flight handling during PDCP PDU release (ID: 11218035)

**4.1.1.1.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11218039`)

DDDS Handling
Decrement the data on flight (dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx) of the other interface link by PDCP PDU size (NOTE 2) if the following conditions are satisfied:

- In case when the PDCP PDU is also sent (i.e. transmitted/ retransmitted/ duplicated) over the other interface link (NOTE 1) AND

- Other interface link is not suspended(f1DataSendSuspended/ xXDataSendSuspended = FALSE) AND

- [Before PR669984] PDCP PDU was not indicated as transmitted (via DDDS) over the other interface link AND [End PR669984]

- [PR669984] PDCP PDU was not indicated as transmitted (derived from the IEs

"Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" and

"Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") via

DDDS over the other interface link AND [End PR669984]

- PDCP PDU was not indicated as lost (via DDDS) over the other interface link

NOTE:

1) PDCP PDU may be sent (i.e. transmitted, retransmitted or duplicated) over the other link,

* due to duplication (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5599\_replaced([11219850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or
* during mobility procedure (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6088\_replaced([11227013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZ2FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) / 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6080\_replaced([11226924](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZPBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* [5GC001354-C-UPD001] or due to delay threshold based PDCP PDU retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End 5GC001354-C-UPD001]

[Before PR669984]

2) If the PDCP PDU is sent (i.e. transmitted/ retransmitted/ duplicated) over both the interfaces, it is accounted in data on flight (dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx) on both interfaces. Hence when such packet is indicated as delivered on X2-U interface and is not yet indicated as transmitted (via DDDS) on the F1-U interface, Data on Flight needs to be decremented on the F1-U interface and vice versa.

[End PR669984]

[PR669984]

2) If the PDCP PDU is sent (i.e. transmitted/ retransmitted/ duplicated) over both the interfaces,

it is accounted in data on flight (dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx) on both interfaces.

Hence when such packet is indicated as delivered (derived from the IEs

"Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" or

"Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") via DDDS

on X2-U interface and is not yet indicated as transmitted (derived from the IEs

"Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" or

"Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") via DDDS on the F1-U interface,

Data on Flight needs to be decremented on the F1-U interface and vice versa.

[End PR669984]

#### 4.1.1.1.0-13 DDDS Handling Handling of the PDCP PDUs before the PDUs are released (ID: 11218047)

**4.1.1.1.0-13.0-2**  (ID: `11218061`)

DDDS Handling
Store the PDCP SN and the corresponding NR-U SN of F1-U and Secondary link interfaces for the PDCP PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15059\_replaced([11218066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) NOTE 2) when the following conditions are satisfied:

* PDCP PDU is sent (i.e. retransmitted/ duplicated) over both F1-U/ Secondary link interfaces (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15059\_replaced([11218066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) NOTE 1) AND
* PDCP PDU is not marked for retransmission AND

PDCP PDU has the highest PDCP SN among the PDCP PDUs to be released

[CB008490-D]

NOTE:

For NR DC bearers, the requirements mentioned above related to Secondary link are applicable. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NR DC Glossary for the definition of Primary and Secondary link.

[End CB008490-D]

#### 4.1.1.1.0-14 DDDS Handling NOTE section for Handling of the PDCP PDUs before the PDUs are released (ID: 11218066)

**4.1.1.1.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `11218078`)

DDDS Handling
11218078:
DDDS Handling
NOTE section of 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (Handling of the PDCP PDUs before the PDUs are released) is as follows:
1) PDCP PDU may be sent (i.e. retransmitted or duplicated) over the other link,
- due to duplication (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5599\_replaced([11219850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or
- [5GC001354-C-UPD001] or due to delay threshold based PDCP PDU retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End 5GC001354-C-UPD001]
 
2) The highest PDCP SN to be released and the corresponding NR-U SN of both the interface links are stored and processed as explained in the below example.
 
Link for the below table:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table with 6 steps. Each step has rows for PDCP SN, F1 NR-U SN, and X2 NR-U SN. The table also includes columns for DDDS, HTx, HDeliv, ReTx, and ReTxDeliv. Some cells are colored green, red, or yellow, indicating specific values or statuses.

|  | X2 NR-U SN |  |  | 3 | 2 |  |  |  |  |  | 4 X2 | 0 | 0 | 6 | 6 |  |  |  |  |

| PDCP SN 10 and 13 to 17 (mapped to NR-U SN 5 and  6 to 10) are sent over F1-U. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| -     Step 2: PDCP SN 11 (mapped to NR-U SN 1) is lost over X2-U. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| - Step 3: PDCP SN 11 is retransmitted (mapped to NR-U SN 3) over X2-U. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| -     Step 4: PDCP SNs 10 and 13 are indicated as successfully delivered over F1-U, hence released from the buffer. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| PDCP SN 18 (mapped to NR-U SN 4) is sent over X2-U. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| - Step 5: Delay threshold based retransmission condition is met for PDCP SN 14, 15, 16, |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| hence the PDUs are retransmitted over X2-U mapped to NR-U SN 5, 6, 7. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| - Step 6: Unidirectional link failure occurs over F1-U leading to release of PDCP PDUs sent over F1-U |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| i.e. PDCP SNs 14, 15, 16, 17 will be released from the buffer. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| The PDUs shall be released after storing the following: |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| \* “Highest released PDCP SN” sent over both the interfaces = 16 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| \* Corresponding X2-U NR-U SN = 7 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| \* Corresponding F1-U NR-U SN  = 9 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| - Case 1: DDDS is received over X2-U with "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" = 15. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NR-U SN corresponding to PDCP SN 15 sent over X2-U interface is not available since the PDU is released in step 6. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| However, the highest PDCP SN 16 and corresponding NR-U SNs are stored in step 6, |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| hence if the DDDS is received over X2-U with "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" (i.e. 15) < |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| “Highest released PDCP SN” (i.e. 16), perform the following: |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| o For each PDU sent over X2-U with PDCP SN < 15, if the X2-U NR-U SN < X2-U NR-U SN corresponding to “Highest released PDCP SN” (i.e. 7), release the PDU (i.e. PDCP PDU with SN 11, 12 shall be released). |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| - Case 2: DDDS is received over X2-U with “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” = 15. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| NR-U SN corresponding to PDCP SN 15 sent over X2-U interface is not available since the PDU is released in step 6. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| However, the highest PDCP SN 16 and corresponding NR-U SNs are stored in step 6, |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| hence if the DDDS is received over X2-U with “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” (i.e. 15) < |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| “Highest released PDCP SN” (i.e. 16), perform the following: |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| o For each PDU sent over X2-U with PDCP SN < 15, if the X2-U NR-U SN < X2-U NR-U SN corresponding to “Highest released PDCP SN” (i.e. 7), update the parameters retxdataOutFlowToMac, dataOutFlowToMac and dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5480\_replaced([11219139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxoaCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/ 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5544\_replaced([11219548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxq2S_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (i.e. parameters shall be updated for PDCP PDU with SN 11, 12). |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

#### 4.1.1.1.0-15 DDDS Handling Handling of DDDS Retransmissions IEs when the corresponding PDCP PDU is released (ID: 11218084)

**4.1.1.1.0-15.0-1**  (ID: `11218090`)

DDDS Handling
“Highest released PDCP SN” (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used in place of

“Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” and/or "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" IEs of the current DDDS message in case the following conditions are satisfied:

* PDCP PDU corresponding to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” and/or "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" is/are not available in the buffer AND
* “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” and/or "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" <= “Highest released PDCP SN”

NOTE:

1) Few examples where the above handling is required are as follows:

* “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” handling (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5480\_replaced([11219139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxoaCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5544\_replaced([11219548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxq2S_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" handling (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6517\_replaced([11218123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTbPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-16 DDDS Handling Handle updating of flow control parameter (ID: 11218096)

**4.1.1.1.0-16.0-1**  (ID: `11218103`)

DDDS Handling
Perform the below steps only if source IP address of the UL GTP-U PDU containing the F1-U DDDS = current F1-U IP address of the DRB.

In case when dlFlowControlAlgo is set to 3gppFlowControl

* Stop the tMaxPollingResp timer or xxDddsMaxPollRespTimer accordingly based on the DDDS received over F1-U or X2-U.
* 5G-L2-HI shall perform action defined in "5G\_UP\_ALG\_5462\_replaced([11218999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): 5G-L2-HI shall update the 3GPP F1-U flow control parameters" or "5G\_UP\_ALG\_5518\_replaced([11219421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): 5G-L2-HI shall update the 3GPP X2-U flow control parameters" accordingly for F1-U or [Before CB008717-B]X2-U interface[End CB008717-B][CB008717-B]X2-U interface in case of EN DC SN Split bearer and SCG F1-U in case of NR DC Split bearer [End CB008717-B].
* 5G-L2-HI shall perform action defined in “5G\_UP\_ALG\_5422\_replaced([11218786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxmk1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): Dl Gain Calculation

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-17 DDDS Handling Lost packet report handling (ID: 11218109)

**4.1.1.1.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11218115`)

DDDS Handling
Upon receiving "lost packet report" IE set to 1 in Downlink Data Delivery Status (DDDS) over the F1-U or X2-U and if (NRBTS/NRDRB.actLostPduFastRetx  is set to TRUE OR NRBTS/NRDRB.nsaDrbParam.actX2DuplicateTxNSA3x is set to TRUE), perform the following:

5G-L2-HI shall repeat the following steps "Number of lost NR-U Sequence Number ranges reported" times:

For each PDCP PDU mapped to respective NR-U SN starting from "Start of lost NR-U Sequence Number range" to "End of lost NR-U Sequence Number range" perform the following:

* In case when NRBTS/NRDRB.actLostPduFastRetx  is set to TRUE,
* The PDU shall NOT be marked for retransmission and skip the below steps,

1) lost PDU is the PDCP control PDU OR

2) lost PDU is the NR-U DUD without PDCP data PDU but with report polling set to '1' OR

3) lost PDU is the NR-U DUD with PDU discard indication and without PDCP data PDU OR

4) lost PDU is not found in PDCP buffer (NOTE 5) OR

5) lost PDU is a duplicated PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7573\_replaced([11220303](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvHz_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) OR

[5GC001354-C-UPD004]

6) lost PDU was retransmitted due to threshold monitoring on the other interface OR

7) lost PDU is marked for retransmission due to delay threshold monitoring.

[End 5GC001354-C-UPD004]

* PDCP PDU shall be marked for retransmission due to lost packet report [Before 5GC001354-C-UPD004] (NOTE 6) [End 5GC001354-C-UPD004] and the information shall be stored about the interface over which the packet was reported as lost.
* Decrement data on flight (dataOnFlight or dataOnFlightXx) of the interface over which the DDDS is received, by PDU size of the PDCP data PDU (NOTE 2, 3) [5GC001354-A-UPD001] if data on flight was not already decremented for the PDCP data PDU during unidirectional link reinitialization (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5336\_replaced([11218171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or DDDS missing (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5341\_replaced([11218220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End 5GC001354-A-UPD001]

NOTE:

1) "Number of lost NR-U Sequence Number ranges reported", "Start of lost NR-U Sequence Number range" and "End of lost NR-U Sequence Number range" are received in DDDS.

2) If the PDCP PDU is lost over the interface, data is not on flight for the corresponding PDU, hence data on flight should be updated.

3) For the below case over X2-U interface,

PDCP SN 105 sent with NR-U SN 10

DDDS polling with NR-U SN 11

DDDS received from X2-U with Lost report with NR-U SN 10 as lost.

dataOnFlightXx = size of PDCP SN 105, however eNB buffer would be empty.

PDCP would never send duplicate PDCP PDU toward X2-U since data on flight is non zero value.

Hence dataOnFlight should be decremented for packet which are indicated as lost.

4) PDCP PDU shall be retransmitted everytime the lost packet indication is received for the PDU as long as it is not the duplicated PDU.

(Rationale: This is a hypothetical case and not expected to occur often. Hence, there is no need of optimization.)

[Before 5GC001354-C-UPD003]

5) PDCP PDUs may be released for example during unidirectional link reinitialization (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5336\_replaced([11218171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [5GC001354-A-UPD001] or DDDS missing (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5341\_replaced([11218220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End 5GC001354-A-UPD001] on a particular link, and later the lost packet may be received in DDDS over the other link.

[End 5GC001354-C-UPD003]

[5GC001354-C-UPD003]

5) PDCP PDUs may be released for example in the following cases on a particular link, and later the lost packet may be received in DDDS over the other link:

* During unidirectional link reinitialization (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5336\_replaced([11218171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* DDDS missing (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5341\_replaced([11218220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* PDCP PDU initially sent over F1-U link and later retransmitted over X2-U link due to delay threshold based retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7509\_replaced([11220415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuy_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and ACK is received over F1-U link.

[End 5GC001354-C-UPD003]

[Before 5GC001354-C-UPD004]

6) In case the PDCP PDU was already marked for retransmission due to threshold monitoring (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), here it shall overwrite by marking the PDCP PDU for retransmission due to lost packet report since lost packet report handling is considered as higher priority.

[End 5GC001354-C-UPD004]

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-18 DDDS Handling Delivered Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind handling (ID: 11218123)

**4.1.1.1.0-18.0-3**  (ID: `11218145`)

DDDS Handling
After receiving of Downlink Data Delivery Status (DDDS) indication over the F1-U or XxU (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6474\_replaced([11217803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxgePPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-HI shall do the following:

IF the bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer [CB008490-D]OR SA bearer with additional link (NR DC Split bearer)[End CB008490-D]

If Delivered Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

For each retransmitted PDCP PDU (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the buffer with NR-U SN (NOTE 2)  <= NR-U SN mapped to "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" IE received in F1-U DDDS message or X2-U DDDS message accordingly taking into account the PDCP PDU sent over F1-U or Secondary link respectively, perform the following:

* IF the PDCP PDU is NOT marked for retransmission due to lost packet report (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and NOTE 7), perform the following:
* Update the data on flight as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8895\_replaced([11218035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* If Data on Flight is decremented in above step, perform the following:
* Store the PDCP SN of the PDCP PDU for discarding over the other interface link. (NOTE 5 and 8)
* Perform the procedure specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the PDCP PDU.
* Release the PDCP PDU (NOTE 1 and 3).

If the PDCP PDU corresponding to PDCP SN "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number"

received in the DDDS is not available in the buffer, perform the following:

If "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" received in the DDDS <= “Highest released PDCP SN” (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), release all the PDCP PDUs with NR-U SN < NR-U SN corresponding to “Highest released PDCP SN” over the interface.

END

IF the bearerType = SA bearer

If Delivered Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

For each retransmitted PDCP PDU (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the buffer with NR-U SN <= NR-U SN mapped to "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" IE received in F1-U DDDS message, perform the following:

-  IF the PDCP PDU is NOT marked for retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* Release the PDCP PDU.

END

IF the bearerType = SA bearer AND "SCG F1-U is Suspended" (refer Rationale)

If Delivered Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

For each retransmitted PDCP PDU (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the buffer with NR-U SN <= NR-U SN mapped to "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" IE received in F1-U DDDS message, perform the following:

* Release the PDCP PDU.

Rationale:

* The bearerType with value "SA bearer" is used for NR DC bearers (treated as SA bearers with one or more links) in the current implementation.
* During SCG Bearer takeback procedure for MN terminated Intra-gNB NR DC Split bearers, previously transmitted PDCP PDUs over SCG F1-U shall be retransmitted over MCG F1-U (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15266\_replaced([11226442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyVkofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The retransmission shall start on SCG F1-U suspension and can continue post SCG F1-U release, if there are ongoing PDCP PDU retransmissions.

END

NOTE:

1) For implementation of releasing PDCP PDUs, refer to 5G\_L2\_3938\_replaced([11226964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2__ycPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) PDCP SN mapping to NR-U SN shall be maintained for each PDCP data PDU at 5G-L2-HI.

3) Duplicate PDCP data PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8910\_replaced([11220484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or the PDCP data PDU retransmitted due to delay threshold based criteria (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7509\_replaced([11220415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuy_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) could be indicated as delivered via both the interface. It is always released when indicated as delivered (derived from the IEs "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" or "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") for the first time on any given interface and delivered status from the other interface is ignored thereafter.

4) If the PDCP PDU is sent on both the interface links, it is accounted in data on flight (dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx) on both interfaces. Hence when such packet is indicated as delivered (derived from the IEs "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" or "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") via DDDS over one of the interface and is not yet indicated as transmitted (derived from the IEs "Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" or "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") via DDDS on the other interface, Data on Flight needs to be decremented for the other interface since the PDCP PDU will be discarded.

5) Since the PDCP PDU will be released in below steps, 5G-L2-HI should remember the PDCP SN.

6) Duplicated PDCP PDU is not requested to be discarded over X2-U when the PDU is delivered over F1-U to avoid eNB buffer becoming empty and requiring additional duplication.

7) gNB-DU may not consider PDCP PDUs lost over the interface while computing  "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number", hence gNB-CU should check if PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission before releasing the PDU buffer.

8) PDCP PDU may be sent over the other link when the delay threshold 1 or 2 criteria is met (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB008490-D]

9) Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NR DC Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

---

#### 4.1.1.1.0-19 DDDS Handling DDDS handling when flow control is disabled (ID: 11218152)

**4.1.1.1.0-19.0-1**  (ID: `11218157`)

DDDS Handling
5G-L2-HI shall handle the DDDS when dlFlowControlAlgo is set to None as described below:

If PDCP and RLC entities of 5G-L2-HI are co-located,

* If Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1, release all the PDCP PDU(s) with

PDCP SN <= "Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" IE received in the DDDS message.

---

### 4.1.1.2 Handling for missing DDDS

#### 4.1.1.2.0-1 Handling for missing DDDS Invoke DDDS report missing actions over F1-U/X2-U/Xn-U interface (ID: 11218171)

**4.1.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11218184`)

Handling for missing DDDS
5G-L2-HI shall detect interface link failure based on missing DDDS on that link.

* If the flow control is disabled for the DRB, skip the below procedure.
* [Before CB008717-E] If PDCP and RLC are colocated, skip the below procedure for F1-U Interface. [End CB008717-E]
* [CB008717-E]DDDS Polling is applicable only for links where 5G-L2-HI PDCP and 5G-L2-HI RLC are non-colocated. The following procedure is to be skipped for both F1-U and Secondary link F1-U in colocated deployment.[End CB008717-E]
* [Before CB008717-E] F1-U/ X2-U link is detected as failed, if DDDS has not been received on the corresponding interface link for more than rdDddsReportMissingTimeout ms and data transmission over the corresponding link was not suspended (ie xxDataSendSuspended/f1DataSendSuspended is false) and PDCP SDU and PDU buffer is not empty.  rdDddsReportMissingTimeout is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5374\_replaced([11218453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008717-E]
* [CB008717-E]F1-U/ Secondary link is detected as failed, if DDDS has not been received on the corresponding interface link for more than rdDddsReportMissingTimeout ms and data transmission over the corresponding link was not suspended (ie xxDataSendSuspended/f1DataSendSuspended is false) and PDCP SDU and PDU buffer is not empty.  rdDddsReportMissingTimeout is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5374\_replaced([11218453](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008717-E]

[Before CB008717-E]

When F1-U/X2-U link is detected as failed, [End CB008717-E]

[CB008717-E]

When F1-U/Secondary link is detected as failed, [End CB008717-E]

* 5G-L2-HI shall initialize the impacted [Before CB008717-E](F1-U or X2-U)[End CB008717-E] [CB008717-E](F1-U or Secondary link)[End CB008717-E] interface parameter as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) accordingly.
* Update the data on flight as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8895\_replaced([11218035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for each PDCP PDU sent over the impacted interface.
* Perform the procedure specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for each PDCP PDU sent over the impacted interface.
* Stop the delay threshold monitoring procedure for all the PDCP PDUs as

defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7580\_replaced([11220420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* If any of the PDCP PDU(s) is marked for retransmission over the impacted interface due to

delay threshold monitoring (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), remove the marking for retransmission of

the PDCP PDU(s) since the impacted interface is currently not available. (refer NOTE 4).

* 5G-L2-HI shall release the following PDCP PDUs:
* PDCP PDUs which were sent (i.e. Transmitted/ Retransmitted/ Duplicated) over the impacted interface.
* PDCP PDUs marked for retransmission due to lost packet report received over impacted interface.
* For F1-U link failure, set f1DataSendPaused = TRUE.
* For bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer
* Set initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE
* In case dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UX2U

1. In case f1DataSendPaused = TRUE AND xxDataSendPaused = TRUE, proceed with action defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5339\_replaced([11218193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6d_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* In case dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1U

1. In case f1DataSendPaused = TRUE, proceed with action defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5339\_replaced([11218193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6d_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* In case dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverX2U

1. In case xxDataSendPaused = TRUE, proceed with action defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5339\_replaced([11218193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6d_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* For bearerType = SA
* In case f1DataSendPaused = TRUE, proceed with action defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5339\_replaced([11218193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6d_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* [CB008717-E] For bearerType = NR DC Split Bearer
* Set initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE
* In case dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UX2U

1. In case f1DataSendPaused = TRUE AND xxDataSendPaused = TRUE, proceed with action defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5339\_replaced([11218193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6d_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* In case dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1U

1. In case f1DataSendPaused = TRUE, proceed with action defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5339\_replaced([11218193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6d_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* In case dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverX2U

1. In case xxDataSendPaused = TRUE, proceed with action defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5339\_replaced([11218193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6d_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008717-E]

Note:

1)  [Before CB008717-E]When data transmission is stopped over F1-U or X2-U (f1DataSendPaused or xxDataSendPaused set to TRUE), polling is continued over the respective interface using F1-U/ X2-U Downlink User Data with empty payload. [End CB008717-E]

[CB008717-E] When data transmission is stopped over F1-U or Secondary link (f1DataSendPaused or xxDataSendPaused set to TRUE), in case of non-colocated 5G-L2-HI CU & 5G-L2-HI DU, polling is continued over the respective interface using F1-U/Secondary link Downlink User Data with empty payload. [End CB008717-E]

[Before CB008717-DA]

2) dlDataSplitMode is a NIDD parameter. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008717-DA]

2) dlDataSplitMode is an algorithm parameter specific for EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent parameter is dlDataSplitModeNrDc. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008717-DA]

3) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

4)   If the PDCP PDU was sent over interface X and later marked for retransmission over interface Y due to

delay threshold monitoring and if the unidir link failure has occurred on interface Y, retransmission can

be done over the interface Y only after link is re-initialized which introduces additional delay.

This defeats the purpose of delay threshold based retransmission, hence the retransmission

marking should be removed.

Rationale:

[Before CB008717-E]

During Initial Data Routing if the DDDS is not received over either F1-U or X2-U, it is better to switch to the working link. This is achieved by ending Initial Data routing.[End CB008717-E]

[CB008717-E]

During Initial Data Routing if the DDDS is not received over either F1-U or Secondary link, it is better to switch to the working link. This is achieved by ending Initial Data routing.[End CB008717-E]

---

#### 4.1.1.2.0-2 Handling for missing DDDS 5G-L2-HI shall perform F1-U/X2-U interface failure actions. (ID: 11218193)

**4.1.1.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11218207`)

Handling for missing DDDS
5G-L2-HI shall start a recovery timer tLinkRecoveryWait on detecting F1-U/[Before CB008717-E]X2-U[End CB008717-E] [CB008717-E]Secondary link[End CB008717-E] interface failure.

The F1-U/[Before CB008717-E]X2-U[End CB008717-E] [CB008717-E]Secondary link[End CB008717-E] interface failure is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5336\_replaced([11218171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6dPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Timer value is defined by R&D parameter rdLinkRecoveryTimeout(defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5372\_replaced([11218427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkInfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

On receiving the first DDDS message on the failed link,

* 5G-L2-HI shall stop the timer tLinkRecoveryWait.
* Start the delay threshold monitoring procedure for the new PDCP PDUs sent after receiving first DDDS as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7580\_replaced([11220420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

On tLinkRecoveryWait timer expiry, 5G-L2-HI shall send inform CPlane about the failure.

---

### 4.1.1.3 Handling of Unidirectional Link failure

#### 4.1.1.3.0-1 Handling of Unidirectional Link failure Invoke link re-initialization action over F1-U/ X2-U or Xn-U interface. (ID: 11218220)

**4.1.1.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11218233`)

Handling of Unidirectional Link failure
gNB-CU-UP shall:

 Initialize the impacted (F1-U or X2-U) interface parameter as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) accordingly.

* Update the data on flight as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8895\_replaced([11218035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for each PDCP PDU sent over the impacted interface.
* Perform the procedure specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for each PDCP PDU

sent over the impacted interface.

* Stop the delay threshold monitoring procedure for all the PDCP PDUs as

defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7580\_replaced([11220420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* If any of the PDCP PDU(s) is marked for retransmission over the impacted interface due to

delay threshold monitoring (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), remove the marking for retransmission of

the PDCP PDU(s) since the impacted interface is currently not available. (refer NOTE 4).

 Release the following PDCP PDUs:

* PDCP PDUs which were sent (i.e. Transmitted/ Retransmitted/ Duplicated) over the impacted interface.
* PDCP PDUs marked for retransmission due to lost packet report received over impacted interface.

 For F1-U link failure, set f1DataSendPaused = True, linkReintPerformed = True

 For X2-U link failure, set xxDataSendPaused = True, linkReintPerformedXx = True

 Set lastSnSentBeforeLinkReinit = Highest SN of the PDCP PDU sent over F1-U excluding

* PDCP PDU which were requested to be discarded according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5325\_replaced([11217991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* retransmitted PDCP PDU (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx" - refer NOTE 3 )
* "PDCP PDU marked for retransmission" (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Set lastSnSentBeforeLinkReinitXx = Highest SN of the PDCP PDU sent over X2-U excluding,

* PDCP PDU which were requested to be discarded according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5325\_replaced([11217991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* retransmitted PDCP PDU (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx" - refer NOTE 3 )
* "PDCP PDU marked for retransmission" (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

NOTE:

1) When data transmission is stopped over F1-U or X2-U (f1DataSendPaused or xxDataSendPaused set to TRUE), polling is continued over the respective interface using F1-U/ X2-U Downlink User Data with empty payload.

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

3) Retransmitted PDUs are not considered during link re-initialization to avoid complexity.

4)  If the PDCP PDU was sent over interface X and later marked for retransmission over interface Y

due to delay threshold monitoring and if the unidir link failure has occurred on interface Y, retransmission can be done over the interface Y only after link is re-initialized which introduces

additional delay. This defeats the purpose of delay threshold based retransmission, hence the retransmission marking should be removed.

[CB008490-D]

5) For Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only, all the above requirements related to PDCP Fast retransmission are applicable. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

---

### 4.1.1.4 Handling of data burst

### 4.1.1.4-1 Handling of data burst

#### 4.1.1.4-1.0-1 Handling of data burst PDCP SDU transmission is not allowed when difference between oldest non acked PDCP PDU and last sent is equal or greater than Window_Size(5G_UP_IF_3774_replaced( 11533557 )) (ID: 11218317)

#### 4.1.1.4.0-1 Handling of data burst Choose interface during start of a data burst (ID: 11218246)

**4.1.1.4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11218269`)

Handling of data burst
In case when  dlFlowControlAlgo is 3gppFlowControl, sendingOverXx shall be set to True when below conditon are met

* flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = TRUE AND dataOnFlightXx < DBSXx \* rdDbsScaleFactorCalibrationXx

OR

* flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = FALSE AND estimated latency pduDeliveryDelayXx <= pduDelvDelayLimitXx

5G-L2-HI shall choose Secondary link, when the below conditions are met.

[Before CNI-97440]

 PDCP SDU is not “icmp” packet. “icmp” packet identification is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5303\_replaced([11217785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxgeOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CNI-97440]

 dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U

 actPrioritizeX2AfterInactivity= True

 preferXxInterface = True

 sendingOverXx = True

[Before CNI-97376]

 (initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = TRUE AND initialDLTrafficRouting = initDLoverX2U) OR initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE (refer Rationale)

[End CNI-97376]

In case when Secondary link is not chosen above, 5G-L2-HI shall choose Primary when below conditions are met

 dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U

 actPrioritizeX2AfterInactivity = True

 preferXxInterface = True

 Unsent PDCP Buffer/estTputXx >= dlDataSplitBufferBuildUpThresholdPrioritizeX2

 firstDDDSreceivedOnPrimary = TRUE

initialDLTrafficRouting, dlFlowControlAlgo, dlDataSplitMode, actPrioritizeX2AfterInactivity and dlDataSplitBufferBuildUpThresholdPrioritizeX2 are algorithm parameters specific to EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, refer to equivalent parameters initialDLTrafficRoutingNrDc, dlDataSplitModeNrDc, actPrioritizeXxAfterInactivityNrDc and dlDataSplitBufferBuildUpThresholdPrioritizeXxNrDc. These parameters (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are received during Bearer Setup and Bearer modification.

rdDbsScaleFactorCalibrationXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17015\_replaced([11220735](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rationale:

Secondary link should not be prioritized when initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = TRUE AND initialDLTrafficRouting = initDLoverF1U since F1-U link is the first preference. Below shown is the list of scenarios that impacts Secondary link prioritization functionality.

1) BearerSetup / Inter gNB Mobility:

a. If initial phase of traffic routing is ongoing and initial traffic routing preference is Primary link, initial Secondary link prioritization is not applied.

b. If initial phase of traffic routing is ongoing and initial traffic routing preference is Secondary link, initial Secondary link prioritization is applied.

c. After the initial phase of traffic routing is completed, Secondary link prioritization will be applied as per the NIDD setting for Secondary link prioritization.

2) Flow control inactivity for Primary link / Secondary link:

a. After the interface link comes out of inactivity, initial Secondary link prioritization will be applied as per the NIDD setting for Secondary link prioritization.

3) Intra gNB Mobility:

a. If Key change is enabled (i.e. PDCP re-establishment), initial phase of traffic routing is considered as ongoing and initial traffic routing preference is Primary link, hence initial Secondary link prioritization is not applied.

b. If Key change is not enabled, data transmission will continue over Secondary link when Primary link is being re-configured. Initial Secondary link prioritization will be applied as per the NIDD setting for Secondary link prioritization.

Note:

1) initialDLTrafficRouting, actPrioritizeX2AfterInactivity, dlDataSplitBufferBuildUpThreshold, dlDataSplitBufferBuildUpThresholdPrioritizeX2 and dlDataSplitMode are algorithm parameters specific to EN DC bearers. initialDLTrafficRoutingNrDc, actPrioritizeXxAfterInactivityNrDc, dlDataSplitBufferBuildUpThresholdNrDc, dlDataSplitBufferBuildUpThresholdPrioritizeXxNrDc and dlDataSplitModeNrDc are NR DC equivalent parameters. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

---

#### 4.1.1.4.0-2 Handling of data burst Prefer X2-U or Xn-U interface during start of a data burst (ID: 11218275)

**4.1.1.4.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11218303`)

Handling of data burst
In the case of ENDC and when actPrioritizeX2AfterInactivity (see NOTE 2) is set to true, on reception of first PDCP SDU either after Bearer Setup OR when PDCP buffer remain empty (refer NOTE 1) for more than t1 duration,

 Set preferX2StartTime = currentTime

 Set preferXxInterface = True

In case when  preferXxInterface = True AND when PDCP buffer remain empty (refer NOTE 1) for more than t2 duration AND (t3 – (currentTime - preferX2StartTime ) > t1)

 Set preferX2StartTime = currentTime

In case when  preferXxInterface   = True AND (currentTime - preferX2StartTime >= t3)

 Set preferXxInterface = False

Note: The unit for currentTime, preferX2StartTime and rdPreferX2UPeriod shall be in ms.

t1 = inactivityThresholdForPrioritizeX2.

t2 = inactivityThresholdForRestartPrioritizeX2

t3 = prioritizeX2Period

inactivityThresholdForPrioritizeX2, inactivityThresholdForRestartPrioritizeX2 and prioritizeX2Period are NIDD parameters specific for EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent parameters are inactivityThresholdForPrioritizeXxNrDc, inactivityThresholdForRestartPrioritizeXxNrDc and prioritizeXxPeriodNrDc. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more details on NIDD parameters and these parameters are received in Bearer Setup.

Rationale:

1) During the TCP slow start phase, having high BLER (causing high delay) can cause TCP to rampup very slowly and cause low TP. During this phase, it is important to send data over the link with better radio condition. Hence In case of mmW during high BLER, it is better to use LTE leg for TCP slow start. However, since at PDCP we are not aware lower layer configuration and BLER condition, currently PDCP always prefer’s to use X2-U during TCP slow start phase.

2) PDCP does not know if the data stream is TCP or UDP except for ICMP packets and hence the above solution is applied to all traffic excluding ICMP.

3) PDCP does not know when exactly the TCP slow start occurs, hence the solution is applied at Bearer Setup and when data start to flow after some inactivity.

NOTE:

1) PDCP buffer is considered empty when there are no new PDCP SDUs in the buffer (i.e. excluding PDCP PDUs waiting for retransmission).

2) The DL Preferred path functionality is configured via NIDD parameter dlPreferredPath for EN DC and dlPreferredPathNrDc for NR DC bearers. Refer to NIDD parameter details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3) actPrioritizeX2AfterInactivity is a NIDD parameter to be used specific for EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent NIDD parameter is actPrioritizeXxAfterInactivityNrDc. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008490-D]

3) For NR DC bearers, the requirements mentioned above related to Secondary link are applicable to MCG Xn-U. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NR DC Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

---

### 4.1.1.5 R&amp;D Parameters

#### 4.1.1.5.1 F1 interface only

##### 4.1.1.5.1.0-1 F1 interface only rdUlSplitAckWaitTimerDuration (ID: 11218336)

**4.1.1.5.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11218344`)

F1 interface only
Description: The parameters is the wait time for ACK of the split mode measured for the bearer after sending of RLC status to C-plane.

Value range: 5...2000

Default value: 800

Unit: ms

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5302\_replaced([11217774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxgeN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[PR666690] Title object and parameter name were changed from rdUlSplitWaitTimerDuration to rdUlSplitAckWaitTimerDuration. Requirement structure updated [End PR666690]

---
