## 4.1.2 3GPP Flow control

### 4.1.2.1 DDDS Polling

#### 4.1.2.1.0-1 DDDS Polling Perform DDDS polling for 3GPP flow control over F1-U interface (ID: 11218534)

**4.1.2.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11218556`)

DDDS Polling
- In case of BearerSetup OR when the DL data transfer is resumed after suspend due to mobility,

* Perform as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5385\_replaced([11218563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxlWsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* If the DDDS reduction is ON (actDddsReduction = TRUE) set the tdddsPoll timer as below:
* In case when the buffer (both PDCP SDU and PDCP PDU) was non-empty and has become empty now at PDCP, execute the steps defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5387\_replaced([11218583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxlWtfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* In case when buffer at PDCP was empty and has become non-empty now, execute the steps defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5389\_replaced([11218596](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxlWt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case PDCP and RLC entities of 5G-L2-HI are co-located, 5G-L2-HI shall not perform the DDDS polling.

timer tMaxPollingResp and DDDS poll bit setting is as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5391\_replaced([11218616](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxlWuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

dddsPeriod is parameter sent at Bearer Setup.

actDddsReduction is parameter sent at Bearer Setup.

[CB008717-DA]For NR DC bearers SCG F1-U link, dddsPeriodXx is to be used. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD parameters. [End CB008717-DA]

actDDDSPeriodOptimization is parameter sent in 5G-L2-HI CU Configuration Parameter Request

rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5641\_replaced([11220644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw87fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

rdMinDddsPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5377\_replaced([11218483](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-2 DDDS Polling DDDS polling at Bearer Setup/Mobility for F1-U interface (ID: 11218563)

**4.1.2.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11218575`)

DDDS Polling
5G-L2-HI start the periodic tdddsPoll timer for F1-U interface when one following condition is met

* actDDDSPeriodOptimization = False AND DL F1-U tunnel is available
* actDDDSPeriodOptimization = True AND DL F1-U tunnel is available AND PDCP SDU buffer is not empty.

The timer value for tdddsPoll timer is rdMinDddsPeriod

actDDDSPeriodOptimization is parameter sent in [Before CNI-88099-F] HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq [CNI-88099-F] 5G-L2-HI CU Configuration Parameter Request [End CNI-88099-F].

rdMinDddsPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5377\_replaced([11218483](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: In case of mobility, DL F1-U tunnel is target/new tunnel.

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-3 DDDS Polling Handling of DDDS reduction when PDCP buffer is empty (ID: 11218583)

**4.1.2.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11218590`)

DDDS Polling
In case when actDddsReduction is True AND PDCP SDU buffer and PDU buffer is empty

 5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic tdddsPoll  timer with timer value = rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod.

 F1-U flow control parameter are reinitialized as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) except for f1RlOutage, f1DataSendSuspended and f1DataSendPaused

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-4 DDDS Polling DDDS reduction when PDCP SDU buffer is not empty (ID: 11218596)

**4.1.2.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11218609`)

DDDS Polling
/\* Scenario : Data available at PDCP. DDDS reduction is on and flow control calibration is not ongoing.

Polling timer is set to min period. \*/

In case when the actDddsReduction is True

 IF tdddsPoll is set to rdMinDddsPeriod AND PDCP SDU buffer is not empty

If flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing is False,

 5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic tdddsPoll timer with timer value = dddsPeriod.

/\* Scenario: Transition from “rdMinDddsPeriod or dddsPeriod” TO “rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod”.

Conditions: DDDS reduction is on. Data available at PDCP. All the data sent on the F1-U is acked.

No new data is sent over the F1-U for the duration of the last silent period \*/

 IF tdddsPoll is Not set to rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod AND PDCP SDU Buffer is not empty

IF “all PDCP PDU(s) sent over the F1-U interface has been indicated as delivered via DDDS” AND

“Number of PDCP PDU sent over the F1-U interface during the last rdSilentPeriodThreshold(refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5666\_replaced([11220755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 0”,

 5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic tdddsPoll timer with timer value = rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod.

 F1-U flow control parameter are reinitialized as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) except for f1RlOutage, f1DataSendSuspended and f1DataSendPaused

/\* Scenario: Transition from “rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod” TO “rdMinDddsPeriod or dddsPeriod”.

Conditions: DDDS reduction is on. PDCP PDU is sent over F1-U and polling was set to max duration \*/

 IF tdddsPoll is set to rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod AND dataOnFlight > 0

 5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic tdddsPoll timer.

If flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing is True,

The timer value for tdddsPoll timer is rdMinDddsPeriod.

else

The timer value for tdddsPoll timer is dddsPeriod.

For CPU based DDDS polling, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5430\_replaced([11229191](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

dddsPeriod, actDddsReduction are parameters sent at Bearer Setup.

[CB008717-DA]For NR DC bearers SCG F1-U link, dddsPeriodXx is to be used. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters. [End CB008717-DA]

rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5641\_replaced([11220644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw87fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

rdMinDddsPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5377\_replaced([11218483](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-5 DDDS Polling DDDS polling timer handling (ID: 11218616)

**4.1.2.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11218624`)

DDDS Polling
After starting the tdddsPoll timer for the first time OR On expiry of the tdddsPoll timer

IF tMaxPollingResp timer is not running

-  IF within 1ms PDCP PDU is available for transmission and flow control allows,

 Send F1-U DL USER DATA with “Report Polling” set to 1

ELSE

 after 1ms if there is no PDCP PDU available for transmission over F1-U either due to empty buffer or flow control decision, send F1-U DL USER DATA with no payload and “Report Polling” set to 1

END

- Start tMaxPollingResp timer

END

tMaxPollingResp timer period = 2 \* transferDelayMax

transferDelayMax is parameter sent at Bearer Setup.

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-6 DDDS Polling DDDS polling response timer expiry (ID: 11218630)

**4.1.2.1.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11218635`)

DDDS Polling
On tMaxPollingResp expiry, 5G-L2-HI shall set

 flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = true.

 avgDeltaPduDelvDelay = 0.

 numOfDDDSWithDataFlow = 0.

 numOfDDDSWithDataStall = 0.

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-7 DDDS Polling Perform DDDS polling for 3GPP flow control over X2-U or Xn-U interface (ID: 11218642)

**4.1.2.1.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11218656`)

DDDS Polling
- In case of BearerSetup OR when the DL data transfer is resumed after suspend due to mobility,

* Perform as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5400\_replaced([11218665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxl9wfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* If the DDDS reduction is ON (actDddsReduction = TRUE)

set the xxDddsPollTimer timer as below:

* In case when the buffer (both PDCP SDU and PDCP PDU) is empty at PDCP execute the steps defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5403\_replaced([11218683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxl9xPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* In case when buffer at PDCP is non-empty, execute the steps defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5406\_replaced([11218696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxl9xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For CPU based DDDS polling, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5430\_replaced([11229191](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

actDddsReduction is parameter sent at Bearer Setup.

actDDDSPeriodOptimization is parameter sent in [Before CNI-88099-F] HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq [CNI-88099-F] 5G-L2-HI CU Configuration Parameter Request [End CNI-88099-F].

rdMinDddsPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5377\_replaced([11218483](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-8 DDDS Polling DDDS polling at Bearer Setup/Mobility for X2-U interface (ID: 11218665)

**4.1.2.1.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11218678`)

DDDS Polling
If actDDDSPeriodOptimization = True OR  delayDddsPolling = True

 Set dddsPollingOptimisation = True

Else

 Set dddsPollingOptimisation = False

delayDddsPolling is received from CPlane during Bearer Setup

5G-L2-HI start the periodic xxDddsPollTimer timer for X2-U interface when one following condition is met,

* dddsPollingOptimisation = False AND DL F1-U tunnel and UL/DL COUNT are available
* dddsPollingOptimisation = True AND DL F1-U tunnel and UL/DL COUNT are available AND PDCP SDU buffer is not empty

The timer value for xxDddsPollTimer timer is rdMinDddsPeriod.

actDDDSPeriodOptimization is parameter sent in [Before CNI-88099-F] HiCnfgCu\_ConfigParamReq [CNI-88099-F] 5G-L2-HI CU Configuration Parameter Request [End CNI-88099-F].

rdMinDddsPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5377\_replaced([11218483](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Rationale:

1. When SCG split bearer is setup without PDCP anchor change(Direct SCG setup),

a. At source, the X2-U GTP-U tunnel setup is completed on processing of SgNB Modification request.

b. At target, the X2-U GTP-U tunnel setup is completed on processing of SgNB Modification request acknowledge.

Alithough it is allowed by 3GPP to send GTP-U PDU toward target after 1.a, target might not be able to process the GTP-U PDU leading to GTP-U Error indication causing UE release.

To avoid this, source will start DDDS polling when after receiving first DL PDCP SDU which would be received only after the DRB has been setup on target.

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-9 DDDS Polling DDDS reduction over X2-U interface when PDCP SDU buffer is empty (ID: 11218683)

**4.1.2.1.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11218691`)

DDDS Polling
In case when actDddsReduction is True AND PDCP SDU and PDU buffer is empty

* 5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic tdddsPollX2  timer with timer value = rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod.
* X2-U flow control parameter are reinitialized as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) except for xxRlOutage, xxDataSendSuspended and xxDataSendPaused

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-10 DDDS Polling DDDS reduction over X2-U or Xn-U interface when PDCP SDU buffer is not empty (ID: 11218696)

**4.1.2.1.0-10.0-2**  (ID: `11218708`)

DDDS Polling
In case when actDddsReduction is True,

/\* Scenario: Transition from “rdMinDddsPeriod or dddsPeriodX2” TO “rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod”.

Conditions: DDDS reduction is on. Data available at PDCP. All the data sent on the X2-U is acked.

No new data is sent over the X2-U for the duration of the last silent period \*/

 If xxDddsPollTimer is not set to rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod AND PDCP SDU Buffer is not empty

If “all PDCP PDU(s) sent over the X2-U interface has been indicated as delivered via DDDS” AND

“Number of PDCP PDU sent over the X2-U inteface during the last rdSilentPeriodThreshold is 0”,

* 5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic xxDddsPollTimer timer with timer value = rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod.
* X2-U flow control parameter are reinitialized as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) except for xxRlOutage, xxDataSendSuspended and xxDataSendPaused.

/\* Scenario: Transition from “rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod” TO “rdMinDddsPeriod or dddsPeriod”.

Conditions: DDDS reduction is on. PDCP PDU is sent over X2-U and polling was set to max duration \*/

If xxDddsPollTimer is set to rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod AND dataOnFlightXx > 0

* 5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic xxDddsPollTimer timer.

If flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx is True,

* The timer value for xxDddsPollTimer timer is rdMinDddsPeriod.

else

* The timer value for xxDddsPollTimer timer is dddsPeriodX2.

/\* Scenario : Data available at PDCP. DDDS reduction is on and flow control calibration is not ongoing.

Polling timer is set to min period. \*/

 If xxDddsPollTimer is set to rdMinDddsPeriod AND PDCP SDU buffer is not empty

If flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx is False,

* 5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic xxDddsPollTimer timer with timer value for xxDddsPollTimer timer is dddsPeriod

actDddsReduction, dddsPeriodX2 are parameters sent at Bearer Setup.

[CB008717-DA]For SCG F1-U link, dddsPeriodXx parameter is used. Refer to NIDD and algorithm parameter details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CB008717-DA]

rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5641\_replaced([11220644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw87fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

rdSilentPeriodThreshold is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5666\_replaced([11220755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdMinDddsPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5377\_replaced([11218483](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-11 DDDS Polling Timer tdddsPoll  Event handling for X2-U or Xn-U interface (ID: 11218716)

**4.1.2.1.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11218721`)

DDDS Polling
After starting the xxDddsPollTimer timer for the first time OR On expiry of the xxDddsPollTimer timer, 5G-L2-HI shall

IF xxDddsMaxPollRespTimer timer is not running

- IF within 1ms PDCP PDU is available for transmission and flow control allows,

 Send X2-U DL USER DATA with “Report Polling” set to 1

ELSE

 after 1ms if there is no PDCP PDU available for transmission over X2-U either due to empty buffer or flow control decision, send X2-U DL USER DATA with no payload and “Report Polling” set to 1

END

- Start xxDddsMaxPollRespTimer timer

END

xxDddsMaxPollRespTimer timer period = 2 \* maxTransferDelayXx

maxTransferDelayXx is sent at Bearer Setup.

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-12 DDDS Polling Timer xxDddsMaxPollRespTimer expiry event handling (ID: 11218727)

**4.1.2.1.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11218735`)

DDDS Polling
On xxDddsMaxPollRespTimer expiry, 5G-L2-HI shall set:

* flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = true.
* avgDeltaPduDelvDelayXx = 0.
* numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx = 0.
* numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx = 0.

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-13 DDDS Polling Perform DDDS polling based on unacked PDCP PDU threshold (ID: 11218740)

**4.1.2.1.0-13.0-3**  (ID: `11218761`)

DDDS Polling
5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic xxDddsPollTimer timer with timer value = rdUnackedPdcpPduDddsPeriod on X2-U interface when the following condition are met

* actDDDSPeriodOptimization is True
* Number of PDCP PDU and SDU stored per Bearer Group >= rdPDCPBufferCongestionThreshold \* Max number of availbale PDCP PDU and SDU buffer per Bearer Group
* Number of Unacked PDCP PDU(s) > rdMinUnackedPdcpPduThreshold
* xxDddsPollTimer timer > rdUnackedPdcpPduDddsPeriod

5G-L2-HI shall restart the periodic tdddsPoll timer with timer value = current X2-U DDDS period on X2-U interface when the following condition are met

* actDDDSPeriodOptimization is True
* Number of Unacked PDCP PDU(s) for DRB < rdMinUnackedPdcpPduThreshold
* xxDddsPollTimer timer value = rdUnackedPdcpPduDddsPeriod

current X2-U DDDS period is the DDDS period for X2-U used before the xxDddsPollTimer timer was restarted with timer value = rdUnackedPdcpPduDddsPeriod.

Unacked PDCP PDU(s) are PDCP PDU(s) that is/are indicated as transmitted (via "Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" or "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") in DDDS but not delivered (via "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" or "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") in DDDS.

In case PDCP PDU corresponding to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number”

and/or "Successfully delivered retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number"

of current DDDS is not available in the buffer (i.e. PDU is already released),

perform the steps described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15100\_replaced([11218084](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and identify the Unacked PDCP PDU(s).

Number of Unacked PDCP PDU(s)  = Number of Unacked PDCP PDU(s) sent over F1-U interface + Number of Unacked PDCP PDU(s) sent over X2-U interface

dddsPeriod and dddsPeriodX2 are parameters sent at Bearer Setup.

[CB008717-DA]For NR DC bearers SCG F1-U link, dddsPeriodXx is to be used. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters. [End CB008717-DA]

actDDDSPeriodOptimization is parameter sent in 5G-L2-HI CU Configuration Parameter Request

rdPDCPBufferCongestionThreshold is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5688\_replaced([11220918](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdMinUnackedPdcpPduThreshold is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5689\_replaced([11220926](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdUnackedPdcpPduDddsPeriod is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5701\_replaced([11220994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxzZIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 4.1.2.1.0-14 DDDS Polling Handling of DDDS polling on DL data suspension during Mobility (ID: 11218768)

**4.1.2.1.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `11218774`)

DDDS Polling
5G-L2-HI shall,

* Stop tdddsPoll timer/ xxDddsPollTimer if already running.
* IF dlFlowControlAlgo is 3gppFlowControl,
* Send F1-U/X2-U DL USER DATA with no payload and “Report Polling” set to 1.

---

### 4.1.2.2 3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling

#### 4.1.2.2.0-1 3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling DL Gain Calculation (ID: 11218786)

**4.1.2.2.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `12343206`)

3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling
5G-L2-HI shall calculate:

 Desired buffer size

The average Desired Buffer Size over the Primary or Secondary link everytime DesBufferF1 or DesBufferXx are updated, respectively

avgDesBufferXx **= (1 – rdAvgDesBufferFilt) \* avgDesBufferXx** + rdAvgDesBufferFilt \* DesBufferXx;\*\*\*\*

avgDesBufferF1 = (1 – rdAvgDesBufferFilt) \* avgDesBufferF1 + rdAvgDesBufferFilt \* DesBufferF1;

where:

rdAvgDesBufferFilt is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5676\_replaced([11220798](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

DesBufferXx = DBSXx as indicated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5518\_replaced([11219421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

DesBufferF1 = DBS as indicated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5462\_replaced([11218999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 Downlink data split gain

5G-L2-HI shall estimate the data split gain as below only when all the below conditions are met

 dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UXxU. Refer Note 3.

 initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct is FALSE

 Atleast one DDDS with “Desired buffer size for the data bearer"> 0 is received on the Secondary link after the flow control parameters were initialised (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Atleast one DDDS with “Desired buffer size for the data bearer"> 0 is received on the Primary after the flow control parameters were initialised (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: dlDataSplitMode is a NIDD parameter. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Refer Note 3.

In case the Preferred Path is set to Secondary link (*dlPreferredPath = "*Secondary (X2-U, SCG F1-U)" - see note 4), some variables need to be swapped so let's introduce generic names like:\*\*

IF Preferred = Primary

*avgDesBufferPref = avgDesBufferF1*

*dataSendPausedPref = f1DataSendPaused*

*estTputPref = estTput*

ELSE

*avgDesBufferPref = avgDesBufferXx*

*dataSendPausedPref = xxDataSendPaused*

*estTputPref = estTputXx*

END

If *f1DataSendSuspended = TRUE OR xxDataSendSuspended = TRUE OR f1RlOutage = TRUE OR xxRlOutage = TRUE,*

set dlDataSplitAllowed = False,

skip the rest of the below procedure for Downlink data split gain, “Buffer delay threshold”, “data split decision”.

IF (avgDesBufferPref > 0)

avgBufferVolGain = ((avgDesBufferXx + avgDesBufferF1)/ avgDesBufferPref) \* 100 – 100;

ELSE

avgBufferVolGain = 100;

END

 Buffer delay threshold

Set bufferDelayThresholdExceeded = False

In case when (Amount of unsent data / *estTputPref*) >= dlDataSplitBufferBuildUpThreshold),\*\*

**OR (IF** enableEnhancedDlDataSplit**is TRUE** AND "data on flight" of the non-preferred path for DL data sending is > 0)(refer **Rationale)*****\****\*

set bufferDelayThresholdExceeded = True

Rationale:

* When the DL data received at PDCP is bursty (typically for TCP flows and is RTT sensitive) - the PDCP buffer can become empty briefly and this could lead to disabling of DL data split. To avoid this impact of burst traffic on DL data split decision, the buffer delay threshold state is retained until the data on flight on the non-preferred path is > 0.
* This solution is useful in case the TCP traffic is RTT bound (in case of lower sessions), and the preferred path is lower bandwidth compared to the non-Preferred path. Lower Bandwidth link is configured as preferred path in case the operator wants to route the low throughput sessions and use data split for high throughput sessions.

 Data split decision

IF (((avgBufferVolGain >= dlDataSplitGainThreshold) AND (bufferDelayThresholdExceeded = True) *OR (dataSendPausedPref* *= True))*\*\*

numOfConsecutiveGainPeriod++

IF (numOfConsecutiveGainPeriod > dlNumOfCongOrGainDdds)

Set dlDataSplitAllowed = True;

END

* dlDataSplitAllowed once set to True as per above, shall be maintained during flow control calibration ongoing (for either or both of the links) across DDDS periods till both the links are out of flow control calibration.

IF ((flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = False) AND (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = False))

Estimate the throughput gain:

avgEstTputGain = ((estTputXx + estTput)/ estTputPref) \* 100 - 100;

IF ((avgEstTputGain < dlDataSplitGainThreshold) AND (dataSendPausedPref = False))

Set dlDataSplitAllowed = False;

END

END

ELSE

numOfConsecutiveGainPeriod = 0;

Set dlDataSplitAllowed = False;

END

where:

estTputXx and estTput are derived as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5518\_replaced([11219421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5462\_replaced([11218999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

dlNumOfCongOrGainDdds is NRDRB.nsaDrbParam.dlNumOfCongOrGainDdds. Refer Note 3.

"Amount of unsent data" accounts for the new PDCP SDU(s)/PDU(s) which are stored in

Radio bearer buffer and not scheduled over Primary **or secondary link (excluding the PDCP PDUs waiting for retransmission).**

**Note:**

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

2) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

3)   dlDataSplitMode, dlDataSplitBufferBuildUpThreshold, dlDataSplitGainThreshold, dlNumOfCongOrGainDdds, initDLDataTrafficRouting **are NIDD parameters used specific for EN DC bearers. dlDataSplitModeNrDc, dlDataSplitBufferThresholdNrDc, dlDataSplitGainThresholdNrDc, dlNumOfCongOrGainDddsNrDc, initialDLTrafficRoutingNrDc are NR DC equivalent NIDD parameters.  Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

4)   The DL Preferred path functionality is configured via NIDD parameter dlPreferredPath for EN DC and dlPreferredPathNrDc for NR DC bearers. Refer to NIDD parameter details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[CNI-144227-A]**

5)  NRBTS.NRDRB.nrDcDrbParam.actEnhancedDlDataSplitNrDc is the NR-DC specific activation parameter to be used for enabling enhanced downlink data split for NR-DC bearers.

**[End CNI-144227-A]**

---

#### 4.1.2.2.0-2 3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling Updating of reported throughput for 3GPP flow control. (ID: 11218832)

**4.1.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11218838`)

3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling
IF dlFlowControlAlgo is set to 3gppFlowControl

5G-L2-HI shall derive the reported throughput over X2-U  from the “Desired Data Rate” on receipt of DDDS message over X2-U interface.

* IF Data Rate Indication = 1 in the X2-U DDDS, Set avgRepTputX2 = Desired Data Rate
* IF Data Rate Indication = 0 in the X2-U DDDS, Set avgRepTputX2 = minThFlowCtrlX2

5G-L2-HI shall derive the reported throughput over F1-U from the “Desired Data Rate” on receipt of DDDS message over F1-U interface.

* IF Data Rate Indication = 1 in the F1-U DDDS, Set avgRepTput = Desired Data Rate
* IF Data Rate Indication = 0 in the F1-U DDDS, Set avgRepTput = minThFlowCtrl

END

---

#### 4.1.2.2.0-3 3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling Link availability based on throughput (ID: 11218845)

**4.1.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11218851`)

3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling
5G-L2-HI shall set isXxTputAvailable to False, when below conditions are met

* avgRepTputXx < minThFlowCtrlX2 AND avgRepTput > minThFlowCtrl AND avgRepTput >= rdMinTpGainLinkAvailableThreshold \* avgRepTputXx OR [CB008717-B]Refer Note 4[End CB008717-B]
* estTput > rdAvgEstTpGainLinkAvailableThreshold \* estTputXx

5G-L2-HI shall set f1Available to False, when below conditions are met

* avgRepTput < minThFlowCtrl AND avgRepTputXx minThFlowCtrlX2 AND avgRepTputXx >= rdMinTpGainLinkAvailableThreshold \* avgRepTput OR [CB008717-B] Refer Note 4 [End CB008717-B]
* estTputXx > rdAvgEstTpGainLinkAvailableThreshold \* estTput

rdAvgEstTpGainLinkAvailableThreshold is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5684\_replaced([11220872](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdMinTpGainLinkAvailableThreshold is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5685\_replaced([11220886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

estTput is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5462\_replaced([11218999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

estTputXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5518\_replaced([11219421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

avgRepTputXx, avgRepTput are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5425\_replaced([11218832](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxmk2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rationale:

[Before CB008717-B]

Current CU estimate TP does not to go below min TP to avoid completely blocking the data sending. However, in case of Desired Data Rate reported by F1-U is below the min Throughput, but Desired Data Rate reported by X2-U is above the min Throughput, we should avoid sending data over F1-U to avoid PDCP reordering timeout at UE. Same is applicable vice versa case.

When the ratio of average estimated TP between F1-U and X2-U is quite large, then sending data over both the F1-U and X2-U can cause PDCP reordering timeout at UE. Hence it is better to avoid using the link with lowest average estimated TP. [End CB008717-B]

[CB008717-B]

Current CU estimate TP does not to go below min TP to avoid completely blocking the data sending. However, in case of Desired Data Rate reported by MCG F1-U is below the min Throughput, but Desired Data Rate reported by secondary link is above the min Throughput, we should avoid sending data over MCG F1-U to avoid PDCP reordering timeout at UE. Same is applicable vice versa case.

When the ratio of average estimated TP between MCG F1-U and secondary link is quite large, then sending data over both the MCG F1-U and secondary link can cause PDCP reordering timeout at UE. Hence it is better to avoid using the link with lowest average estimated TP.[End CB008717-B]

Note:

1) minThFlowCtrlX2 is a NIDD parameter. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2)  This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

[CB008717-B]

3)  The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

4) minThFlowCtrlX2 is used for secondary F1-U in NR-DC. The minThFlowCtrlX2 NIDD parameter will be updated in a future subfeature.

[End CB008717-B]

---

#### 4.1.2.2.0-4 3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling AMBR based Link availability (ID: 11218859)

**4.1.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11218865`)

3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling
If DL DRB AMBR limit feature is enabled (actDlAmbr = SA),

 5G-L2-HI shall stop sending DL data for the non-GBR DRB, when any of the below conditions are met:

 If the dlDrbAvgOutBitRate is greater than the dlDrbDynAmbr for the non-GBR DRB.

 If the sum of dlDrbAvgOutBitRate for all the non-GBR DRBs of the UE (to which the current DRB is mapped to) is greater than “DL UE AMBR limit”.

If the DL data sending is stopped (Note 1) due to DL AMBR limitation,

 5G-L2-HI shall resume the DL data sending for the non-GBR DRB, when all the below conditions are met:

 If the dlDrbAvgOutBitRate is less than the dlDrbDynAmbr for the non-GBR DRB.

 If the sum of dlDrbAvgOutBitRate for all the non-GBR DRBs of the UE (to which the current DRB is mapped to is less than “DL UE AMBR limit”.

- dlDrbAvgOutBitRate, dlDrbDynAmbr are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19313\_replaced([11227904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyfVpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- NRBTS/actDlAmbr is a NIDD parameter received from C-Plane.

Note:

1. If the DL data for the non-GBR DRB is stopped due to any other cause (other than AMBR limit), the DL Data resumption is based on the respective cause. AMBR based DL data resumption is only applicable when the DL data path(s) for the non-GBR DRB are available for DL data sending.

2. The check for suspending/resuming the DL data for the non-GBR DRB shall be done every time the dlDrbAvgOutBitRate is updated for the non-GBR bearer.

---

#### 4.1.2.2.0-5 3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling R&amp;D Parameters (ID: 11218873)

**4.1.2.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11218880`)

3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling
rdEnableEnhancedDlSplit

---

**4.1.2.2.0-5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11218891`)

3GPP flow control specific DDDS handling
[Before CNI-123430]

Description: The parameter enables the flow control algorithm to sustain downlink split enable decision even when the amount of unsent data is zero if there is data on flight on the non-preferred path.

Note: This solution is useful in case the TCP traffic is RTT bound (in case of lower sessions), and the preferred path is lower bandwidth compared to the non-Preferred path. Lower Bandwidth link is configured as preferred path in case the operator wants to route the low throughput sessions and use data split for high throughput sessions.

Value range: true or false

Default value: false

Unit: boolean

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: N/A

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27533\_replaced([11218349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxjhlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5422\_replaced([11218786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxmk1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CNI-123430]

### 4.1.2.3 Flow Control Parameters and Initialization

#### 4.1.2.3.0-1 Flow Control Parameters and Initialization Maintain 3GPP flow control variable per bearer (ID: 11218906)

**4.1.2.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11218910`)

Flow Control Parameters and Initialization
5G-L2-HI shall maintain flow control parameters for F1 and X2 interfaces as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5448\_replaced([11218917](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and initialize the parameters as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5451\_replaced([11218932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-HI shall maintain common flow control parameters as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5454\_replaced([11218954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and initialize the parameters as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5456\_replaced([11218965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 4.1.2.3.0-2 Flow Control Parameters and Initialization 3GPP flow control variables per bearer for F1-U interface or  X2-U or Xn-U interface. (ID: 11218917)

**4.1.2.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11218924`)

Flow Control Parameters and Initialization
5G-L2-HI shall maintain the following 3GPP flow control variables per bearer for F1-U interface or  [Before CB008717-B]X2-U interface[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link [End CB008717-B] .

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Parameter Name | Description |
| Time instant of DDDS reception(timeInstDDDSRcv) over F1-U  Time instant of DDDS reception (timeInstDDDSRcvXx over [Before CB008717-B]X2-U [End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link [End CB008717-B] | The time when the last F1-U or  [Before CB008717-B]X2-U[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link [End CB008717-B] Downlink Data Delivery Status Indication message was received. The timestamp is maintained with 1ms of granularity. |
| Time instant of valid DDDS reception (timeInstLastValidDDDSRcv) over F1-U. Time instant of valid DDDS reception (timeInstLastValidDDDSRcvXx) over [Before CB008717-B]X2-U [End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link [End CB008717-B] | The time when the last valid F1-U or  [Before CB008717-B]X2-U[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link[End CB008717-B] Downlink Data Delivery Status Indication message was received. “Valid” means message which was used for updating flow control variables (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5462\_replaced([11218999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5518\_replaced([11219421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details). The timestamp is maintained with 1ms of granularity. |
| Data on flight(dataOnFlight) over F1-U Data on flight(dataOnFlightXx) over [Before CB008717-B]X2-U [End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link [End CB008717-B] | The number of bytes for the given bearer sent to the gNB-DU or eNB and not yet forwarded to the MAC. |
| Average F1-U PDU Delivery Delay (avgPduDelvDelay) [Before CB008717-B] Average X2-U PDU Delivery Delay (avgPduDelvDelayXx)  [End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B] Average Secondary link PDU Delivery Delay (avgPduDelvDelayXx)  [End CB008717-B] | The Average PDU Delivery Delay calculated for the PDU sent over F1-U or  [Before CB008717-B]X2-U[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link[End CB008717-B] interface |
| Average estimated throughput(avgEstTput) Average estimated throughput (avgEstTputXx) | The average estimated throughput as calculated based on “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” |
| Current estimated throughput(estTput) Current estimated throughput (estTputXx) | The current estimated throughput used for PDCP PDU estimated latency calculation |
| Delta Data filling for F1-U (avgDeltaDataFilling) [Before CB008717-B] Delta Data filling for X2-U (avgDeltaDataFillingXx) [End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B] Delta Data filling for Secondary link (avgDeltaDataFillingXx) [End CB008717-B] | This provides the average of the difference between the Desired Buffer requested by DU/eNB and data in flight toward DU/eNB |
| PDU delivery delay limit over F1-U(pduDelvDelayLimit) [Before CB008717-B]  PDU delivery delay limit over X2-U (pduDelvDelayLimitXx)  [End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]  PDU delivery delay limit over Secondary link (pduDelvDelayLimitXx)  [End CB008717-B] | This define the limit of the estimated PDCP PDU Delivery Delay beyond which PDCP PDU are not sent. |
| Data sending over F1-U Paused (f1DataSendPaused) [Before CB008717-B] Data sending over X2-U Paused (xxDataSendPaused) [End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B] Data sending over Secondary link Paused (xxDataSendPaused) [End CB008717-B] | Indicates that data sending over F1-U or  [Before CB008717-B]X2-U[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link[End CB008717-B]  is paused. |
| Flow control calibration Ongoing over F1-U (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing) [Before CB008717-B] Flow control calibration Ongoing over X2-U (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx) [End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B] Flow control calibration Ongoing over Secondary link (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx) [End CB008717-B] | This signals that calibration is ongoing for Flow control parameters for F1 PDU delivery delay or  [Before CB008717-B]X2-U[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link [End CB008717-B] PDU delivery and estimated throughput. |
| Number of silent period(numOfSilentPeriod) Number of silent period (numOfSilentPeriodXx) | This define the number of period that no data was sent to gNB-DU or eNB. |
| f1DataSendSuspended xxDataSendSuspended | Indicates that data sending over F1-U or  [Before CB008717-B]X2-U[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link [End CB008717-B] interface is suspended. |
| avgDesBufferF1 avgDesBufferXx | Defines the average desired buffer size calculated and used for gain calculation |
| f1RlOutage xxRlOutage | Indicate status of Radio link over F1-U and  [Before CB008717-B]X2-U[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link [End CB008717-B] |
| numOfDDDSWithDataStall, numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx | Indicate the number of DDDS for which there was no data outflow indicated by DU/eNB but there is still data available on DU/eNB. |
| numOfDDDSWithDataFlow, numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx | Indicate the number of DDDS for which there was data outflow indicated by DU/eNB after Data stall was detected. Data Stall detection is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5462\_replaced([11218999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_5518\_replaced([11219421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection, numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetectionXx | Indicates the number of DDDS used to detect the link failure |
| linkReintPerformed, linkReintPerformedXx | Indicates that F1-U parameter were re-initialised due to link failure. Indicates that  [Before CB008717-B]X2-U[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link[End CB008717-B] parameter were re-initialised due to link failure |
| lastSnSentBeforeLinkReinit, lastSnSentBeforeLinkReinitXx | [Before 5GC001354-A] Indicates the last SN sent over F1-U after flow control was re initialised due to link failure. Indicates the last SN sent over X2-U after flow control was re initialised due to link failure. [End 5GC001354-A]   [5GC001354-A] Indicates the highest SN of the PDCP PDU sent over F1-U (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after flow control was re initialised due to link failure. Indicates the highest SN of the PDCP PDU sent over [Before CB008717-B]X2-U[End CB008717-B] [CB008717-B]Secondary Link [End CB008717-B] (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) after flow control was re initialised due to link failure. [End 5GC001354-A] |
| highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev, highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx | [Before 5GC001354-A] Indicates the next PDCP SN sent on the interface after the previous highest Transmitted PDCP SN reported in DDDS. [End 5GC001354-A]   [5GC001354-A] Indicates the next PDCP SN (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) sent on the interface after the previous highest Transmitted PDCP SN reported in DDDS. [End 5GC001354-A] |
| LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSN, LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSNXx | Indicates the highest Transmitted PDCP SN reported in latest DDDS. |
| LatestHighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSN, LatesthighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSNXx | Indicates the highest successfully delivered PDCP SN reported in latest DDDS. |
| timeSinceLastBufferActivity/ timeSinceLastBufferActivityXx | Indicate the amount of time after the last DDDS with Data In Flight and Data Out to MAC was 0 |
| [5GC001354-A] retransmittedNrUSNPrev, retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx [End 5GC001354-A] | [5GC001354-A] Indicates the NR-U SN of the next PDCP PDU retransmitted (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over the interface after the previous NR-U SN mapped to "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" reported in DDDS. [End 5GC001354-A] |

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

[CB008717-B]

2)   The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

3)   retransmittedNrUSNPrev, retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx parameters are not applicable for NR DC Split bearer. Interworking with CB001354 will be introduced in a later sub-feature of CB008717.

[End CB008717-B]

#### 4.1.2.3.0-3 Flow Control Parameters and Initialization Flow control interface-specific parameters initialization. (ID: 11218932)

**4.1.2.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11218946`)

Flow Control Parameters and Initialization
5G-L2-HI shall initialize the flow control parameters as below:

· f1DataSendPaused = False and xxDataSendPaused = False

· timeInstDDDSRcv = current time and timeInstDDDSRcvXx = current time.

· timeInstLastValidDDDSRcv = current time - dddsPeriod and timeInstLastValidDDDSRcvXx = current time - dddsPeriod.

Note: Parameter is initialized to a value from the past to make sure that first DDDS is handled correctly (first DDDS would be ignored if received within 2ms after Bearer Setup).

For non-GBR DRB,

· flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = True and flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = True.

· Set avgEstTput = 0 and Set avgEstTputXx =0

For GBR DRB

· flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = False and flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = False

· Set avgEstTput = DL MFBR and Set avgEstTputXx =0

DL MFBR is provided by CPlane during the DRB setup

· numOfSilentPeriod = 0 and numOfSilentPeriodXx = 0.

· Set dataOnFlight = 0 and dataOnFlightXx = 0;

· Set avgPduDelvDelay = 0 and avgPduDelvDelayXx =0;

· Set estTput = minThFlowCtrl and estTputXx = minThFlowCtrlX2;

· Set pduDelvDelayLimit = maxTransferDelay \* 2

· Set pduDelvDelayLimitXx = maxTransferDelayX2 \* 2;

· Set avgEstTput = 0 and Set avgEstTputXx =0

· Set avgDesBufferXx  =0 and avgDesBufferF1 = 0

· Set f1DataSendSuspended = True.

Note: During bearer setup 5G-L2-HI shall not receive the DL F1-U TEID and hence we need to suspend the data transfer over F1-U.

· Set xxDataSendSuspended = False.

· Set f1RlOutage = FALSE, xxRlOutage = FALSE

· numOfDDDSWithDataStall = 0, numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx = 0

· numOfDDDSWithDataFlow = 0, numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx = 0

· numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection = 0, numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetectionXx = 0

· linkReintPerformed = False , linkReintPerformedXx = False

· lastSnSentBeforeLinkReinit = 0, lastSnSentBeforeLinkReinitXx = 0

· highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev = INVALID SN,

· highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx = INVALID SN,

· In case when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev is INVALID\_SN, after sending a PDCP PDU (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on the interface, set highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev to the PDCP SN of the PDU.

· In case when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx is INVALID\_SN, after sending a PDCP PDU (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on the interface, set highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx to the PDCP SN of the PDU.

· Set LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSN = INVALID SN

· Set LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSNXx = INVALID SN

· Set LatestHighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSN = INVALID SN

· Set LatesthighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSNXx = INVALID SN

· timeSinceLastBufferActivity = 0

· timeSinceLastBufferActivityXx = 0

· retransmittedNrUSNPrev = INVALID SN

· retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx = INVALID SN

· In case when retransmittedNrUSNPrev is INVALID\_SN, after a PDCP PDU (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is sent on the interface, set retransmittedNrUSNPrev to the NR-U SN mapped to the PDCP PDU.

· In case when retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx is INVALID\_SN, after a PDCP PDU (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is sent on the interface, set retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx to the NR-U SN mapped to the PDCP PDU.

Note:

1) maxTransferDelayX2 and minThFlowCtrlX2 are NIDD parameter. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

3)  The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[Before CB008717-DA]

4)   maxTransferDelayX2 and minThFlowCtrlX2 NIDD parameters are used for NRDC also. The NIDD parameters will be updated in a future subfeature.

[CB008717-DA]

4)   For NR DC bearers, refer to maxTransferDelayXx, minThFlowCtrlXx and dddsPeriodXx. Refer to the NIDD and algorithm parameters at 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB008717-DA]

---

#### 4.1.2.3.0-4 Flow Control Parameters and Initialization 3GPP flow control common variables per bearer (ID: 11218954)

**4.1.2.3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11218959`)

Flow Control Parameters and Initialization
5G-L2-HI shall maintain the following common 3GPP flow control variables per bearer.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Parameter Name | Description |
| initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct | Indicates that initial phase of traffic routing is ongoing. |
| avgBufferVolGain | Average buffer volume gain. |
| numOfConsecutiveGainPeriod | Incremented during data split gain calculation. Indicates how many times gain is continuously above threshold, which allows for splitting DL traffic between F1-U and X2-U. |

---

#### 4.1.2.3.0-5 Flow Control Parameters and Initialization 3GPP flow control common parameters initialization (ID: 11218965)

**4.1.2.3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11218985`)

Flow Control Parameters and Initialization
5G-L2-HI shall initialize the flow control parameters as below:

· Set avgBufferVolGain = 0;

 Set numOfConsecutiveGainPeriod =0

[Before CNI-97376]

 Set initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = True;

 In case when bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer and dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1U , set initDLDataTrafficRouting = initDLoverF1U

 In case when bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer and dlDataSplitMode = dlOverX2U , set initDLDataTrafficRouting = initDLoverX2U

 In case when case bearerType = SA bearer, set initDLDataTrafficRouting = initDLoverF1U.

[CNI-97376]

 Set initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = False;

 In case when bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer and dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U and and initialDlTrafficRouting is not initDlDynamic, set initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = True

 In case when bearerType = SA (NRDC) split bearer and dlDataSplitModeNrDc = dlOverF1UXxU and and initialDlTrafficRoutingNrDc is not initDlDynamic, set initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = True

 Set firstDDDSreceivedOnPrimary = False;

 Set firstDDDSreceivedOnSecondary = False;

[End CNI-97376]

Note:

1. The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

2.  dlDataSplitMode and initDLDataTrafficRouting Act are algorithm parameters specific for EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent parameters are dlDataSplitModeNrDc and initDLDataTrafficRoutingActNrDc. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

### 4.1.2.4 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures

#### 4.1.2.4.0-1 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Update the 3GPP F1-U flow control parameters (ID: 11218999)

**4.1.2.4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13338348`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
gNB-CU-UP upon receiving the F1-U DDDS message from gNB-DU shall execute the below steps per bearer accordingly and update the corresponding bearer parameters defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

* Check and update the DBS as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5464\_replaced([11219024](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Update DBS based congestion as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5466\_replaced([11219035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before CB015946-A]

* If DDDS is too closely spaced as per in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5470\_replaced([11219061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then skip the below steps, ignore the DDDS and end the procedure.

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE: The closely spaced DDDS handling shall be guarded with a temporary activation flag actFCCloselySpacedDdds, this is mapped to NRBTS.actInternalImprovements1 (bit 6). The closely spaced DDDS shall be supported when the activation flag is true, and the legacy behaviour of discarding closely spaced DDDS shall be supported if the activation flag is false. The default value of the activation flag will be true. The temporary activation flag is reserved only for 26R3 release and shall be removed in subsequent releases (27R1 onwards).

[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

     Determine the interface availability as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5468\_replaced([11219049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

f conditions for uni-directional link re-initialization are satisfied as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5472\_replaced([11219083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxoaAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 Check and re-initialize the F1--U link as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5474\_replaced([11219095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxoaA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Skip the below steps and end the procedure.

* Update the uni-directional link re-initialization state as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5476\_replaced([11219114](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxoaBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Check if 5G-L2-HI can end initial data routing as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5478\_replaced([11219127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxoaCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Compute dataOnFlight and dataOutFlowToMac as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5480\_replaced([11219139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxoaCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Update the uni-directional link failure detection as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5482\_replaced([11219196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpBFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 If F1-U link is detected as failed and re-initialised as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5484\_replaced([11219216](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpBF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), Skip the below steps and end the procedure.

     Set the time instant of last valid DDDs reception and Calculate Estimated throughput over F1-U as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5486\_replaced([11219236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpBGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

      In case DU is congested as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5510\_replaced([11219380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) then skip the below steps and end the procedure.

* In case F1-U link is suspended or in Outage as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5512\_replaced([11219390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), skip the below steps and end the procedure.

     Compute the PDU delivery delay over F1-U as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5497\_replaced([11219322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpoJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

     Update the PDU delivery delay limit over F1-U as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5508\_replaced([11219357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpoLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

     Update VoNR DL Mute flag information as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29647\_replaced([11219404](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rationale for flow control calibration:

1)   At Bearer Setup, the estimated throughput will take some time before it reaches a stable value as it is based on the data outflow. During this time, the estimated throughput is set minThFlowControl to make sure gNB-CU is sending enough data to DU to maintain good outflow. Also, for the average estimated throughput is calculated so that it allows faster ramp-up.

2)   In case when no data is being sent, the estimated throughput starts to reduce as the outflow reduces. In such case, gNB-CU do not allow the estimated throughput to reduce very low value and freezes the estimated throughput. This allows then when gNB-CU get some data, the flow control algorithm allow to send data to gNB-DU.

3)   If the no data transmission is beyond a certain threshold, the value of average estimated throughput becomes quite old and hence in such case when gNB-CU receive data, it starts in the same way as Bearer Setup.

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-2 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Updating of DBS based on the transmitted buffer size (ID: 11219024)

**4.1.2.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11219029`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case when Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

Set LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSN= “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” IE received in current DDDS message.

In case when Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

Set LatestHighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSN = "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" IE received in current DDDS message.

In case when rdCuFlowControlNewDBSEnabled is TRUE, perform the following:

 Set TxPduBufferSize = 0.

 In case when LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSN != INVALID SN AND LatestHighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSN != INVALID SN,

-    Set TxPduBufferSize = Sum of PDU sizes of all PDUs with (PDCP sequence number >

LatestHighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSN and PDCP sequence number <= LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSN) +

[5GC001354-A-UPD005] Sum of PDU sizes of all the retransmitted PDCP PDUs

with NR-U "Retransmission flag" set to '1' (i.e."retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx"

as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) that are indicated as submitted to MAC

via "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number".

[End 5GC001354-A-UPD005]

* In case LatestHighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSN = INVALID SN AND LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSN != INVALID SN,

-    Set TxPduBufferSize = Sum of PDU sizes of all PDUs with PDCP sequence number <=

LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSN +

[5GC001354-A-UPD005] Sum of PDU sizes of all the retransmitted PDCP PDUs

with NR-U "Retransmission flag" set to '1' (i.e."retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx"

as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) that are indicated as submitted to MAC

via "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number".

[End 5GC001354-A-UPD005]

[5GC001354-A-UPD006]

* In case PDCP PDU corresponding to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number”

of current DDDS is not available in the buffer (i.e. PDU is already released),

perform the steps described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15100\_replaced([11218084](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and calculate TxPduBufferSize.

[End 5GC001354-A-UPD006]

     In case when (DBS != 0),

-      Set DBS = max(0, (DBS – TxPduBufferSize))

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-3 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures DBS based congestion handling. (ID: 11219035)

**4.1.2.4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11219042`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
Check if the interface must be paused based on DBS:

In case when DBS = 0,

Set f1DataSendPaused = true

Set initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = False

In case when DBS > 0

Set f1DataSendPaused = false

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-4 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Update the interface availability (ID: 11219049)

**4.1.2.4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11219057`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
Set f1Available = True

Determine the interface availability

IF (f1DataSendSuspended = TRUE) OR

(f1lDataSendPaused = TRUE) OR

(f1RlOutage = TRUE),

set f1Available = FALSE.

END

#### 4.1.2.4.0-5 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Handling of too closely spaced DDDS (ID: 11219061)

**4.1.2.4.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13338351`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
[Before CB015946-A]

Update the timeInstDDDSRcv – set it to the current time.

deltaTimeInstDDDS = timeInstDDDSRcv – timeInstLastValidDDDSRcv

 DDDS is considered to be closely spaced if the condition deltaTimeInstDDDS < 2ms is satisfied.

*Rationale: If the DDDS are closely spaced it could cause jitter as the PDUs sent out could be minimal and distorts the delay/throughput calculations.*

**Note:**

1) If an empty PDCP buffer is detected, the timeInstLastValidDDDSrcv parameter will be adjusted according to the 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32055\_replaced([11220286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvHy_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE:

1) The closely spaced DDDS handling shall be guarded with a temporary activation flag actFCCloselySpacedDdds, this is mapped to NRBTS.actInternalImprovements1 (bit 6). The closely spaced DDDS shall be supported when the activation flag is true, and the legacy behaviour of discarding closely spaced DDDS shall be supported if the activation flag is false. The default value of the activation flag will be true. The temporary activation flag is reserved only for 26R3 release and shall be removed in subsequent releases (27R1 onwards).

[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-6 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Conditions for unidirectional link re-initialization detection (ID: 11219083)

**4.1.2.4.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13338386`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case when Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number is not sent in the current DDDS message, 5G-L2-HI shall assume that Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number of current DDDS message is same as Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number in the previous DDDS message.

In case when linkReintPerformed = True AND (lastSnSentBeforeLinkReinit >= Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number of current DDDS message),

[Before CB015946-A]

IF f1Available = True

numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection = numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection + 1

ELSE

numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection = 0

END

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A]

IF f1Available = True

timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection = timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection + [Before CB015946-A-UPD001]dddsPeriod[CB015946-A-UPD001]deltaTimeInstDDDS[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

ELSE

timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection = 0

END

[Before CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE: dddsPeriod referred to here is the current used DDDS period value and not the configured value from cplane.[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

[CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE: deltaTimeInstDDDS refers to the instantaneous time difference between the reception time of the current DDDS versus the previously received DDDS on the same link.[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

[End CB015946-A]

Rationale: IF the link (F1-U) from CU-UP and DU is broken, then the PDCP PDUs sent from CU-UP would be lost. This information can be derived from DDDS reports sent from DU by monitoring Highest transmitted NR PDCP SN. IF the SN does not change during the monitoring period then the link is declared failed uni-directionally between CU-UP and DU.

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-7 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Conditions for execution of unidirectional link re-initialization (ID: 11219095)

**4.1.2.4.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `13338390`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
[Before CB015946-A]

IF numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection > numLinkFailureDlDetectPeriod

Trigger link re-initialization as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5341\_replaced([11218220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Set numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection = 0

END

numLinkFailureDlDetectPeriod is derived as below,

numLinkFailureDlDetectPeriod = roundup(rdLinkFailuretimerPeriod/*dddsPeriod)*

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A]

IF timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection > rdLinkFailureTimerPeriod

Trigger link re-initialization as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5341\_replaced([11218220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Set timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection = 0

END

[End CB015946-A]

rdLinkFailureTimerPeriod is a R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5375\_replaced([11218464](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For NR DC bearers SCG F1-U link, dddsPeriodXx is to be used. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters.

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-8 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Conditions for reseting the unidirectional link re-initialization (ID: 11219114)

**4.1.2.4.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `13338391`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case when linkReintPerformed = True AND (lastSnSentBeforeLinkReinit < Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number of current DDDS message),

[Before CB015946-A]

* numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection = 0

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A]

* timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection = 0

[End CB015946-A]

* linkReintPerformed = False
* Start the delay threshold monitoring procedure for the new PDCP PDUs sent after link re-initialization as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7580\_replaced([11220420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
