#### 4.1.2.4.0-9 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Conditions for ending the initial data routing and execution of flow contol calibration procedure (ID: 11219127)

**4.1.2.4.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11219134`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
5G-L2-HI shall end the Initial data routing after the successful completion of flow control calibration as detailed below,

initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct shall be set to False, when the all below conditions are met

 initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = True

 initialDLTrafficRouting = initDLoverF1U

 rdInitialRoutingTimeout has elapsed since the first PDCP PDU was sent over F1-U when initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = True

rdInitialRoutingTimeout is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5686\_replaced([11220898](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IF (“Number of DDDS reports received during flow control calibration” > rdFlowControlCalibrationNum ) AND

(“flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing” = true for last rdFlowControlCalibrationPeriod)



Set the parameters as below:

flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = false

Number of DDDS reports received during flow control calibration = 0

avgDeltaPduDelvDelay = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataFlow = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStall = 0

IF initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = True

IF initialDLTrafficRouting is set to initDLoverF1U

Set initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = False

END

END

END

Number of DDDS reports received during flow control calibration is incremented only after first DL PDCP SDU was received after Bearer Setup.

Incase when the “dataOnFlight = 0”:

 Number of DDDS reports received during flow control calibration is reset to 0,.

 Restart the calibration (refer Note 1).

Note:

1. Calibration shall be executed again for a period defined by rdFlowControlCalibrationPeriod .

rdFlowControlCalibrationNum is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5635\_replaced([11220576](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw84vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdFlowControlCalibrationPeriod is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5677\_replaced([11220811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-10 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Computation of dataOnFlight and dataOutFlowToMac (ID: 11219139)

**4.1.2.4.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11219146`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
[Before 5GC001354-A]

IF Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1

* In case when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev != INVALID SN,

dataOutFlowToMac = Sum of:

(PDU sizes of all PDUs with PDCP sequence number greater than or equal to "highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev") AND (less than or equal to “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.)

* In case when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev = INVALID SN, dataOutFlowToMac = 0
* highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev = PDCP SN of the next PDU (excluding the PDCP PDU which were requested to be discarded as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5325\_replaced([11217991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) sent over the F1U interface after “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev = INVALID SN if no PDCP PDU sent on the inferface after “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* dataOnFlight = dataOnFlight - dataOutFlowToMac

ELSE

 dataOutFlowToMac = 0

[End 5GC001354-A]

[5GC001354-A]

In case Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1

 Perform the procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22459\_replaced([11219153](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxoaDPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1

 Perform the procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22460\_replaced([11219164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxoaDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC001354-A]

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-11 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind Handling for F1-U interface (ID: 11219153)

**4.1.2.4.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11219158`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

* In case when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev != INVALID SN,

dataOutFlowToMac = Sum of:

(PDU sizes of all PDUs (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx" and "PDCP PDU marked for retransmission due to lost packet report" - refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with PDCP SN greater than or equal to highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev AND less than or equal to “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message)

The above calculation should exclude the PDCP SNs which were indicated as lost and dataOnFlight was already decremented in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) considering these lost PDCP SNs.

* In case when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev = INVALID SN, dataOutFlowToMac = 0.
* highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev = PDCP SN of the next PDU (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx" -  refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and excluding the PDCP PDU which were requested to be discarded as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5325\_replaced([11217991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) sent over the F1U interface after “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev = INVALID SN if no PDCP PDU (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) sent over the F1U inferface after “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* dataOnFlight = MAX(dataOnFlight - dataOutFlowToMac, 0)

ELSE

 dataOutFlowToMac = 0

END

NOTE:

1) For implementation of calculating dataOutFlowToMac, please refer to 5G\_L2\_3938\_replaced([11226964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2__ycPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-12 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind Handling for F1-U interface (ID: 11219164)

**4.1.2.4.0-12.0-2**  (ID: `11219179`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

* In case when retransmittedNrUSNPrev != INVALID SN,

retxDataOutflowToMac = Sum of (PDU sizes of all retransmitted PDCP PDUs (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with NR-U SN greater than or equal to retransmittedNrUSNPrev AND less than or equal to NR-U SN mapped to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message)

* In case when retransmittedNrUSNPrev = INVALID SN, retxDataOutflowToMac = 0
* retransmittedNrUSNPrev = NR-U SN of the next PDCP PDU retransmitted (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over the F1U interface after NR-U SN mapped to“Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* retransmittedNrUSNPrev = INVALID SN if no PDCP PDU was retransmitted (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over the F1U inferface after NR-U SN mapped to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* In case when when retransmittedNrUSNPrev != INVALID SN AND

PDCP PDU corresponding to PDCP SN “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS

is not available in the buffer AND

“Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS <= “Highest released PDCP SN”

(refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

* retxdataOutFlowToMac = Sum of (PDU sizes of all retransmitted PDCP PDUs (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with NR-U SN greater than or equal to retransmittedNrUSNPrev) AND (less than NR-U SN mapped to “Highest released PDCP SN” (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the current DDDS).
* retransmittedNrUSNPrev = NR-U SN of the next PDCP PDU retransmitted (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over the F1-U interface after NR-U SN mapped to “Highest released PDCP SN” (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the current DDDS.
* retransmittedNrUSNPrev = INVALID SN if no PDCP PDU retransmitted (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over F1-U inferface after NR-U SN mapped to “Highest released PDCP SN” (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the current DDDS.
* dataOutFlowToMac = dataOutFlowToMac + retxDataOutflowToMac
* dataOnFlight = MAX(dataOnFlight - retxDataOutflowToMac, 0)

ELSE

 retxDataOutflowToMac = 0

END

IF Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 0 AND Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 0,

 dataOutFlowToMac = 0

END

NOTE:

1) For implementation of calculating dataOutFlowToMac, please refer to 5G\_L2\_3938\_replaced([11226964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2__ycPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) PDCP SN mapping to NR-U SN shall be maintained for each PDCP data PDU at 5G-L2-HI.

[CB008717-F]

3) The calculation of the dataOutFlowToMac and dataOnFlight defined above shall be applicable in case of

retransmission PDUs during SCG Bearer takeback for NR DC Split bearers.

[End CB008717-F]

Example 1:

gNB-CU retransmitted the PDCP PDUs shown below after reception of DDDS:

PDCP SN   NR-U SN

11                 1

10                 2

15                 3

12                 4

9                   5

14                 6

8                   7

retransmittedNrUSNPrev = 1

DDDS is received with Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number = 8

retxDataOutflowToMac = Sum of PDCP PDU sizes from NR-U SN 1 to NR-U SN 7 (mapped to PDCP SN 8).

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-13 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Handling of PDCP PDUs marked for Retransmission (ID: 11219186)

**4.1.2.4.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `11219189`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case when Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1 AND highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev != INVALID SN,

For each PDCP PDU with PDCP SN greater than or equal to highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrev AND less than

or equal to “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message, perform the following:

* In case when the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission due to threshold monitoring (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PDCP PDU shall not be retransmitted since it is already indicated as transmitted in current DDDS message (i.e. remove the marking for retransmission of the PDU) (refer NOTE 1).

In case when Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1 AND retransmittedNrUSNPrev != INVALID SN,

For each PDCP PDU with with NR-U SN greater than or equal to retransmittedNrUSNPrev AND less than or equal to NR-U SN mapped to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message, perform the following:

* In case when the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission due to threshold monitoring (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PDCP PDU shall not be retransmitted since it is already indicated as transmitted in the current DDDS message (i.e. remove the marking for retransmission of the PDU).

NOTE:

1) This check is done to avoid unnecessary retransmission of the PDCP PDU for which the transmitted indication is received.

Example:

* PDCP PDU is sent (i.e. Transmitted) over F1-U.
* Threshold 1 monitoring started.
* Threshold 1 exceeded and the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission over X2-U.
* The PDU is not retransmitted for sometime due to flow control decision.
* If the PDU is indicated as Transmitted (via DDDS) over F1-U, then the PDU marked for retransmission over X2-U should NOT be retransmitted.

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-14 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Conditions for uni-directional link failure detection (ID: 11219196)

**4.1.2.4.0-14.0-3**  (ID: `13338372`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
Detection of unidirectional link failure

IF ((f1Available = True) AND

(Bearer Modify message *with Bearer Setup is received) AND*

(PDCP-RLC are not co-located)) (refer *NOTE),*

[Before CB015946-A]

IF dataOnFlight > 0 AND dataOutFlowToMac = 0

numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection = numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection+1

ELSE

numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection = 0

END

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A]

IF dataOnFlight > 0 AND dataOutFlowToMac = 0

timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection = timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection+[Before CB015946-A-UPD001]dddsPeriod[CB015946-A-UPD001]deltaTimeInstDDDS[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

ELSE

timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection = 0

END

[Before CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE: dddsPeriod referred to here is the current used DDDS period value and not the configured value from cplane.[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

[CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE: deltaTimeInstDDDS refers to the instantaneous time difference between the reception of the current DDDS versus the previously received DDDS on the same link.[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

[End CB015946-A]

ELSE

[Before CB015946-A]

numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection = 0

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A]

timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection = 0

[End CB015946-A]

END

*NOTE:*

* If F1-U interface remote IP address received in *Bearer Modify is 0.0.0.0, 5G-L2-HI identifies that the PDCP and RLC are co-located (i.e. Classical deployment).*
* Detection of unidirectional link failure is disabled till 5G-L2-HI receives PDCP-RLC co-location information.
* Detection of unidirectional link failure is disabled for Classical deployment.

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-15 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Condition for execution of uni-directional link failure (ID: 11219216)

**4.1.2.4.0-15.0-3**  (ID: `13338381`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
[Before CB015946-A]

IF numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection > numLinkFailureDlDetectPeriod

Trigger link re-initialization as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5341\_replaced([11218220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetection = 0

END

numLinkFailureDlDetectPeriod is derived as below,

numLinkFailureDlDetectPeriod = roundup(rdLinkFailuretimerPeriod/*dddsPeriod)*

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A]

IF timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection > rdLinkFailureTimerPeriod

Trigger link re-initialization as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5341\_replaced([11218220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetection = 0

END

[End CB015946-A]

rdLinkFailureTimerPeriod is a R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5375\_replaced([11218464](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkvo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For NR DC bearers SCG F1-U link, dddsPeriodXx is to be used. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters.

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-16 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Computation of estimated throughput (ID: 11219236)

**4.1.2.4.0-16.0-3**  (ID: `11219253`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
Update the time stamp of the latest valid DDDS received.

timeInstLastValidDDDSRcv = timeInstDDDSRcv

Note: DDDS is considered as "valid" from this point.

a)  Update the average estimated throughput

instEstTput = dataOutFlowToMac/MIN(deltaTimeInstDDDS, dddsPeriod)

Note: dddsPeriod refers to the current DDDS period either based on

* configuration (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5385\_replaced([11218563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxlWsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or
* updated as part of DDDS period optimization specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5436\_replaced([11229218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5821\_replaced([11222360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kx6t6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or

Note: In the implementation for co-located deployment of PDCP and RLC, gNB-CU-UP indicates the ddds period change to gNB-DU.

* updated as part of DDDS reduction specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5389\_replaced([11218596](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxlWt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: that the DDDS reduction can result in

1. DDDS period of rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod when there is no data (buffer empty) at PDCP and RLC, and

2. DDDS period of rdMinDddsPeriod, or dddsPeriod (based on 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5436\_replaced([11229218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5821\_replaced([11222360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kx6t6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when buffer is non-empty.

3.   The buffer empty condition is when there are no PDCP PDU or PDCP SDU in the buffer and no PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission.

In this case the DDDS period mentioned in point 2 is applicable for throughput estimation due to buffer non-empty.

1) For the case, when avgEstTput =0 AND dataOutFlowToMac > 0,

avgEstTput = instEstTput

2) For the case, when dataOnFlight = 0 AND dataOutFlowToMac = 0 AND flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = FALSE

 Handle silent periods as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5489\_replaced([11219261](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpBHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3) For case, when dataOnFlight > 0 OR dataOutFlowToMac > 0

 Check and handle the data stall as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5492\_replaced([11219272](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpoIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Compute the average estimated throughput as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5494\_replaced([11219294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpoI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* Reset the silent period count.
* numOfSilentPeriod = 0
* timeSinceLastBufferActivity = 0

b)  Compute the estimated throughput

IF flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = true

estTput = max (minThFlowCtrl, avgEstTput, avgRepTput)

ELSE

For non-GBR DRB,

* estTput = max (minThFlowCtrl, avgEstTput)

For GBR DRB [CB008600-C] OR DC-GBR DRB [End CB008600-C]

* estTput = min(DL MFBR, max (DL GFBR, avgEstTput))

DL GFBR and DL MFBR are provided by CPlane during DRB setup

END

avgRepTput is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5425\_replaced([11218832](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxmk2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB008118-A]

NOTE:

* MC-GBR DRB (5QI 65, 66, 67) are handled similar to other GBR DRB with no specific extension.

[End CB008118-A]

Rationale :

* The estimated Throughput(estTput) for GBR DRB [CB008600-C] OR DC-GBR DRB [End CB008600-C] [CB008118-A]OR MC-GBR DRB[End CB008118-A]  is capped to DL MFBR to optimise the buffering at RLC. This also allow PDCP to discard the PDCP SDU(s) exceeding the configured discard timer.

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-17 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Handling of silent period (ID: 11219261)

**4.1.2.4.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11219268`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
a) Increment numOfSilentPeriod by 1.

b)   Increment timeSinceLastBufferActivity by deltaTimeInstDDDS

c) IF numOfSilentPeriod < rdSilentAvgTpFreezeThreshold.

[Before PR666690] avgEstTput = instEstTput \* (rdEthAveConst) + avgEstTput \* (1 – rdEthAveConst) [End PR666690]

[PR666690] avgEstTput = instEstTput \* (rdEthAveConst) + avgEstTput \* (1 – rdEthAveConst) [End PR666690]

END

d) Check if calibration must be enabled due to silent periods.

IF timeSinceLastBufferActivity > rdSilentPeriodThreshold

For non-GBR DRB, set flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = true

For GBR DRB, set avgEstTput = DL MFBR

DL MFBR is provided by CPlane during DRB setup

numOfSilentPeriod = 0

timeSinceLastBufferActivity = 0

avgDeltaPduDelvDelay = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataFlow = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStall = 0

END

Note: In the above case, silent period is detected only when DU has not sent any data to MAC and gNB-CU has not sent at data to DU/eNB. Both conditions are checked to avoid detecting silent period in case intermittent data transfer

rdEthAveConst is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5637\_replaced([11220602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw85vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdSilentPeriodThreshold is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5666\_replaced([11220755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdSilentAvgTpFreezeThreshold is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5667\_replaced([11220770](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rationale:

After inactivity, the throughput estimation at gNB-CU would be be calibrated and hence flow control calibration is started. However for GBR DRB, we do not start calibration, but start with DL MFBR.

Note:

* rdSilentPeriodThreshold is defined in terms of ms. The check for silent period threshold, in terms of absolute time (ms) or number of DDDS periods is left to implementation detail.

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-18 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Conditions for entry and exit of data stall procedure and actions (ID: 11219272)

**4.1.2.4.0-18.0-2**  (ID: `11219287`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
IF flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = false

 Exiting of Data stall

IF numOfDDDSWithDataStall >= rdNumOfDDDSWithDataStallThreshold AND dataOutFlowToMac > 0

numOfDDDSWithDataFlow = numOfDDDSWithDataFlow + 1

IF numOfDDDSWithDataFlow >= rdNumOfDDDSWithDataFlowThreshold

For non-GBR DRB, set flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = true

For GBR DRB [CB008600-C] OR DC-GBR DRB [End CB008600-C], set avgEstTput = DL MFBR

DL MFBR and DL GFBR are provided by CPlane during DRB setup

numOfDDDSWithDataFlow = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStall = 0

avgDeltaPduDelvDelay = 0

END

ELSE

IF dataOutFlowToMac > 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStall = 0

END

END

 Entering Data stall

If dataOutFlowToMac = 0

IF numOfDDDSWithDataFlow > 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStall = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataFlow = 0

END

numOfDDDSWithDataStall = numOfDDDSWithDataStall + 1

END

END

rdNumOfDDDSWithDataStallThreshold is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5680\_replaced([11220848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdNumOfDDDSWithDataFlowThreshold is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5681\_replaced([11220853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB008118-A]

NOTE:

* MC-GBR DRB (5QI 65, 66, 67) are handled similar to other GBR DRB with no specific extension.

[End CB008118-A]

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-19 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Computation of average estimated throughput (ID: 11219294)

**4.1.2.4.0-19.0-3**  (ID: `11219313`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
IF flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = true

If (DBS > dataOnFlight)

instScaledEstTput = (1+ rdScaleTpForCalibration) \* instEstTput

When the scaled instantaneous throughput (instScaledEstTput) > 0, perform the below

IF (DBS / instScaledEstTput > 2 \* maxRlcQueueingDelay)

instEstTput = instScaledEstTput

END

END

In case when instEstTput != 0,

avgEstTput = instEstTput \* (rdEthAveSilentConst) + (1 – rdEthAveSilentConst) \* avgEstTput

ELSE

[Before 04454414]

In case when instEstTput != 0,

avgEstTput = instEstTput \* (tpConst ) + avgEstTput \* (1 – tpConst )

In case when instEstTput == 0,

avgEstTput = avgEstTput \* (1 – rdeThAvgZeroSampleConst)

[04454414]

1. Compute the decay factor:

In case the deltaTimeInstDDDS > dddsPeriod,

 Round the deltaTimeInstDDDS to the nearest multiple of dddsPeriod.

 Compute decayFactor = (deltaTimeInstDDDS/ dddsPeriod) – 1

2. Compute the average eTH as:

a. Update the average eTH based on the computed decay factor:

In case the deltaTimeInstDDDS > dddsPeriod,

 Decay the average eTH based on the delay between DDDS

avgEstTput =

avgEstTput \* (1 – rdeThAvgZeroSampleConst)^decayFactor

Rationale: If the deltaTimeInstDDDS is greater than dddsPeriod, irrespective of the instantaneous throughput the average throughput should be decayed as per the deltaTimeInstDDDS (excludes the action for current DDDS).

b. Compute the average eTH when instEstTput = 0,

 Decay the average eTH as below:

avgEstTput = avgEstTput \* (1 – rdeThAvgZeroSampleConst)

Rationale: When the data on flight > 0 and no DDDS is received due to actDddsPeriodReduction = True implies 0 outflow from MAC layer and no change to other parameters. When this occurs, the average eTH must be decayed for the current DDDS.

c. Compute the average eTH when instEstTput > 0 as:

avgEstTput = instEstTput \* (tpConst) + avgEstTput \* (1 – tpConst)

[End 04454414]

END

[Before 04454414]

If deltaTimeInstDDDS < = 10ms,

* tpConst = rdEthAveConst,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDS > 10ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDS <= 20ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst1,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDS > 20ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDS <= 30ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst2,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDS > 30ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDS <= 40ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst3,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDS > 40ms

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst4,

[04454414]

If dddsPeriod < = 10ms,

* tpConst = rdEthAveConst,

else if dddsPeriod > 10ms AND dddsPeriod <= 20ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst1,

else if dddsPeriod > 20ms AND dddsPeriod <= 30ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst2,

else if dddsPeriod > 30ms AND dddsPeriod <= 40ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst3,

else if dddsPeriod > 40ms

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst4,

[End 04454414]

deltaTimeInstDDDS is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5470\_replaced([11219061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveConst1 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5690\_replaced([11220934](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveConst2 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5691\_replaced([11220942](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveConst3 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5692\_replaced([11220947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveConst4 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5693\_replaced([11220953](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdEthAveConst is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5637\_replaced([11220602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw85vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdEthAveSilentConst is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5638\_replaced([11220616](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw86PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdScaleTpForCalibration is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5678\_replaced([11220823](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAvgZeroSampleConst is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5687\_replaced([11220913](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Parameter name changed from rdeThAveConst to rdEthAveConst. Parameter name changed

from rdeThAveSilentConst to rdEthAveSilentConst.

NOTE:

1. For NR DC bearers, the algorithm parameter maxRlcQueueingDelay is used for MCG F1-U link, the algorithm parameter maxRlcQueueingDelayXx is to be used for SCG F1-U link. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters.

[04454414]

1. dddsPeriod refers to the current DDDS period either based on
2. configuration (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5385\_replaced([11218563](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxlWsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or
3. updated as part of DDDS period optimization specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5436\_replaced([11229218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5821\_replaced([11222360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kx6t6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: that in the implementation for co-located deployment of PDCP and RLC, gNB-CU-UP indicates the ddds period change to gNB-DU.

* updated as part of DDDS reduction specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5406\_replaced([11218696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxl9xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: that the DDDS reduction can result in

1. DDDS period of rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod when there is no data (buffer empty) at PDCP and RLC, and

2. DDDS period of rdMinDddsPeriod, or dddsPeriod (based on 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5436\_replaced([11229218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5406\_replaced([11218696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxl9xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when buffer is non-empty.

In this case the DDDS period mentioned in point 2 is applicable for throughput estimation due to buffer non-empty.

[End 04454414]

#### 4.1.2.4.0-20 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Estimation of PDU delivery delay (ID: 11219322)

**4.1.2.4.0-20.0-2**  (ID: `11219338`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
1) Calculate instantaneous F1 PDU Delivery delay as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5500\_replaced([11219346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxpoKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

2) Calculate average F1-U PDU delivery delay based on historical averaging

a) For case when avgPduDelvDelay = 0

Set avgPduDelvDelay = min(instPduDelvDelay, 2 \* maxTransferDelay)

b) For other case,

avgPduDelvDelay = avgPduDelvDelay\* latencyConst  + ( min(instPduDelvDelay, 2 \* maxTransferDelay) \* (1 – latencyConst  ))

If deltaTimeInstDDDS < = 10ms,

* latencyConst = rdLatencyAveConst,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDS > 10ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDS <= 20ms,

* latencyConst = rdLatencyAveConst1,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDS > 20ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDS <= 30ms,

* latencyConst = rdLatencyAveConst2,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDS > 30ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDS <= 40ms,

* latencyConst = rdLatencyAveConst3,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDS > 40ms

* latencyConst = rdLatencyAveConst4,

deltaTimeInstDDDS is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5470\_replaced([11219061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConst1 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5694\_replaced([11220961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConst2 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5695\_replaced([11220968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConst3 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5696\_replaced([11220973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConst4 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5697\_replaced([11220980](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConst is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5636\_replaced([11220589](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw85PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB008717-DA]For NR DC bearers SCG F1-U link, maxTransferDelayXx is to be used. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters. [End CB008717-DA]

#### 4.1.2.4.0-21 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Estimation of instantaneous PDU delivery delay (ID: 11219346)

**4.1.2.4.0-21.0-1**  (ID: `11219350`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
IF instEstTput=0 AND dataOnFlight > 0

instPduDelvDelay = instPduDelvDelayprevious + deltaTimeInstDDDS

ELSE IF instEstTput=0 AND dataOnFlight = 0

instPduDelvDelay = avgPduDelvDelay

ELSE

instPduDelvDelay =   dataOnFlight / instEstTput

END

---

#### 4.1.2.4.0-22 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Update the PDU delivery delay limit (ID: 11219357)

**4.1.2.4.0-22.0-2**  (ID: `11219371`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
1) For case when flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = true

pduDelvDelayLimit = 2 \* maxTransferDelay;

2) For other case,

pduDelvDelayLimit = min (max (0, avgPduDelvDelay + (DBS/ estTput ) + margin), maxTransferDelay \* 2)

where,

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Parameter | Description |
| minThFlowCtrl, | Defines that Minimum throughput to be used for flow control. This is a vendor specific parameter received at Bearer Setup. |
| maxTransferDelay | Define the max estimated latency/delay for normal flow control operation. This is a parameter received at Bearer Setup.   Note: NIDD parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| margin | Define the additional delay margin. It is calculated as rdTransferDelayMargin% of maxRlcQueueingDelay rdTransferDelayMargin is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5369\_replaced([11218415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkImvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |

[CB008717-DA]For NR DC bearers SCG F1-U link, maxTransferDelayXx, minThFlowCtrlXx and maxRlcQueueingDelayXx are to be used. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters. [End CB008717-DA]

#### 4.1.2.4.0-25 F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Handling reception of VoNR DL Mute flag (ID: 11219404)

**4.1.2.4.0-25.0-1**  (ID: `11219410`)

F1-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
gNB-CU-UP upon receiving the F1-U DDDS message from gNB-DU with VoNR DL Mute flag embedded in GTP-U extension header (Nokia internal) "VoNR DL Mute flag" which signifies DL Air Interface Mute occurance, the same is updated as:

Mute\_Occurance = "DL\_Backhaul\_Mute" (updated from CB013550) OR "VoNR DL Mute flag"

For details on GTP-U extension header (Nokia internal) "VoNR DL Mute flag", refer 5G\_UP\_IF\_14469\_replaced([11547527](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tY-VYvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

### 4.1.2.5 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures

#### 4.1.2.5.0-1 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Update the 3GPP X2-U or Xn-U flow control parameters (ID: 11219421)

**4.1.2.5.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13338403`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
Upon receiving the X2-U DDDS message from eNB, 5G-L2-HI shall execute the below per bearer accordingly and update the corresponding bearer parameters defined 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

* Check and update the DBS as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5520\_replaced([11219436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Update DBS based congestion as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5523\_replaced([11219449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before CB015946-A]

* If the DDDS is too closely spaced as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5529\_replaced([11219472](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPP_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then skip the below steps, ignore the DDDS and end the procedure.

​​​​​​​[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE: The closely spaced DDDS handling shall be guarded with a temporary activation flag actFCCloselySpacedDdds, this is mapped to NRBTS.actInternalImprovements1 (bit 6). The closely spaced DDDS shall be supported when the activation flag is true, and the legacy behaviour of discarding closely spaced DDDS shall be supported if the activation flag is false. The default value of the activation flag will be true. The temporary activation flag is reserved only for 26R3 release and shall be removed in subsequent releases (27R1 onwards).

[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

* Determine the interface availability as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5526\_replaced([11219461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 f conditions for uni-directional link re-initialization are satisfied as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5532\_replaced([11219491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxq2QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 Check and re-initialize the X2-U link as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5535\_replaced([11219503](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxq2RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Skip the below steps and end the procedure.

* Update the uni-directional link re-initialization state as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5538\_replaced([11219517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxq2RvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Check if 5G-L2-HI can end initial data routing as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5541\_replaced([11219528](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxq2SPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Compute dataOnFlight and dataOutFlowToMac as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5544\_replaced([11219548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxq2S_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Update the uni-directional link failure detection as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5547\_replaced([11219597](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxrdVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* If X2-U link is detected as failed and re-initialised as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5550\_replaced([11219618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxrdV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), Skip the below steps and end the procedure.
* Set the time instant of last valid DDDs reception and Calculate Estimated throughput over X2-U as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5553\_replaced([11219630](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxrdWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* In case eNB is congested as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5585\_replaced([11219753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsEbfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) then skip the below steps and end the procedure.
* In case X2-U link is suspended or in Outage as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5588\_replaced([11219764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsEb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), skip the below steps and end the procedure.
* Compute the PDU delivery delay over X2-U as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5568\_replaced([11219701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsEY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Update the PDU delivery delay limit over X2-U as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5582\_replaced([11219732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsEafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rationale for flow control calibration:

1) At Bearer Setup, the estimated throughput will take some time before it reaches a stable value as it is based on the data outflow. During this time, the estimated throughput is set to minThFlowControlX2 or throughput received in "Minimum desired buffer size for UE" to make sure gNB-CU is sending enough data to eNB to maintain good outflow. Also for the average estimated throughput is calculated so that it allows faster ramp up.

2) In case when no data is being sent, the estimated throughput starts to reduce as the outflow reduces. In such case, gNB-CU do not allow the estimated throughput to reduce very low value and freezes the estimated throughput. This allows then when gNB-CU get some data, the flow control algorithm allow to send data to eNB.

3) If the no data transmission is beyond a certain threshold, the value of average estimated throughput becomes quite old and hence in such case when gNB-CU receive data, it starts in the same way as Bearer Setup [5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))].

---

#### 4.1.2.5.0-2 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Updating the DBS based on the transmitted buffer size (ID: 11219436)

**4.1.2.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11219441`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case when Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

Set LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSNXx = “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” IE received in current DDDS message.

In case when Highest delivered NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

Set LatesthighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSNXx = "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" IE received in current DDDS message.

In case when rdCuFlowControlNewDBSEnabled is TRUE, perform the following:

·     Set TxPduBufferSizeXx = 0.

* In case when LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSNXx!= INVALID SN AND LatesthighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSNXx!= INVALID SN,
* Set TxPduBufferSizeXx = Sum of PDU sizes of all PDUs with (PDCP sequence number > LatesthighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSNXx and PDCP sequence number <= LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSNXx)
* In case LatesthighestSuccessfullyDeliveredPdcpSNXx = INVALID SN AND LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSNXx!= INVALID SN,

- Set TxPduBufferSizeXx = Sum of PDU sizes of all PDUs with PDCP sequence number

<= LatestHighestTransmittedPdcpSNXx.

·     In case when (DBSXx!= 0),

- Set DBSXx = max(0, (DBSXx – TxPduBufferSizeXx)

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

[CB008717-B]

2)   The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[End CB008717-B]

#### 4.1.2.5.0-5 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Handling of too closely spaced DDDS (ID: 11219472)

**4.1.2.5.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13338414`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
[Before CB015946-A]

Update the timeInstDDDSRcvXx – set it to the current time.

deltaTimeInstDDDSXx = timeInstDDDSRcvXx – timeInstLastValidDDDSRcvXx

IF deltaTimeInstDDDSXx < 2ms

End the procedure

END

Rationale: If the DDDS are closely spaced it could cause jitter as the PDUs sent out could be minimal and distorts the delay/throughput calculations.

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

2) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

3) If the empty PDCP buffer is detected, the timeInstLastValidDDDSrcv parameter will be adjusted according to the 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32055\_replaced([11220286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvHy_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE:

1) The closely spaced DDDS handling shall be guarded with a temporary activation flag actFCCloselySpacedDdds, this is mapped to NRBTS.actInternalImprovements1 (bit 6). The closely spaced DDDS shall be supported when the activation flag is true, and the legacy behaviour of discarding closely spaced DDDS shall be supported if the activation flag is false. The default value of the activation flag will be true. The temporary activation flag is reserved only for 26R3 release and shall be removed in subsequent releases (27R1 onwards).

[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

#### 4.1.2.5.0-9 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Conditions for ending the initial data routing and execution of flow contol calibration procedure (ID: 11219528)

**4.1.2.5.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11219542`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
5G-L2-HI shall end the Initial data routing after the successful completion of flow control calibration as detailed below,

initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct shall be set to False, when the all below conditions are met

·initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = True

·initialDLTrafficRouting = initDLoverX2U

·rdInitialRoutingTimeout has elapsed since the first PDCP PDU was sent over X2-U when initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = True

Number of DDDS reports received during flow control calibration =0

flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx = 0

IF initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = True

IF initialDLTrafficRouting is set to initDLoverX2U

Set initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = False

END

END

END

Number of DDDS reports received during flow control calibration is incremented only after first DL PDCP SDU was received after Bearer Setup.

Number of DDDS reports received during flow control calibration is reset to 0, when dataOnFlightXx = 0.

rdflowControlCalibrationNumXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16635\_replaced([11220677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdFlowControlCalibrationPeriod is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5677\_replaced([11220811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 4.1.2.5.0-10 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Computation of dataOnFlight and dataOutFlowToMac (ID: 11219548)

**4.1.2.5.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11219554`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
[Before 5GC001354-A] IF Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1

* In case when when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx != INVALID SN,
* dataOutFlowToMac = Sum of PDU sizes of all PDUs with PDCP sequence number greater than or equal to "highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx"  and less than or equal to “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message (refer NOTE 2).
* In case when when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx = INVALID SN, dataOutFlowToMac = 0.
* highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx = PDCP SN of the next PDU (excluding the PDCP PDU which were requested to be discarded as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6531\_replaced([11220543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) sent over the X2U interface after  “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx = INVALID SN if no PDCP PDU sent on the interface after  “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* dataOnFlightXx = dataOnFlightXx - dataOutFlowToMac

ELSE

* dataOutFlowToMac = 0

END

[End 5GC001354-A]

[5GC001354-A]

In case Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1

 Perform the procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22469\_replaced([11219560](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxq2TfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1

 Perform the procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22470\_replaced([11219573](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxrdUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC001354-A]

#### 4.1.2.5.0-11 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind Handling for Xx interface (ID: 11219560)

**4.1.2.5.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11219566`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

* In case when when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx != INVALID SN,

-     dataOutFlowToMac = Sum of PDU sizes of all PDUs (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx" and "PDCP PDU marked for retransmission due to lost packet report" (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) with PDCP SN greater than or equal to highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx  and less than or equal to “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message (refer NOTE 2).

The above calculation should exclude the PDCP SNs which were indicated as lost and dataOnFlightXx was already decremented in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) considering these lost PDCP SNs.

* In case when when highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx = INVALID SN, dataOutFlowToMac = 0.
* highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx = PDCP SN of the next PDU (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  sent over the X2U interface after  “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx = INVALID SN if no PDCP PDU (excluding "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  sent over X2U interface after  “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* dataOnFlightXx = MAX(dataOnFlightXx - dataOutFlowToMac, 0)

ELSE

* dataOutFlowToMac = 0

NOTE:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

2)  For implementation of calculating dataOutFlowToMac, please refer to 5G\_L2\_3938\_replaced([11226964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2__ycPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008717-B]

3)  The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[End CB008717-B]

#### 4.1.2.5.0-12 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind Handling for Xx interface (ID: 11219573)

**4.1.2.5.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11219579`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1,

* In case when when retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx != INVALID SN,

retxdataOutFlowToMac = Sum of (PDU sizes of all retransmitted PDCP PDUs (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with NR-U SN greater than or equal to retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx) AND (less than or equal to NR-U SN mapped to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message)

* In case when when retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx = INVALID SN, retxDataOutflowToMac = 0
* retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx = NR-U SN of the next PDCP PDU retransmitted (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over the X2-U interface after NR-U SN mapped to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.
* retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx = INVALID SN if no PDCP PDU retransmitted (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over X2-U inferface after NR-U SN mapped to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message.

[5GC001354-A-UPD006]

* In case when when retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx != INVALID SN AND

PDCP PDU corresponding to PDCP SN “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS

is not available in the buffer AND

“Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS <= “Highest released PDCP SN”

(refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

* retxdataOutFlowToMac = Sum of (PDU sizes of all retransmitted PDCP PDUs (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with NR-U SN greater than or equal to retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx) AND (less than NR-U SN mapped to “Highest released PDCP SN” (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the current DDDS).
* retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx = NR-U SN of the next PDCP PDU retransmitted (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over the X2-U interface after NR-U SN mapped to “Highest released PDCP SN” (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the current DDDS.
* retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx = INVALID SN if no PDCP PDU retransmitted (i.e. "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx", refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over X2-U inferface after NR-U SN mapped to “Highest released PDCP SN” (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15025\_replaced([11218047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the current DDDS.

[End 5GC001354-A-UPD006]

* dataOutFlowToMac = dataOutFlowToMac  +  retxdataOutFlowToMac
* dataOnFlightXx = MAX(dataOnFlightXx - retxdataOutFlowToMac, 0)

ELSE

 retxdataOutFlowToMac = 0

END

IF Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 0 AND Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 0,

 dataOutFlowToMac = 0

END

NOTE:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

2)  For implementation of calculating dataOutFlowToMac, please refer to 5G\_L2\_3938\_replaced([11226964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2__ycPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008717-B]

3)  The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[End CB008717-B]

#### 4.1.2.5.0-13 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Handling of PDCP PDUs marked for Retransmission (ID: 11219584)

**4.1.2.5.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `11219591`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
In case when Highest Transmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1 AND highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx != INVALID SN

For each PDCP PDU with PDCP SN greater than or equal to highestTransmittedPdcpSNPrevXx  and less than or equal to

“Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message, perform the following:

* In case when the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission due to threshold monitoring (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PDCP PDU shall not be retransmitted since it is already indicated as transmitted in the current DDDS message (i.e. remove the marking for retransmission of the PDU) (refer NOTE 1).

In case when Retransmitted NR PDCP SN Ind = 1 AND retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx != INVALID SN,

For each PDCP PDU with NR-U SN greater than or equal to retransmittedNrUSNPrevXx AND less than or equal to NR-U SN mapped to “Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” of current DDDS message, perform the following:

* In case when the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission due to threshold monitoring (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PDCP PDU shall not be retransmitted since it is already indicated as transmitted in the current DDDS message (i.e. remove the marking for retransmission of the PDU).

NOTE:

1) This check is done to avoid unnecessary retransmission of the PDCP PDU for which the transmitted indication is received.

Example:

* PDCP PDU is sent (i.e. Transmitted) over X2-U.
* Threshold 1 monitoring started.
* Threshold 1 exceeded and the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission over F1-U.
* The PDU is not retransmitted for sometime due to flow control decision.
* If the PDU is indicated as Transmitted (via DDDS) over X2-U, then the PDU marked for retransmission over F1-U should NOT be retransmitted.

---

#### 4.1.2.5.0-14 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Conditions for uni-directional link failure detection (ID: 11219597)

**4.1.2.5.0-14.0-3**  (ID: `13338416`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
Detection of unidirectional link failure

IF ((isXxTputAvailable = True) AND (Bearer Modify message *with Bearer Setup is already received) AND  (PDCP-RLC are not co-located)),*

[Before CB015946-A]

IF dataOnFlightXx > 0 AND dataOutFlowToMac = 0

numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetectionXx = numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetectionXx +1

ELSE

numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetectionXx =0;

END

[End CB015946-A]

[CB015946-A]

IF dataOnFlightXx > 0 AND dataOutFlowToMac = 0

timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetectionXx = timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetectionXx + [Before CB015946-A-UPD001]dddsPeriod[CB015946-A-UPD001]deltaTimeInstDDDS[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

ELSE

timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetectionXx =0

END

[Before CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE: dddsPeriod referred to here is the current used DDDS period value and not the configured value from cplane.[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

[CB015946-A-UPD001]

NOTE: deltaTimeInstDDDS refers to the instantaneous time difference between the reception of the current DDDS versus the previously received DDDS on the same link.[End CB015946-A-UPD001]

[End CB015946-A]

ELSE

[Before CB015946-A]

numOfDDDSForLinkFailureDetectionXx = 0

[CB015946-A]

timeElapsedForDDDSLinkFailureDetectionXx =0

[End CB015946-A]

END

**Note:**

1) Detection of unidirectional link failure is disabled for Classical deployment.

**2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.**

#### 4.1.2.5.0-16 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Computation of estimated throughput (ID: 11219630)

**4.1.2.5.0-16.0-2**  (ID: `11219641`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
Set the time instant of last valid DDDS reception timeInstLastValidDDDSRcvXx = timeInstDDDSRcvXx

Note: DDDS is considered as "valid" from this point.

a)    Update the average estimated throughput over secondary link

[Before PR798938]

instEstTputXx = dataOutFlowToMac/deltaTimeInstDDDSXx

[PR798938]

[Before 04454414]

instEstTputXx = dataOutFlowToMac/ dddsPeriodXx

[04454414]

instEstTputXx = dataOutFlowToMac/MIN(deltaTimeInstDDDS, dddsPeriodXx)

[End 04454414]

Note: dddsPeriodXx refers to the current DDDS period either based on

* configuration (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5395\_replaced([11218642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxlWvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or
* updated as part of DDDS period optimization specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5436\_replaced([11229218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or
* updated as part of DDDS reduction specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5406\_replaced([11218696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxl9xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[04454414]

Note: that the DDDS reduction can result in

1. DDDS period of rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod when there is no data (buffer empty) at PDCP and RLC, and

2. DDDS period of rdMinDddsPeriod, or dddsPeriod (based on 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5436\_replaced([11229218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5821\_replaced([11222360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kx6t6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when buffer is non-empty.

3.   The buffer empty condition is when there are no PDCP PDU or PDCP SDU in the buffer and no PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission.

In this case the DDDS period mentioned in point 2 is applicable for throughput estimation due to buffer non-empty.

[End 04454414]

[End PR798938]

1) For the case, when avgEstTput =0 AND dataOutFlowToMac > 0, avgEstTput = instEstTput

2) For the case, when dataOnFlightXx = 0 AND dataOutFlowToMac = 0 AND flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = FALSE

 Handle silent periods as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5557\_replaced([11219648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxrdXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3) For case, when dataOnFlightXx > 0 OR dataOutFlowToMac > 0

 Check and handle the data stall as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5561\_replaced([11219665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxrdXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Compute the average estimated throughput as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5564\_replaced([11219679](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsEYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* Reset the silent period count
* numOfSilentPeriodXx = 0
* timeSinceLastBufferActivityXx = 0

b) IF flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = true

estTputXx = max (minThFlowCtrlX2, avgEstTputXx, avgRepTputXx)

ELSE

estTputXx = max (minThFlowCtrlX2, avgEstTputXx)

END

avgRepTputXx is defined 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5425\_replaced([11218832](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxmk2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note:

1) minThFlowCtrlX2 is a NIDD parameter. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

3)   The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

4)   minThFlowCtrlX2 NIDD parameter is used for NRDC also. NIDD parameters will be updated in a later subfeature.

#### 4.1.2.5.0-17 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Handling of silent period (ID: 11219648)

**4.1.2.5.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11219656`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
a) Increment numOfSilentPeriodXx by 1.

b) Increment timeSinceLastBufferActivityXx by deltaTimeInstDDDSXx

c) IF numOfSilentPeriodXx < rdSilentAvgTpFreezeThreshold

avgEstTputXx = instEstTputXx \* (rdeThAveConstXx) + avgEstTputX2 \* (1 – rdeThAveConstXx)

d) Check if calibration has to be enabled due to silent periods.

IF timeSinceLastBufferActivityXx > rdSilentPeriodThreshold

flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = True

numOfSilentPeriodXx = 0

timeSinceLastBufferActivityXx = 0

flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStalXx = 0

END

rdSilentPeriodThreshold is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5666\_replaced([11220755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdethAveConstXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16636\_replaced([11220690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdSilentAvgTpFreezeThreshold is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5667\_replaced([11220770](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note :

1) In the above case, silent period is detected only when eNB has not sent any data to MAC and gNB-CU has not sent at data toDU/eNB. Both condition are checked to avoid detecting silent period In case intermittent data transfer

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

3)  rdSilentPeriodThreshold is defined in terms of ms. The check for silent period threshold, in terms of absolute time (ms) or number of DDDS periods is left to implementation detail.

[CB008717-B]

4) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[End CB008717-B]

#### 4.1.2.5.0-18 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Conditions for entry and exit of data stall procedure and actions (ID: 11219665)

**4.1.2.5.0-18.0-1**  (ID: `11219672`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
IF flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = false

c. Exiting of Data stall

IF numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx >= rdNumOfDDDSWithDataStallThreshold AND dataOutFlowToMac > 0

numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx = numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx + 1

IF numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx >= rdNumOfDDDSWithDataFlowThreshold

flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = true

numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx = 0

flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = 0

END

ELSE

IF dataOutFlowToMac > 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx = 0

END

END

d. Entering Data stall

If dataOutFlowToMac = 0

IF numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx > 0

numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx = 0

numOfDDDSWithDataFlowXx = 0

END

numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx = numOfDDDSWithDataStallXx + 1

END

END

rdNumOfDDDSWithDataStallThreshold is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5680\_replaced([11220848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdNumOfDDDSWithDataFlowThreshold is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5681\_replaced([11220853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature

[CB008717-B]

2) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[End CB008717-B]

---

#### 4.1.2.5.0-19 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Computation of average estimated throughput (ID: 11219679)

**4.1.2.5.0-19.0-2**  (ID: `11219692`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
IF flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = True

IF (DBSXx > dataOnFlight)

instScaledEstTputXx = (1+ rdScaleTpForCalibration) \* instEstTputX

* In case when (DBSXx / instScaledEstTputXx > 2 \* rdXxMaxRlcQueueForDBS), instEstTputXx = instScaledEstTputXx.

rdXxMaxRlcQueueForDBS is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16633\_replaced([11218386](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkIlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

END

In case when instEstTputXx!= 0,

avgEstTputXx = instEstTputXx \* (rdeThAveSilentConstXx) + avgEstTputXx \* (1 – rdeThAveSilentConstXx)

ELSE

[Before 04454414]

In case when instEstTputXx!= 0,

avgEstTputXx = instEstTputXx \* (tpConst) + avgEstTputXx \* (1 – tpConst)

In case when instEstTputXx == 0,

avgEstTputXx = avgEstTputXx \* (1 – rdeThAvgZeroSampleConst)

[04454414]

1. Compute the decay factor:

In case the deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > dddsPeriodXx,

 Round the deltaTimeInstDDDSXx to the nearest multiple of dddsPeriod.

 Compute decayFactor = (deltaTimeInstDDDSXx/ dddsPeriodXx) – 1

2. Compute the average eTH as:

a. Update the average eTH based on the computed decay factor

In case the deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > dddsPeriodXx,

 Decay the average eTH based on the delay between DDDS

avgEstTputXx =

avgEstTputXx \* (1 – rdeThAvgZeroSampleConst)^decayFactor

Rationale: If the deltaTimeInstDDDSXx is greater than dddsPeriodXx, irrespective of the instantaneous throughput the average throughput should be decayed as per the deltaTimeInstDDDSXx (excludes the action for current DDDS).

b. Compute the average eTH when instEstTputXx = 0 as,

 Decay the average eTH as below:

avgEstTputXx = avgEstTputXx \* (1 – rdeThAvgZeroSampleConst)

Rationale: When the data on flight > 0 and no DDDS is received due to actDddsPeriodReduction = True implies 0 outflow from MAC layer and no change to other parameters. When this occurs, the average eTH must be decayed for the current DDDS.

c. Compute the average eTH when instEstTputXx > 0 as:

avgEstTputXx = instEstTputXx \* (tpConst) + avgEstTputXx \* (1 – tpConst)

[End 04454414]

END

[Before 04454414]

If deltaTimeInstDDDSXx < = 10ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConstXx

else if deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > 10ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDSXx <= 20ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst1,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > 20ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDSXx <= 30ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst2,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > 30ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDSXx <= 40ms,

* tpConst = rdeThAveConst3,else if deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > 40ms
* tpConst = rdeThAveConst4,

[04454414]

If dddsPeriodXx < = 10ms,

 tpConst = rdeThAveConstXx

else if dddsPeriodXx > 10ms AND dddsPeriodXx <= 20ms,

 tpConst = rdeThAveConst1,

else if dddsPeriodXx > 20ms AND dddsPeriodXx <= 30ms,

 tpConst = rdeThAveConst2,

else if dddsPeriodXx > 30ms AND dddsPeriodXx <= 40ms,

 tpConst = rdeThAveConst3,

else if dddsPeriodXx > 40ms

 tpConst = rdeThAveConst4,

[END 04454414]

deltaTimeInstDDDSXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5529\_replaced([11219472](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPP_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveConst1 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5690\_replaced([11220934](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveConst2 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5691\_replaced([11220942](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveConst3 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5692\_replaced([11220947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveConst4 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5693\_replaced([11220953](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveConstXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16636\_replaced([11220690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdSilentAvgTpFreezeThreshold is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5667\_replaced([11220770](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdScaleTpForCalibration is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5678\_replaced([11220823](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAvgZeroSampleConst is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5687\_replaced([11220913](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdeThAveSilentConstXx  is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16638\_replaced([11220704](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

2)   The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[04454414]

1) dddsPeriodXx refers to the current DDDS period either based on

* configuration (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5395\_replaced([11218642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxlWvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or
* updated as part of DDDS period optimization specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5436\_replaced([11229218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: In the implementation for co-located deployment of PDCP and RLC (ex: Intra-gNB NR-DC), gNB-CU-UP indicates the ddds period change to gNB-DU.

* updated as part of DDDS reduction specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5406\_replaced([11218696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxl9xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: that the DDDS reduction can result in

1. DDDS period (xxDddsPollTimer) of rdMaxDDDSSkipPeriod when there is no data (buffer empty) at PDCP and RLC, and

2. DDDS period (xxDddsPollTimer) of rdMinDddsPeriod, or dddsPeriod (based on 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5436\_replaced([11229218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5821\_replaced([11222360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kx6t6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when buffer is non-empty.

In this case the DDDS period mentioned in point 2 is applicable for throughput estimation due to buffer non-empty.

[End 04454414]

#### 4.1.2.5.0-20 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Estimation of PDU delivery delay (ID: 11219701)

**4.1.2.5.0-20.0-2**  (ID: `11219715`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
Derive the PDU delivery delay over secondary link:

1) Calculate instantaneous secondary link PDU Delivery delay as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5572\_replaced([11219721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsEZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

2) Calculate average secondary link PDU delivery delay based on historical averaging

a)  For case when avgPduDelvDelayXx = 0

Set avgPduDelvDelayXx = min(instPduDelvDelayXx, 2 \* maxTransferDelayX2)

b)  For other case,

avgPduDelvDelayXx = avgPduDelvDelayXx \* (latencyConst  ) + (min(instPduDelvDelayXx, 2 \* maxTransferDelayX2) \* (1 – latencyConst  ))

If deltaTimeInstDDDSXx < = 10ms,

* latencyConst  = rdLatencyAveConstXx,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > 10ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDSXx <= 20ms,

* latencyConst  = rdLatencyAveConst1,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > 20ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDSXx <= 30ms,

* latencyConst  = rdLatencyAveConst2,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > 30ms AND deltaTimeInstDDDSXx <= 40ms,

* latencyConst  = rdLatencyAveConst3,

else if deltaTimeInstDDDSXx > 40ms

* latencyConst  = rdLatencyAveConst4,

deltaTimeInstDDDS is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5529\_replaced([11219472](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPP_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConst1 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5694\_replaced([11220961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConst2 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5695\_replaced([11220968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConst3 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5696\_replaced([11220973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConst4 is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5697\_replaced([11220980](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyyIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdLatencyAveConstXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5657\_replaced([11220719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note:

1) maxTransferDelayX2 is a NIDD parameter. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

3)   The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[Before CB008717-DA]

4)   maxTransferDelayX2 NIDD parameter is used for NR DC secondary link. Flow control related NIDD paramaters will be updated in a later subfeature.

[CB008717-DA]

4) For NR DC bearers SCG F1-U link, maxTransferDelayXx is to be used. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters.

[End CB008717-DA]

---

#### 4.1.2.5.0-21 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Estimation of instantaneous PDU delivery delay (ID: 11219721)

**4.1.2.5.0-21.0-1**  (ID: `11219727`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
IF instEstTputXx =0 AND dataOnFlightXx > 0

instPduDelvDelayXx = instPduDelvDelayXxprevious + deltaTimeInstDDDSXx

ELSE IF instEstTputXx =0 AND dataOnFlightXx = 0

instPduDelvDelayXx = avgPduDelvDelayXx

ELSE

instPduDelvDelayXx =   dataOnFlightXx / instEstTputXx

END

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

[CB008717-B]

2)  The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[End CB008717-B]

---

#### 4.1.2.5.0-22 X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures Update the PDU delivery delay limit (ID: 11219732)

**4.1.2.5.0-22.0-2**  (ID: `11219745`)

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
Update the PDU delivery delay limit over secondary link

1) For case when flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = true

pduDelvDelayLimitXx = 2 \* maxTransferDelayX2;

2) For other case,

pduDelvDelayLimitXx = min (max (0, avgPduDelvDelayXx + (DBSXx / estTputXx) + marginXx), maxTransferDelayX2\* 2)

where,

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Parameter | Description |
| minThFlowCtrlX2 | Defines that Minimum throughput to be used for flow control. |
| maxTransferDelayX2 | Define the max estimated latency/delay for normal flow control operation. |
| marginXx | Define the additional delay margin. It is calculated as rdTransferDelayMarginXx% of rdXxMaxRlcQueueForDBS. rdTransferDelayMarginXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5369\_replaced([11218415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkImvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) rdXxMaxRlcQueueForDBS is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16633\_replaced([11218386](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkIlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). |

Note:

1) minThFlowCtrlX2 and maxTransferDelayX2 are NIDD parameters. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

3)   The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[Before CB008717-DA]

4)   maxTransferDelayX2, minThFlowCtrlX2 NIDD parameters are used for NRDC also. The Flow Control related NIDD parameters will be updated in a later subfeature.

[CB008717-DA]

4)   maxTransferDelayXx, minThFlowCtrlXx NIDD parameters are used for NR DC bearers. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters.

[End CB008717-DA]

X2-U or Xn-U Flow control parameter updating and procedures
