### 4.1.2.6 Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U

#### 4.1.2.6.0-1 Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U 3GPP Flow control of PDCP PDU over F1-U Interface (ID: 11219789)

**4.1.2.6.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11219805`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
When PDCP SDU or PDCP PDU marked for retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is available for transmission over F1-U interface, 5G-L2-HI shall calculate the PDU delivery delay for newly created PDU or PDCP PDU marked for retransmission with the following:

timeDecay = t - timeInstLastValidDDDSRcv, after first DDDS has been received after flow control was intitialised as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5451\_replaced([11218932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

timeDecay = 0, for all other cases.

In case when actDddsReduction is False,

PDUDeliveryDelay =  PDU\_size / estTput + Max (0, dataOnFlight/ estTput - timeDecay )

In case when actDddsReduction is True,

PDUDeliveryDelay =  PDU\_size / estTput + Max (0, dataOnFlight/ estTput - MIN(timeDecay, Max ( rdMaxPduDeliveryDelayDecay, dddsPeriod )

Rationale: This parameter is introduced to take care of the case when there is no DL data                             scheduled and so no DDDS send for a long duration, to limit the amount of decay.

where,

t is the current time in ms,

PDU\_size is the Size of the PDCP SDU + Size of PDCP Header in bytes.

rdMaxPduDeliveryDelayDecay is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13331\_replaced([11221001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxzZIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

dataOnFlight, timeInstLastValidDDDSRcv and estTput is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and updated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5462\_replaced([11218999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB008717-DA]For NR DC bearers SCG F1-U link, dddsPeriodXx is to be used. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on NIDD and algorithm parameters. [End CB008717-DA]

---

#### 4.1.2.6.0-2 Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U 3GPP Flow control of PDCP PDU over X2-U or Xn-U Interface (ID: 11219809)

**4.1.2.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11219822`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
When PDCP SDU or PDCP PDU marked for retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is available for transmission over Secondary link interface, gNB-CU-UP shall calculate estimated delay for newly created PDU or PDCP PDU marked for retransmission with the following:

timeDecay = t - timeInstLastValidDDDSRcvXx, after first DDDS has been received after flow control was intitialised as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5451\_replaced([11218932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

timeDecay = 0, for all other cases.

pduDeliveryDelayXx =  PDU\_size/estTputXx + Max (0, dataOnFlightXx/estTputXx - timeDecay)

where,

t is the current time

PDU\_size is the Size of the PDCP SDU + Size of PDCP Header.

dataOnFlightXx, timeInstLastValidDDDSRcvXx and estTputXx are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5446\_replaced([11218906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and updated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5518\_replaced([11219421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

2)   The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[Before CB008490-D]

3)   Retransmissions for NR DC bearer are not considered in CB008717-B. The delay calculation is applicable for new transmissions only. Interworking with CB001354 will be supported in a later sub-feature.

[CB008490-D]

3) Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. For NR DC bearers, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

#### 4.1.2.6.0-3 Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U Handling PDCP SDU(s)/ PDU(s) stored in the radio bearer data buffer (ID: 11219830)

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11219837`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Handling of PDCP SDU(s)/ PDU(s) stored in the buffer

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11219842`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
[Before 5GC001354-A]

For every unsent PDCP SDU stored in the radio bearer data buffer and allowed for transmission,

* If Bearer type = SN terminated split Bearer, Start of DL data transmission is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6059\_replaced([11226464](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyVkpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* If Bearer type = StandAlone Bearer, Start of DL data transmission is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6149\_replaced([11227524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyc5bPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC001354-A]

[5GC001354-A]

For every unsent PDCP SDU or PDCP PDU marked for retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) stored in the radio bearer data buffer and allowed for transmission in following priority order:

 PDCP PDU marked for retransmission (refer NOTE)

 PDCP SDU

If Bearer type = SN terminated split Bearer, Start of DL data transmission is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6059\_replaced([11226464](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyVkpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If Bearer type = StandAlone Bearer, Start of DL data transmission is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6149\_replaced([11227524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyc5bPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC001354-A]

a. If bearerType = ENDC SN split bearer, execute the steps defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5599\_replaced([11219850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

b. If bearerType =SA bearer, execute the steps defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5622\_replaced([11220178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugr_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008717-B]

c. If bearerType =NR DC Split bearer, execute the steps defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10757\_replaced([11226402](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyU9l_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008717-B]

NOTE:

[5GC001354-A]

* PDCP PDUs marked for retransmission should be sent in order of PDCP SN.

[End 5GC001354-A]

[CB008717-B]

2) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[End CB008717-B]

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11219850`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Flow control actions per PDCP PDU for Split bearer

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11219873`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
1. Initialize the interface availability -Set f1Available = TRUE,

xxAvailable = TRUE

2. Check and update the interface availability as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5601\_replaced([11219880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

3. In case when f1Available = FALSE AND xxAvailable = FALSE, skip the below steps and end the procedure.

4. If f1Available = TRUE, 5G-L2-HI shall execute the algorithm for the PDCP SDU as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5592\_replaced([11219789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to get the PDUDeliveryDelay.

5. If xxAvailable = TRUE, 5G-L2-HI shall execute the algorithm for the PDCP SDU as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5593\_replaced([11219809](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) accordingly to get the PDUDeliveryDelayXx.

6. Check PDCP SDU transmission is allowed as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6752\_replaced([11218311](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxjhjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case when PDCP SDU transmission is not allowed,

* move to step 12.

Note : Window check needs to be performed before choosing the interface to avoid update of dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx.

6a.  In case the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission due to Threshold monitoring (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and  5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

* IF (current time instant - time instant at which the PDCP PDU was marked for retransmission) has exceeded NRBTS/NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpRetxPduSendMaxDelay,
* PDCP PDU shall not be retransmitted since it has exceeded the maximum allowed time for retransmission of the PDU.
* Remove the retransmission marking for the PDCP PDU.
* Skip the below steps and end the procedure for the PDCP PDU.
* IF the total number of PDCP PDUs retransmitted for the DRB that are not yet released, exceeds NRBTS/NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpMaxNumRetxPdu,
* PDCP PDU shall not be retransmitted, since the number of retransmitted PDCP PDUs has reached the maximum limit (refer NOTE 1).
* Skip the below steps and end the procedure for the PDCP PDU.

7. Choose interface for sending the PDCP PDU as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5608\_replaced([11219941](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxtSiPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* In case "PDU sending not allowed over chosen interface",
* Skip the below steps and end the procedure for the PDCP PDU.
* In case the chosen interface is "None",
* move to step 12.

8. if NRDRB.queuingDelayDiscarding= 2 (PI2), 5G-L2-HI shall check if the SDU should be dropped according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24616\_replaced([11223971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyEe6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and end the procedure if the SDU is indeed dropped.

9. Stop flow control timer if running.

10.   If PDCP SDU does not have SN assigned,

* 5G-L2-HI shall assign the SN using the TX\_NEXT variable (5G\_UP\_IF\_3536\_replaced([11531155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWfpKPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* Create the PDCP PDU and perform ciphering as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5628\_replaced([11220228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvHsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: For unacked PDCP PDUs to be resent during mobility, PDCP SN assignment and/or ciphering is not needed. In case PDCP PDUs are stored as unciphered, then ciphering is needed.

1. Send PDCP PDU based on chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5630\_replaced([11220250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvHtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. In case chosen interface is F1-U/ Secondary link AND Duplication is needed over the other interface as per condition defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8910\_replaced([11220484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
3. Send PDCP PDU also on the other interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5630\_replaced([11220250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvHtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
4. Update dataOnFlightXx/ dataOnFlight = dataOnFlightXx/ dataOnFlight + PDU\_size

Note:

PDU\_Size = PDCP SDU Size + PDCP Header Size

Note: In implementation we can ignore the PDCP Header size for sake of simplicity.

13.   In case when the “PDCP SDU/ PDU sending is not allowed” OR “none of the interface was chosen”,

 Start flow control timer [5G\_UP\_ALG\_5293\_replaced([11217660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))], if not running. The timer period is 1ms.

 End the procedure.

NOTE:

1) The PDCP PDU may be considered for retransmission later if the number of retransmitted PDUs is within the maximum defined limit.

[Before CB008490-D]

2)  Steps 6a and 11 are not applicable for NR DC Split bearer.

[CB008490-D]

2) Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. For NR DC bearers, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11219880`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Set the interface availability for Split bearer.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11219902`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
a. If f1DataSendSuspended = TRUE OR f1DataSendPaused = TRUE OR f1RlOutage = TRUE,

set f1Available = FALSE.

b. If xxDataSendSuspended = TRUE OR xxDataSendPaused = TRUE OR xxRlOutage = TRUE, set isXxTputAvailable = FALSE.

c.   In case when DL data split is disabled due to action defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5432\_replaced([11229197](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

* Set isXxTputAvailable, f1Available as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5605\_replaced([11219908](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxtSg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

d. If rdTpBasedLinkAvailableEnabled = True AND dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U AND f1Available = TRUE AND isXxTputAvailable = TRUE,

· Set isXxTputAvailable, f1Available as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5427\_replaced([11218845](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxmk3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

e. In case when packet per ms limit is reached on F1-U as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10955\_replaced([11224706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIwXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), set f1Available = FALSE

f. In case when  [Before CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingX2[Before CB008490-DT][CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx[End CB008490-DT] is set to True [CB008490-DT]refer Note 5 [End CB008490-DT], if the burst size limit is reached for X2-U [CB008490-DT]and Xn-U[End CB008490-DT] , as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17883\_replaced([11219922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxtShfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), set XxAvailable = FALSE.

In case when [Before CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingX2[Before CB008490-DT][CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx[End CB008490-DT] is set to False, when packet per ms limit is reached on X2-U [CB008490-DT]and Xn-U[End CB008490-DT] as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10955\_replaced([11224706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIwXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), set XxAvailable = FALSE.

rdTpBasedLinkAvailableEnabled is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5683\_replaced([11220860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxyLDPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

1) dlDataSplitMode is the algorithm parameter specific for EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent parameter is dlDataSplitModeNrDc. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

3) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

4)  dlOverF1UX2U is used for NRDC also. Flow control NIDD parameters will be updated in a future subfeature.

[CB008490-DT]

5)   NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx is the L2 traffic shaping activation parameter. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17794\_replaced([11224548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIJRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details.

[End CB008490-DT]

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11219908`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Set the interface non availability for Split bearer during CPU overload

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11219914`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
If F1-U is selected for this DRB in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5432\_replaced([11229197](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) AND f1Available = TRUE

isXxTputAvailable = FALSE

[Before CB008717-B]If X2-U is selected for this DRB in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5432\_replaced([11229197](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and isXxTputAvailable = TRUE [End CB008717-B]

[CB008717-B]If secondary link is selected for this DRB in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5432\_replaced([11229197](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and isXxTputAvailable = TRUE [End CB008717-B]

f1Available = FALSE

If F1-U is selected for this DRB in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5432\_replaced([11229197](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and f1Available = FALSE,

If f1DataSendSuspended = FALSE AND  f1RlOutage = FALSE,

isXxTputAvailable = FALSE

[Before CB008717-B]If X2-U is selected for this DRB in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5432\_replaced([11229197](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and isXxTputAvailable = FALSE, [End CB008717-B]

[CB008717-B]If secondary link is selected for this DRB in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5432\_replaced([11229197](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kymqZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and isXxTputAvailable = FALSE, [End CB008717-B]

If xxDataSendSuspended = FALSE AND  xxRlOutage = FALSE ,

f1Available = FALSE

Rationale:

[Before CB008717-B]

When F1-U is chosen for sending DL data due to CPU overload but F1-U is not available, DL data is allowed over X2-U when either F1-U is suspended or radio link outage was detected over F1-U. The same also applicable for X2-U interface. [End CB008717-B]

[CB008717-B]When MCG F1-U is chosen for sending DL data due to CPU overload but F1-U is not available, DL data is allowed over secondary link when either F1-U is suspended or radio link outage was detected over F1-U. The same also applicable for secondary link. [End CB008717-B]

Note:

1) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

[CB008717-B]

2) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[End CB008717-B]

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11219922`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Set the Interface non availability for X2-U or Xn-U due the Traffic Shaping restrictions

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11219936`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
X2-U [CB008490-DT]or Xn-U[End CB008490-DT] interface for this DRB is set to non-available if the "per bearer burst size threshold" per ms (as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17806\_replaced([11224568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIJR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) OR "per bearer-group burst size threshold" (as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17850\_replaced([11224659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIwVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are exceeded. Refer NOTE.

NOTE:

1. The non-availability of the X2-U [CB008490-DT]or Xn-U[End CB008490-DT] interface is temporary and availability shall be checked every ms (as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17806\_replaced([11224568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIJR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and during the next burst period (as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17850\_replaced([11224659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIwVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
2. The bearer traffic shaping is applied only when the L2 Traffic Shaping feature is activated with [Before CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingX2 [CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx[End CB008490-DT] is set to True and applicable only for X2-U [CB008490-DT]and/or Xn-U[End CB008490-DT] interface.

[CB008490-DT]

3.   NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx is the L2 traffic shaping activation parameter. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17794\_replaced([11224548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIJRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details.

[End CB008490-DT]

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11219941`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Choose the interface for sending PDCP PDUs for Split bearer

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `11219967`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
5G-L2-HI shall choose interface as defined below,

1)   Set the chosen interface to None

2) In case when the PDCP PDU to be sent is the PDCP PDU marked for retransmission due to lost PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND NRBTS.NRPDCP\_CUUP.dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UXxU,

In case PDCP PDU is already sent (i.e. transmitted/retransmitted) over the other link (refer NOTE 3) OR

Incase NRBTS.NRFLOWCONTROL\_RETX.reTxPrioritizationType is set to retxPrioSameLink,

a. Choose the interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6565\_replaced([11219975](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxtSj_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

b. In case when [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T] or Secondary link is chosen AND PDU can be sent over the chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5619\_replaced([11220157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 Set the chosen interface accordingly and skip the below steps and end the procedure.

c.    In case when [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T] or Secondary link is chosen AND PDU cannot be sent over the chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5619\_replaced([11220157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 Set the chosen interface to "PDU sending not allowed over chosen interface" and skip the below steps and end the procedure.

[CNI-97440]

3) Choose the interface for ICMP traffic (note that this does not apply to retransmitted ICMP which was considered in point 2 already).

In case the Protocol of IP packet is ICMP (ICMP packet identification is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5303\_replaced([11217785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxgeOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND an interface is selected in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23445\_replaced([11220038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5lvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) AND PDU can be sent over the chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5619\_replaced([11220157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 Set the interface accordingly and skip the below steps and end the procedure.

[End CNI-97440]

[CNI-97376]

4) Choose the interface for the initial routing.

In case the initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = TRUE AND an interface is selected in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23446\_replaced([11220060](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5mfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) AND PDU can be sent over the chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5619\_replaced([11220157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 Set the interface accordingly and skip the below steps and end the procedure.

[End CNI-97376]

5) Choose the interface for data burst as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5345\_replaced([11218246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxi6f_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

a. In case when [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T] or Secondary link is chosen AND PDU can be sent over the chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5619\_replaced([11220157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 Set the chosen interface accordingly and skip the below steps and end the procedure.

6) Choose interface for sending PDCP SDU as below

[Before CB008717-T]

a. Set the chosen interface to F1-U interface when the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5610\_replaced([11220073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5m_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.

b. In case when F1-U was not chosen,

* Set the chosen interface to Secondary link interface when the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5613\_replaced([11220104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5n_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.

[End CB008717-T]

[CB008717-T]

If the Preferred path is set to Primary link:

a. Set the chosen interface to Primary interface when the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5610\_replaced([11220073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5m_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.

b. In case when Primary was not chosen,

* Set the chosen interface to Secondary link interface when the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5613\_replaced([11220104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5n_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.

Else i.e. the Preferred path is set to Secondary link:

a. Set the chosen interface to Secondary interface when the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5613\_replaced([11220104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5n_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.

b. In case when Secondary was not chosen,

* Set the chosen interface to Primary link interface when the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5610\_replaced([11220073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5m_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.

[End CB008717-T]

c. In case when [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T] OR Secondary link was NOT chosen,

* Set the chosen interface according to the interface chosen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5616\_replaced([11220132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

d. In case chosen interface is [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T]/ Secondary link AND PDU cannot be sent over the chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5619\_replaced([11220157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) AND Duplication is needed over the other interface as per condition defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8910\_replaced([11220484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

1. Set the chosen interface to [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T]/ Secondary link (refer NOTE 1).

2.   dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx = dataOnFlight/ dataOnFlightXx + PDU\_size

3.    Skip the below steps and end the procedure.

where,

PDU\_Size = PDCP SDU Size + PDCP Header Size (refer NOTE 2)

e. In case the interface is chosen in the above steps and the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission due to Threshold monitoring (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

* If the chosen interface is same as the interface over which the PDU was last sent, set the chosen interface to "PDU sending not allowed over chosen interface" and skip the below steps and end the procedure.

f.    In case the interface is chosen in the above steps and the PDCP PDU marked for retransmission due to lost PDCP PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND NRBTS.NRPDCP\_CUUP.dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UXxU,

* If the PDCP PDU is already sent (i.e. transmitted/ retransmitted) over the chosen interface (refer NOTE 3), set the chosen interface to "PDU sending not allowed over chosen interface" and skip the below steps and end the procedure.

g.   In case when PDU cannot be sent over the chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5619\_replaced([11220157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

* Set the chosen interface to None.

NOTE:

1) In case sending of the PDCP PDU over [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T]/Secondary link is not allowed as the PDU Delivery limit has reached the max allowed and duplication over the other interface is needed, flow control shall allow the PDCP SDU to be sent over [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T]/Secondary link so that duplication can be done over the other interface.

2) In implementation, we can ignore the PDCP Header size for sake of simplicity.

3) IF the PDCP PDU is initially transmitted over [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T] and later retransmitted over Secondary link due to delay threshold based retransmission and if the PDU is lost over Secondary link interface, the PDU will be marked for retransmission due to lost PDU. In this case, the PDU shall not be retransmitted over [Before CB008717-T]F1-U[End CB008717-T][CB008717-T]Primary[End CB008717-T] since it is already sent once.

4)  The Secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

5) dlDataSplitMode is a NIDD parameter specific for EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent parameter is dlDataSplitModeNrDc. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008717-T]

6)  The Primary link when datasplit is configured, can be MCG F1-U only.

7)  The DL Preferred path functionality is configured via NIDD parameter dlPreferredPath for EN DC and dlPreferredPathNrDc for NR DC bearers. Refer to NIDD parameter details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008717-T]

8)  Interworking with 5GC001354 will be introduced in a later feature. Steps 2, 4e and 4f are not applicable for NR DC.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-7**  (ID: `11219975`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Choose the interface for retransmission of PDCP PDUs for Split bearer

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11219988`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
\* If the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over F1-U interface

OR if F1-U is the preferred interface for retransmission,

* F1-U interface shall be chosen if the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5610\_replaced([11220073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5m_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.
* In case when F1-U was not chosen, X2-U interface shall be

chosen if the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5613\_replaced([11220104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5n_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.

* If the PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) over X2-U interface

OR if X2-U is the preferred interface for retransmission,

* X2-U interface shall be chosen if the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5613\_replaced([11220104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5n_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.
* In case when X2-U was not chosen, F1-U interface shall be

chosen if the conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5610\_replaced([11220073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5m_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met.

* In case when F1-U or X2-U was NOT chosen as per the above conditions,

choose the interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5616\_replaced([11220132](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008490-D]

NOTE:

Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. For NR DC bearers, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-8**  (ID: `11219997`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Choose the interface for lost PDCP PDU Retransmission

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11220010`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
When the PDCP PDU to be sent is PDCP PDU marked for retransmission due to lost PDU (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If

dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UX2U

 PDCP PDU is already sent (i.e. transmitted/retransmitted) over the other link (refer NOTE 1)

OR

NRBTS/NRDRB.nsaDrbParam.reTxPrioritizationType is set to retxPrioSameLink,

* Choose the interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6565\_replaced([11219975](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxtSj_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE:

1) IF the PDCP PDU is initially transmitted over F1-U and later retransmitted over Secondary link due to delay threshold based retransmission and if the PDU is lost over Secondary link interface, the PDU will be marked for retransmission due to lost PDU. In this case, the PDU shall not be retransmitted over F1-U since it is already sent once.

[PR714765]

2) For SA bearers, the value of reTxPrioritizationType shall be fixed to retxPrioSameLink

[End PR714765]

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-9**  (ID: `11220018`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Choose the interface for PDCP PDUs for Split bearer considering Duplication

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11220031`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
In case chosen interface is F1-U/Secondary link AND PDU cannot be sent over the chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5619\_replaced([11220157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) AND Duplication is needed over the other interface as per condition defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8910\_replaced([11220484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

1. Set the chosen interface to F1-U/ Secondary link (refer to NOTE ).

2.   dataOnFlight = dataOnFlight + PDU\_size OR dataOnFlightXx = dataOnFlightXx + PDU\_size

where,

PDU\_Size = PDCP SDU Size + PDCP Header Size (refer to NOTE)

NOTE:

1) In implementation, we can ignore the PDCP Header size for sake of simplicity.

[CB008490-D]

2) Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. For NR DC bearers, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]
