**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-10**  (ID: `11220038`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
ICMP routing

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-10.0-2**  (ID: `11220052`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
For ENDC bearers only and when the IP packet protocol is ICMP:

* IF actFlexibleIcmpRouting = TRUE,
* 5G-L2-Hi shall choose the F1-U link when (primaryULpath = ulOverNrOnly OR primaryULpath = ulSharedPrimaryOverNr), else, 5G-L2-Hi shall choose the X2-U link
* IF actFlexibleIcmpRouting = FALSE, 5G-L2-Hi shall choose the F1-U link.

[CB008490-D]

For SN Terminated Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only and when the IP packet protocol is ICMP:

* IF actFlexibleIcmpRouting = TRUE,
* gNB-CU-UP shall choose the MCG Xn-U link when (primaryULpath = ulOverMCG or ulDataSplit\_PrimaryPathMCG), else, the SCG F1-U link is chosen.
* IF actFlexibleIcmpRouting = FALSE, gNB-CU-UP shall choose the SCG F1-U link.

[End CB008490-D]

Note:

* The actFlexibleIcmpRouting is the activation flag of CNI-97440
* “icmp” packet identification is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5303\_replaced([11217785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxgeOfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Variable primaryULpath is set and updated by CP according to the procedure described in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_11756\_replaced([11250676](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TnYwAPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-11**  (ID: `11220060`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Initial routing

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11220065`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
[CNI-97376] When initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = TRUE:

5G-L2-HI shall choose Primary link when either of the conditions are met:

 initialDLTrafficRouting = initDLoverF1U) OR

 initialDLTrafficRouting = initDLdynamic AND firstDDDSreceivedOnPrimary = TRUE)

In case when Primary link is not chosen above, 5G-L2-HI shall choose Secondary link, when:

 firstDDDSreceivedOnSecondary = TRUE

Rationale: when the CNI-97376 is active i.e. initialDLTrafficRouting = initDLdynamic, L2-Hi will not use the given path until DDDS is received here.

[End CNI-97376]

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-12**  (ID: `11220073`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Evaluate the F1-U interface for data transmission

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-12.0-3**  (ID: `11220097`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
F1-U interface shall be chosen in case when f1Available = TRUE AND one of the below conditions are met:

1. In case when data split mode is set to F1-U only (dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1U).

[Before CNI-97376]

2. In case when data split mode is set to F1-U + Secondary Link, and Initial downlink data routing is active with initial data routing set to F1-U only.

(dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U AND initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = TRUE AND initialDLTrafficRouting = initDLoverF1U)

[End CNI-97376]

3. In case when data split mode is set to F1-U + Secondary Link, Initial downlink data routing had ended, and data split is not allowed.

(dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U AND initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE AND dlDataSplitAllowed = FALSE)

4. In case when data split mode is set to F1-U + Secondary Link, Initial downlink data routing had ended, data split is allowed, and Secondary link is not available.

(dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U AND initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE AND dlDataSplitAllowed = TRUE AND x2Available = FALSE)

5. In case when data split mode is set to F1-U + Secondary Link, Initial downlink data routing had ended, data split is allowed, and Secondary Link is available.

(dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U AND initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE AND dlDataSplitAllowed = TRUE AND x2Available = TRUE)

AND one of the below conditions is met,

5.1. If calibration is ongoing on F1 (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = TRUE) AND

dataOnFlight < DBS \* rdDbsScaleFactorCalibration.

5.2 If calibration is NOT ongoing on F1 (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = FALSE) AND If calibration is ongoing on Secondary link (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingX2 = TRUE) AND  dlAllowMinDelayLinkXxCalib = False AND PDUDeliveryDelay <= pduDelvDelayLimit.

5.3 If calibration is NOT ongoing on F1 (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = FALSE) AND If calibration is ongoing on Secondary link (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingX2 = TRUE) AND dlAllowMinDelayLinkXxCalib = True AND PDUDeliveryDelay <= PDUDeliveryDelayX2 AND PDUDeliveryDelay <= pduDelvDelayLimit.

rdDbsScaleFactorCalibration is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5640\_replaced([11220629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw86vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note:

1)  The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

2)   dlDataSplitMode and initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct are algorithm parameters specific to EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent parameters are dlDataSplitModeNrDc and initDLDataTrafficRoutingActNrDc. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NIDD Parameter details.

3)  Algorithm parameter dlAllowMinDelayLinkXxCalib (NIDD parameter: NRBTS.NRDRB.dlAllowMinDelayLinkXxCalib) is applicable for X2 in the case of EN DC bearers and for SCG F1-U in the case of NR DC bearers. The flow control calibration conditions defined above are applicable to choose the F1-U in the case of EN DC bearers and MCG F1-U in the case of NR DC bearers. The parameter dlAllowMinDelayLinkX2Calib is received during bearer setup.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-13**  (ID: `11220104`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Evaluate the X2-U or Xn-U interface for data transmission.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-13.0-3**  (ID: `11220124`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Secondary link shall be chosen in case when isXxTputAvailable =TRUE and one of the below conditions are met

1. In case when data split mode is set to X2-U (dlDataSplitMode = dlOverX2U).

[Before CNI-97376]

2. In case when the data split mode is set to MCG F1-U + Secondary Link and initial data routing is ongoing with initial downlink data routing set to Secondary Link only.

(dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U AND initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct=TRUE AND initialDLTrafficRouting= initDLoverX2U).

[End CNI-97376]

3. In case when data split mode is set to MCG F1-U + Secondary link, initial data routing had ended, data split is not allowed,

(dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UXxU AND initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE AND dlDataSplitAllowed = FALSE).

3.1 In case MCG F1 is suspended or radio link outage is trigggered over MCG F1-U

(f1DataSendSuspended = TRUE AND f1RlOutage = TRUE)

4. In case when data split mode is set to MCG F1-U + Secondary link, initial data routing had ended, data split is allowed, and MCG F1-U is not available.

(dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U AND initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE AND dlDataSplitAllowed = TRUE AND f1Available = FALSE).

5. In case when data split mode is set to F1-U + X2-U, initial data routing had ended, data split is allowed, F1-U is available and,

(dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U AND initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE AND dlDataSplitAllowed = TRUE AND f1Available = TRUE AND

5.1 If calibration is ongoing for X2-U, if the data on flight over X2-U is less than the scaled desired buffer size over X2-U. (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = TRUE AND dataOnFlightXx < DBSXx \*rdDbsScaleFactorCalibrationXx)

[CB008717-T]

5.2 If calibration is NOT ongoing on Xx (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = FALSE) AND If calibration is ongoing on Primary link (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = TRUE) AND  dlAllowMinDelayLinkXxCalib = False AND PDUDeliveryDelayXx <= pduDelvDelayLimitXx.

5.3 If calibration is NOT ongoing on Xx (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = FALSE) AND If calibration is ongoing on Primary link (flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = TRUE) AND dlAllowMinDelayLinkXxCalib = True AND PDUDeliveryDelayXx <= PDUDeliveryDelay AND PDUDeliveryDelayXx <= pduDelvDelayLimitXx.

[End CB008717-T]

rdDbsScaleFactorCalibrationXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17015\_replaced([11220735](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note:

1) initialDLTrafficRouting and dlDataSplitMode are algorithm parameters specific to EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent parameters are initialDLTrafficRoutingActNrDc and dlDataSplitModeNrDc. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

3)   When DBS = 0 is received in MCG F1-U DDDS, Secondary link shall be choosen only when DL data split is allowed.

For DBS = 0 case, DL data split is allowed if DBS = 0 last for certain number of DDDS. This ensure temporary DBS = 0 does not lead to Seconday link usage.

4) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-14**  (ID: `11220132`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Conditions to evaluate for choosing between F1-U and X2-U Xn-U

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-14.0-3**  (ID: `12566900`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
[Before 04599536]  
In case when data split mode is set to MCG F1-U + Secondary link, initial data routing had ended, data split is allowed, MCG F1-U is available, Secondary link is available, calibration is Not ongoing for MCG F1-U & Secondary link,   
[04599536]  
For Split bearers with EN DC or NR DC configuration, if the dl data split mode is set to use both the links, the initial data routing has ended, downlink data split is allowed and both the links are available and out of calibration, then:  
[End 04599536]

*(dlDataSplitMode = dlOverF1UX2U* AND *initDLDataTrafficRoutingAct = FALSE* AND *dlDataSplitAllowed = TRUE* AND *f1Available = TRUE* AND isXxTputAvailable *= TRUE* AND *flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = FALSE* AND *flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx* = FALSE)***\*******\****

1. Choose the interface with the minimum delay i.e min (PDUDeliveryDelay, pduDeliveryDelayXx)

[Before 04599536]

1. Secondary link shall be chosen for data transmission when all the below conditions are satisfied

2.1. chosen interface is F1-U.

2.2. PDUDeliveryDelay > pduDelvDelayLimit.

2.3. pduDeliveryDelayXx <= pduDelvDelayLimitXx.

2.4.rdAllowAdditionalLimitForXx = withXxMaxTransferDelay OR

(rdAllowAdditionalLimitForXx = withF1MaxTransferDelay AND pduDeliveryDelayXx <= maxTransferDelay\*2)

rdAllowAdditionalLimitForXx is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16634\_replaced([11218398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxkIl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[04599536]

2. The link chosen in step 1 can be overridden to use the other link if the following conditions are satisfied.:

2.1 pduDeliveryDelaychosen > pduDelvDelayLimitchosen  
2.2 pduDeliveryDelayother <= pduDelvDelayLimitother  
2.3 IF (rdAllowChangeChosenLink is equal to allowChangeChosenLinkBalanced AND pduDeliveryDelayother  <= maxTransferDelaychosen \* 2) OR (rdAllowChangeChosenLink is equal to allowChangeChosenLinkUnBalanced)

RATIONALE:

Previously, the override could only happen when preferred path was set to F1U and X2U had to be chosen once F1U delay capacity was completely utilized. The current update of the algorithm makes the override generic and the chosen link irrespective of preference can be overridden. The rdAllowChangeChosenLink allows to configured a balanced delay profile by restricting the other link to the max transfer delay of the chosen link.

NOTE:

1. The chosen link from step 1 is referred with suffix “chosen”, the other link is referred with suffix “other”.

2. rdAllowChangeChosenLink is a R&D parameter defined in [12568548: rdAllowChangeChosenLink](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_k243BCyyEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).  
[End 04599536]

**Note:**

1) dlDataSplitMode is algorithm parameter specific for EN DC bearers. For NR DC bearers, the equivalent parameter is dlDataSplitModeNrDc. Refer to "NIDD parameter for flow control operation" in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5295\_replaced([11217671](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

3) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-15**  (ID: `11220157`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Check if the PDCP PDU can be sent over the chosen interface

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-15.0-2**  (ID: `11220170`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
\* For case when chosen interface is F1-U

a. Set allowPDUSendCalibration = TRUE, when flowCtrlCalibrationOngoing = TRUE AND dataOnFlight < DBS \* rdDbsScaleFactorCalibration

b. For case estimated latency PDUDeliveryDelay   <= pduDelvDelayLimit OR allowPDUSendCalibration =TRUE [PR803222]OR (IF bearerType is GBR AND dataOnFlight is equal to 0, refer Notes 5 and 6)[End PR803222]

Update dataOnFlight = dataOnFlight + PDU\_size

* For case when chosen interface is Secondary link

a. Set allowPDUSendCalibration = TRUE, when flowCtrlCalibrationOngoingXx = TRUE AND dataOnFlightXx < DBS \* rdDbsScaleFactorCalibrationXx

b. For case estimated latency pduDeliveryDelayXx <= pduDelvDelayLimitXx OR allowPDUSendCalibration =TRUE

Update dataOnFlightXx = dataOnFlightXx + PDU\_size.

rdDbsScaleFactorCalibration is R&D parameter defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5640\_replaced([11220629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxw86vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdDbsScaleFactorCalibrationXx is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17015\_replaced([11220735](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note:

1) PDU\_Size = PDCP SDU Size + PDCP Header Size

2)   In implementation we can ignore the PDCP Header size for sake of simplicity.

3) This object refers to parameters related to “X2-U or Xn-U” interfaces and changes prefix "X2" to "Xx" in parameter name, because L2-HI component implements functionalities of X2-U and Xn-U the same way. However, Xn functionality will be implemented in next feature.

4) The secondary link when datasplit is configured, can be either X2-U, SCG F1-U or Xn-U. In the requirements, the secondary link / parameters are generalized as Xx.

[PR803222]

5) For low data rate traffic (low GFBR) with bigger PDCP SDU size, the pduDelivery can be much higher than the pduDeliveryDelayLimit. To avoid data stall, the current PDU is sent out to the lower layers and the subsequent PDU shall be attempted to send only once the dataOnFlight becomes 0.

6) GBR bearer here refers to all GBR QoS profiles includeing Delay-Critical and Mission Critical GBR profiles.

[End PR803222]

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-16**  (ID: `11220178`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Flow control actions per PDCP PDU for SA bearer

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-16.0-2**  (ID: `11220192`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
 Initialize the interface availability -Set f1Available = TRUE, x2Available = TRUE

 Check and update the interface availability as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5624\_replaced([11220199](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 In case when f1Available = FALSE, Exit the procedure.

[Before CB008441-A]

 In case when f1Available = TRUE, 5G-L2-HI shall execute the steps defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5626\_replaced([11220214](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 If the PDU sending is allowed on the chosen interface, stop flow control timer if running.

[End CB008441-A]

[CB008441-A]

 In case when f1Available = TRUE:

 if NRDRB.queuingDelayDiscarding = 2 (PI2), 5G-L2-HI shall check if the SDU should be dropped according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24616\_replaced([11223971](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyEe6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and end the procedure if the SDU is indeed dropped.

 5G-L2-HI shall execute the steps defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5626\_replaced([11220214](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 If the PDU sending is allowed on the chosen interface, stop flow control timer if running.

[End CB008441-A]

 Create the PDCP PDU and perform ciphering as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5628\_replaced([11220228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvHsfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 Send PDCP PDU based on chosen interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5630\_replaced([11220250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvHtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 In case when the “PDCP SDU sending is not allowed” OR “none of the interface was chosen”,

 Start flow control timer [5G\_UP\_ALG\_5293\_replaced([11217660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))], if not running. The timer period is 1ms.

 End the procedure.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-17**  (ID: `11220199`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Set the interface availability for SA bearer.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11220206`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
a. Set x2Available = FALSE,

b. If f1DataSendSuspended = TRUE OR f1DataSendPaused = TRUE OR f1RlOutage = TRUE,

 Set f1Available = FALSE.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-18**  (ID: `11220214`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Interface selection for SA bearer

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-18.0-1**  (ID: `11220220`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
a. 5G-L2-HI shall execute the algorithm for the PDCP SDU as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5592\_replaced([11219789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to get the PDUDeliveryDelay.

b. F1-U shall be chosen as the interface for data transmission, and check if PDU can be sent over the F1-U interface as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5619\_replaced([11220157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxugrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-19**  (ID: `11220228`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Generate the PDCP header and perform ciphering

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-19.0-2**  (ID: `11220243`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
 In case when PDCP SDU has already SN assigned (i.e. if the PDCP SDU is to be retransmitted OR PDCP SDU is received as part of data forwarding with already has SN assigned),

5G-L2-HI shall use the SN to generate the PDCP header and create the PDCP PDU.

 In case when PDCP SDU does not have SN assigned,

5G-L2-HI shall assign the SN using the TX\_NEXT variable according to 5G\_UP\_IF\_3536\_replaced([11531155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tWfpKPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G-L2-HI shall use the SN to generate the PDCP Header and create PDCP PDU.

 [CB008116-A] If Integrity Protection is enabled for the DRB, integrity protection of the PDCP SDU is performed according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11595\_replaced([11223772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyDQx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB008116-A].

 5G-L2-HI shall perform ciphering of the PDCP SDU according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6216\_replaced([11223741](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyDQwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-20**  (ID: `11220250`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Send the PDCP PDU on the chosen interface.

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-20.0-4**  (ID: `11220279`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Send PDCP PDU based on chosen interface

a. For case when chosen interface for data transmission from the above is Primary link,

* "Retransmission flag" shall be set as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6646\_replaced([11220399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* For GBR DRB [CB008600-C]OR DC-GBR DRB[End CB008600-C], [Before CB008600-CA]include the "CU PDCP SDU delay" GTP-U extension header. The CU PDCP SDU delay value(in ms) shall be filled in the "Extension Header Content". The CU PDCP SDU delay value(in ms) = current time(ms) - time instant of PDCP SDU reception at 5G-L2-HI

Refer to 5G\_UP\_IF\_5967\_replaced([11547393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tY8gOfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details of "CU PDCP SDU delay" GTP-U extension header.

[CB008600-CA]include [Before CB008600-CA-UPD001]"Packet Arrival Timestamp"[CB008600-CA-UPD001]"GBR Assistance Information Data"[End CB008600-CA-UPD001] GTP-U extension header. The time of arrival of the PDCP SDU is filled in the "Extension Header Content". Refer to 5G\_UP\_IF\_15562\_replaced([11547608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tY-8fPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on the "Packet Arrival Timestamp" GTP-U extension header.

[End CB008600-CA]

 In case when gNB-CU-UP (PDCP) and gNB-CU-UP (RLC) entities are co-located, gNB-CU-UP shall perform the action as defined in 5G\_L2\_6995\_replaced([11222994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_n_AfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 In case when gNB-CU-UP (PDCP) and gNB-CU-UP (RLC) entities are NOT co-located, gNB-CU-UP shall perform the action defined in 5G\_L2\_6992\_replaced([11222970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_nX_fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

b. For case when chosen interface for data transmission from the above is Secondary link,

* "Retransmission flag" shall be set as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6646\_replaced([11220399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* gNB-CU-UP shall perform the action defined in 5G\_L2\_6993\_replaced([11223026](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_n_BvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* If [Before CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingX2[CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx[End CB008490-DT] is set to True [CB008490-DT]refer Note 3[End CB008490-DT], the bearer level burst size and bearer group level burst size are updated on each PDCP PDU transmission over X2-U [CB008490-DT]and/or Xn-U[End CB008490-DT], and the traffic shaping shall be applied as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17806\_replaced([11224568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIJR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17850\_replaced([11224659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIwVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) respectively.

NOTE:

1) Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. For NR DC bearers, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Glossary.

2) GBR requirements are not applicable to NR DC Split bearers.

[CB008490-DT]

3)   NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx is the L2 traffic shaping activation parameter. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17794\_replaced([11224548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIJRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details.

[End CB008490-DT]

[CB008118-A]

4) MC-GBR DRB (5QI 65, 66, 67) are handled similar to other GBR DRB with no specific extension.

[End CB008118-A]

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-21**  (ID: `11220286`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
Adjusting timeInstLastValidDDDSRcv

---

**4.1.2.6.0-3.0-21.0-1**  (ID: `11220295`)

Flow Control Action over F1-U and X2-U or Xn-U
**[04454414]In case when NRBTS.NRDRB.actDddsReduction is True:**[End 04454414]\*\*\*\*

When the buffer empty  (includes both PDCP PDU and PDCP SDU and no PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission) is detected at gNB-CU **[Before 04454414]and NRBTS.NRDRB.actDddsReduction is True** [04454414] **OR**\*\*\*\*

If there is no DL data sent on the Dl data path (F1-U or Xx-U) during the last rdSilentPeriodThreshold (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5666\_replaced([11220755](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxxj-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), ***\*AND***\*

**If the *Current Time -**timeInstLastValidDDDSrcv \*> ddsPeriod** [End 04454414]*****\***

the time when the gNB-CU last received the DDDS should be adjusted as follows:

 Upon the transmission of first PDCP PDU from gNB-CU to gNB-DU, set the *timeInstLastValidDDDSrcv (and* timeInstLastValidDDDSRcvXx for NR-DC case) to the current time  **[04454414] – *dddsPeriod (refer Note). \*\*[End 04454414]***\*\*\*\*

Rationale: when DDDS reduction is enabled, the periodic DDDS is suppressed from gNB-DU in case of buffer empty. This leads to wrong computation of the delta DDDS time i.e the difference in time between 2 consecutive DDDSs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5470\_replaced([11219061](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5529\_replaced([11219472](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPP_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used to compute the average PDU delivery delay. This is now corrected by considering the time stamp of the first transmission of PDCP PDU from gNB-CU.

**[04454414]**

The time stamp of the first transmission of PDCP PDU is considered with an offset of configured DDDS period (static value – refer Note) so that the first DDDS from RLC triggered based on the first PDU sent is not ignored due to too closely spaced DDDS.

**Note: *dddsPeriod refers to the \*dddsPeriod/dddsPeriodXx received during bearer setup.***\*

**[End 04454414]**

---

### 4.1.2.7 PDCP PDU Transmission State

#### 4.1.2.7.0-1 PDCP PDU Transmission State Transmission states of PDCP PDU (ID: 11220310)

**4.1.2.7.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11220328`)

PDCP PDU Transmission State
\* PDCP PDU shall be in one of the following transmission state after sending of PDU over F1-U or X2-U interface:

* Transmitted:

PDCP PDU is considered as transmitted,

* After sending PDCP PDU first time over single interface.
* After duplicated PDCP PDU is lost over the interface.
* If the PDCP PDU was marked as “Duplicated” before DL data has been suspended due to mobility (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6084\_replaced([11226967](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZPCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and NOTE 1)
* During mobility procedure, if the PDCP PDU state is reset and sent over X2-U/ F1-U (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11773\_replaced([11227034](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZ2GPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/ 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6088\_replaced([11227013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZ2FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/ 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6080\_replaced([11226924](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZPBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and NOTE 3).
* Duplicated:

PDCP PDU is considered as duplicated after,

* Sending PDCP PDU over two interfaces based on conditions specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8910\_replaced([11220484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (refer NOTE 2)
* Retransmitted:

PDCP PDU is considered as retransmitted after retransmission of the PDU,

* During mobility procedure (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11773\_replaced([11227034](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZ2GPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  if PDCP PDU state is reset and sent over X2-U during suspend (refer NOTE 3)
* Due to "lost packet report" received in DDDS (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* Due to Threshold monitoring based retransmission criteria (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* PDCP PDU state shall be reset during PDCP re-establishment since both F1-U and X2-U links are re-initialized.

NOTE:

1. Refer NOTE section in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22474\_replaced([11220335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008490-D]

1. Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NR DC Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

---

#### 4.1.2.7.0-2 PDCP PDU Transmission State NOTE section for Transmission states of PDCP PDU (ID: 11220335)

**4.1.2.7.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11220351`)

PDCP PDU Transmission State
NOTE section of 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8576\_replaced([11220310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvH4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (Transmission states of PDCP PDU) is as follows:

1) PDCP PDUs that are marked as “Duplicated” will be set to "Transmitted" (i.e. Transmitted over X2-U) during mobility suspend procedure. Following is the example that explains the issue if the PDU state is not changed:

1. gNB-CU-UP sends PDCP PDUs with SNs 4, 5, 6, 7, 8 on F1. PDU with SN = 7 is also duplicated to X2.

2. gNB-CU-UP receives DDDS from F1 with highest transmitted SN = 5.

3. Intra gNB mobility with data recovery is completed.

4. gNB-CU-UP starts resending PDUs on new F1 tunnel from SN = 6 (with flow control).

5. Before PDU with SN = 7 (duplicate) is resent, L2-HI receives DDDS from X2 with highest delivered SN = 7

In this case, the PDCP PDU with SN=7 should be deleted (i.e. it should not be re-sent over new F-U tunnel). If the PDU is marked as Duplicated, the DOF will be decremented on F1-U link which is not desired since F1-U is a new tunnel after mobility. Hence PDU state should not be maintained as Duplicated, it should be moved to "Transmitted" (i.e. Transmitted over X2-U) state.

2) If the PDCP PDU is marked as "Retransmitted" (i.e. retransmitted PDCP PDU without NR-U Retx) and if the duplication condition specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8910\_replaced([11220484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is satisfied, PDCP PDU state shall be changed from "Retransmitted" to "Duplicated".

Rationale: Marking it as duplicated will ensure that the discard will not be triggered over X2-U if the delivered indication is received over F1.

Example:

1. gNB-CU-UP sends PDCP PDUs with SN 0 to 10 over X2-U. Highest sent SN over X2-U  = 10.
2. gNB-CU-UP sends PDCP PDUs with SN 11 to 50 over F1-U. Highest sent SN over F1-U  = 50.
3. PDCP PDUs with SN 47, 48 are lost.
4. PDCP PDUs with SN 47, 48 are retransmitted over F1-U and PDU state will be marked "Retransmitted".
5. PDCP PDU with SN 47 is again lost and marked for retransmission.
6. Duplication is triggered, PDCP PDU with SN 47 is sent over F1-U (chosen interface by FC) and duplicated over X2-U based on conditions specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6806\_replaced([11220499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In this case, PDCP PDU state with SN=47 shall now be marked as "Duplicated".

3) During NSA mobility (data recovery), the PDCP PDUs for which the state reset is performed as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11773\_replaced([11227034](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZ2GPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PDUs will be sent over X2-U during suspend. PDU will be marked as "Transmitted" if the SN >= highest sent SN over X2-U, PDU will be marked as "Retransmitted" if the SN < highest sent SN over X2-U.

Example:

a) PDCP PDUs from 1-10, 21-40 are sent over F1-U and are in "Transmitted" state.

Highest sent SN over F1-U = 50.

b) PDCP PDUs from 11-20 are sent over X2-U and are in "Transmitted" state.

Highest sent SN over X2-U = 20.

c) DDDS received over F1-U with "Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" = 6.

d) NSA mobility (with data recovery) is triggered and DL data transmission is suspended over F1-U.

e) PDU state shall be reset for the unacked PDUs of F1-U interface with SN 7-10, 21-40.

PDUs shall be sent over X2-U during suspend based on flow control decision.

PDUs may be sent over X2-U/ new F1-U tunnel after resume based on flow control decision.

If all the uacked PDUs are sent over X2-U tunnel:

- PDUs with SN 7 to 10 < Highest sent SN over X2-U (i.e. 20 as per step b): PDU state shall be "Retransmitted" state after sending over X2-U

- PDUs with SN 21-40 > Highest sent SN over X2-U (i.e. 20 as per step b): PDU state shall be "Transmitted state after sending over X2-U.

[CB008490-D]

NOTE:

Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. For NR DC bearers, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

---

### 4.1.2.8 PDCP PDU Retransmission

#### 4.1.2.8.0-1 PDCP PDU Retransmission PDCP Retransmission PDU (ID: 11220366)

**4.1.2.8.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11220390`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
At gNB-CU:

* PDCP retransmitted PDU (i.e. PDU already sent):

PDCP PDU sent (i.e. not first time transmission) over F1-U or X2-U interface:

* due to "lost packet report" received in DDDS (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) OR
* During mobility procedure (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11773\_replaced([11227034](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZ2GPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))   if PDCP PDU state is reset and sent over X2-U during suspend
* when the threshold monitoring based retransmission criteria is met (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* During SCG bearer takeback for MN Termintated Intra-gNB NR DC split bearers, when the PDCP PDU sent over SCG F1-U is retransmitted over MCG F1-U [CB008490-D]Refer to Note[End CB008490-D]

PDCP retransmitted PDU indicates one of the following,

* retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx: PDCP PDU with NR-U "Retransmission flag" set to '1' OR
* retransmitted PDCP PDU without NR-U Retx: PDCP PDU with NR-U "Retransmission flag" set to '0'. (NOTE: This type of retransmitted PDCP PDU handling is similar to PDCP PDU in "Transmitted" state.)
* PDCP PDU marked for retransmission (i.e. PDU yet to be sent):

PDCP PDU is marked for retransmission in scenarios described in the below requirements,

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11773\_replaced([11227034](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZ2GPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

At gNB-DU:

PDCP retransmitted PDU:

PDCP PDU received with "Retransmission flag = 1" in NR-U DUD.

[CB008490-D]

NOTE:

Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NR DC Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

---

#### 4.1.2.8.0-2 PDCP PDU Retransmission Retransmission flag in NR-U header of DL USER DATA (DUD) (ID: 11220399)

**4.1.2.8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11220407`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
IF (NRBTS/NRDRB.actLostPduFastRetx is TRUE

[5GC001354-C-UPD003] OR NRBTS/NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpDelayThreshRetxMode is equal to 1 or 2 [End 5GC001354-C-UPD003] ) AND

IF the PDCP SN of the PDU to be retransmitted < highest PDCP SN (considering transmission and retransmission PDUs) sent over the interface link,

* "Retransmission flag" shall be set to '1' in NR-U header for the PDCP PDU.

Otherwise,

* "Retransmission flag" shall be set to '0' in NR-U header for the PDCP PDU.

NOTE:

1) Setting of "Retransmission flag" to 1 will ensure the prioritization of retransmission PDUs over other PDUs that are already buffered at gNB-DU/ eNB-RLC.

Example: If Highest PDCP SN sent over F1-U = 50 and Highest PDCP SN sent over X2-U  = 30.

If PDCP PDUs with SN 25, 26, 27, 40, 41, 42, 43 are reported as lost over F1-U and retransmission is to be done over X2-U based on flow control decision,

“Retransmission flag” shall be set to ‘1’ for PDCP SNs 25, 26, 27 since these SNs are < highest PDCP SN sent over X2-U

“Retransmission flag” shall be set to ‘0’ for PDCP SNs 40, 41, 42, 43 since these SNs are > highest PDCP SN sent over X2-U

2) pdcpDelayThreshRetxMode set to '1 - DelayThresh1Enabled' indicates that Delay Threshold based PDU retransmission with Threshold 1 monitoring is enabled.

pdcpDelayThreshRetxMode set to '2 - DelayThresh1and2Enabled' indicates that Delay Threshold based PDU retransmission with Threshold 1 and 2 monitoring is enabled.

---

#### 4.1.2.8.0-3 PDCP PDU Retransmission Delay Threshold based PDCP PDU Retransmission (ID: 11220415)

**4.1.2.8.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11220420`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
Conditions for Delay Threshold based monitoring

---

**4.1.2.8.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11220428`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
Delay threshold monitoring is performed at two levels as shown below:

 Delay threshold 1 monitoring procedure is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22484\_replaced([11220435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (refer Rationale 1).

 Delay threshold 2 monitoring procedure is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22485\_replaced([11220451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvu0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (refer Rationale 2).

Rationale:

1) Delay Threshold 1: It is used to monitor the transmission delay of the PDCP PDU. The transmission delay may occur due to the delay or loss of the PDCP PDU over the F1-U/X2-U interfaces which may lead to t-Reordering timer expiry at the UE.

When Delay threshold 1 exceeds, PDCP PDU retransmission will be triggered based on the conditions described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) Delay Threshold 2: It is used to monitor the delivery delay of the PDCP PDU. The delivery delay may occur due to air link degradation/ RLC retransmissions leading to t-Reordering timer expiry at the UE.

When Delay threshold 2 exceeds, PDCP PDU retransmission will be triggered based on the conditions described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7579\_replaced([11220466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**4.1.2.8.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11220435`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
Delay Threshold 1 monitoring procedure

---

**4.1.2.8.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11220441`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
Conditions for starting the Delay Threshold 1 based monitoring (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7580\_replaced([11220420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Rationale 1) is described below.

Delay Threshold 1 monitoring shall start for the PDCP PDU with SN x in case:

* pdcpDelayThreshRetxMode is equal to 1 or 2 (refer NOTE 1) AND
* dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UX2U AND
* (pdcpDelayThresh1TrigType is equal to 0 (refer NOTE 2) AND

DDDS is received over the other interface with highest transmitted PDCP SN (derived from "Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") [Before 5GC001354-C-UPD004] or highest retransmitted PDCP SN (derived from "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") [End 5GC001354-C-UPD004]  > x)

OR

(pdcpDelayThresh1TrigType is equal to 1 (refer NOTE 2) AND

PDCP PDU is sent over F1-U/X2-U interface)

Conditions for stopping the Delay Threshold 1 monitoring is described below.

Delay Threshold 1 monitoring shall stop in case:

* DDDS is received over F1-U/ X2-U interface indicating successful transmission of the PDU (derived from the IEs "Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" and "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number") OR
* The PDCP PDU is released OR
* [Before 5GC001354-C-UPD001] Radio Link Outage (RLO) is indicated over the interface where the PDCP PDU was sent (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5315\_replaced([11217915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhFT_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) OR [End 5GC001354-C-UPD001]
* DL data transmission is suspended due to Radio Link Failure (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6743\_replaced([11226798](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyYA6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), Intra gNB Mobility with PDCP Re-establishment (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6068\_replaced([11226825](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyYn8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or Intra gNB Mobility with Data Recovery (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6083\_replaced([11226962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZPCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

NOTE:

1) pdcpDelayThreshRetxMode set to '1 - DelayThresh1Enabled' indicates that Delay Threshold based PDU retransmission with Threshold 1 monitoring is enabled.

pdcpDelayThreshRetxMode set to '2 - DelayThresh1and2Enabled' indicates that Delay Threshold based PDU retransmission with Threshold 1 and 2 monitoring is enabled.

2) pdcpDelayThresh1TrigType is equal to '0' - Delay Threshold 1 monitoring is started based on the Highest Transmitted PDCP SN in DDDS received over the other interface link.

pdcpDelayThresh1TrigType is equal to '1' - Delay Threshold 1 monitoring is started after sending the PDCP PDU.

[5GC001354-C-UPD004]

3) Delay Threshold based monitoring shall not be performed for "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx"

[End 5GC001354-C-UPD004]

---

**4.1.2.8.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11220451`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
Delay Threshold 2 monitoring procedure

---

**4.1.2.8.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11220458`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
Conditions for starting the Delay Threshold 2 based monitoring (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7580\_replaced([11220420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Rationale 2) is described below.

Delay Threshold 2 monitoring shall start for the PDCP PDU in case:

* pdcpDelayThreshRetxMode is equal to 2 (refer NOTE 1) AND
* dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UX2U AND
* The DDDS is received over F1-U/ X2-U interface indicating successful transmission of the PDU (derived from the IEs "Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" [Before 5GC001354-C-UPD004] and "Retransmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number" [End 5GC001354-C-UPD004])
* [5GC001354-C-UPD004] AND PDCP PDU is not already sent (i.e. Transmitted/ Retransmitted) over the other interface (refer NOTE 2) [End 5GC001354-C-UPD004]

Conditions for stopping the Delay Threshold 2 monitoring is described below.

Delay Threshold 2 monitoring shall stop in case:

* The PDCP PDU is released OR
* [Before 5GC001354-C-UPD001] Radio Link Outage (RLO) is indicated over the interface where the PDCP PDU was sent (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5315\_replaced([11217915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhFT_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) OR [End 5GC001354-C-UPD001]
* DL data transmission is suspended due to Radio Link Failure (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6743\_replaced([11226798](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyYA6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), Intra gNB Mobility with PDCP Re-establishment (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6068\_replaced([11226825](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyYn8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or Intra gNB Mobility with Data Recovery (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6083\_replaced([11226962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyZPCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

NOTE:

1) pdcpDelayThreshRetxMode set to '1 - DelayThresh1Enabled' indicates that Delay Threshold based PDU retransmission with Threshold 1 monitoring is enabled.

pdcpDelayThreshRetxMode set to '2 - DelayThresh1and2Enabled' indicates that Delay Threshold based PDU retransmission with Threshold 1 and 2 monitoring is enabled.

[5GC001354-C-UPD004]

2) Following is the scenario where the condition is applicable:

a) PDCP PDU with SN 10 is sent over F1-U interface and Threshold 1 monitoring is started.

b) Threshold 1 monitoring time exceeded and PDCP PDU with SN 10 is sent over X2-U interface.

c) DDDS is received over F1-U interface indicating successful transmission of PDCP PDU with SN 10.

d) Threshold 2 monitoring should not be started for this PDU since the PDU is already sent over X2-U.

3) Delay Threshold based monitoring shall not be performed for "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx"

[End 5GC001354-C-UPD004]

---

**4.1.2.8.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11220466`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
Criteria for Delay Threshold based PDCP PDU Retransmission

---

**4.1.2.8.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11220472`)

PDCP PDU Retransmission
PDCP PDU shall be marked for retransmission due to Delay Threshold based monitoring (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7580\_replaced([11220420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if the following conditions are satisfied:

* (current time instant - time instant at which the threshold 1 monitoring was started) has exceeded NRBTS/NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpPduRetxDelayThresh1 (refer NOTE 2)

OR

current time instant - time instant at which the threshold 2 monitoring was started) has exceeded NRBTS/NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpPduRetxDelayThresh2)

* The total number of PDCP PDUs retransmitted for the DRB that are not yet released, does not exceed NRBTS/NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpMaxNumRetxPdu (refer NOTE 3)

PDCP PDU shall NOT be marked for retransmission if the PDU is,

* Duplicated PDCP PDU - refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8910\_replaced([11220484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* "PDCP PDU marked for retransmission due to lost packet report"  (refer NOTE 1 and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6708\_replaced([11220366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxvuw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx"
* Marked for retransmission due to Delay Threshold based monitoring (refer NOTE 4)

NOTE:

1) If the PDCP PDU is already marked for retransmission due to lost packet report, then skip marking the PDCP PDU for retransmission due to threshold monitoring.

2) Threshold value exceeding may be checked periodically for all the PDCP PDU(s) present in the buffer.

3) NRBTS/NRDRB\_PDCP.pdcpMaxNumRetxPdu limits the maximum number of PDCP PDUs retransmitted for the DRB that are not yet indicated as delivered. The maximum value for this parameter has been calculated considering 5Gbps throughput with 80ms RTT and PDU size 1500bytes.

4) This is the case where the PDCP PDU is already marked for retransmission based on the above conditions but the retransmission is blocked for sometime due to the flow control decision.

[5GC001354-C-UPD004]

5) Delay Threshold based monitoring shall not be performed for "retransmitted PDCP PDU with NR-U Retx".

[End 5GC001354-C-UPD004]

---

### 4.1.2.9 Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU

#### 4.1.2.9.0-1 Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU Criteria for Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU (ID: 11220484)

**4.1.2.9.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11220492`)

Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU
Transmission of the duplicate PDCP PDU is allowed if the conditions described below requirements are met:

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6806\_replaced([11220499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) OR
* [5GC001354-A-UPD001] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8911\_replaced([11220520](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV2PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End 5GC001354-A-UPD001]

---

#### 4.1.2.9.0-2 Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU Criteria for Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU over X2-U or Xn-U interface (ID: 11220499)

**4.1.2.9.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11220513`)

Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU
Duplicated transmission of PDCP PDU is allowed on X2-U when the following condition are met

[Before CB008490-D]

* NRBTS/NRDRB.nsaDrbParam.actX2DuplicateTxNSA3x is set to TRUE
* NRBTS/NRDRB.nsaDrbParam.dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UX2U
* X2-U interface is available(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5526\_replaced([11219461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* PDCP SDU is new transmission(no SN assigned) OR PDCP SDU with assigned PDCP SN > Highest PDCP SN sent over X2-U interface.
* (Data on flight on X2-U interface (dataOnFlightXx) is 0 for last tInact ms)  OR

(Data on flight on X2-U interface (dataOnFlightXx) changed from non-zero to zero due to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB008490-D]

* actX2DuplicateTxNSA3x (for NSA bearers) or actXxDuplicateTxNrDc (for NR DC bearers) is set to TRUE
* NRBTS.NRDRB.nsaDrbParam.dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UX2U  for NSA bearers/ NRBTS.NRDRB.nrDcDrbParam.dlDataSplitModeNrDc is set to dlOverF1UXxU for NR DC bearers
* Secondary link is available(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5526\_replaced([11219461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* PDCP SDU is new transmission(no SN assigned) OR PDCP SDU with assigned PDCP SN > Highest PDCP SN sent over Secondary link.
* (Data on flight on Secondary link (dataOnFlightXx) is 0 for last tInact ms)  OR

(Data on flight on Secondary link (dataOnFlightXx) changed from non-zero to zero due to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6475\_replaced([11218109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB008490-D]

Where

[Before CB008490-D]

tInact = max(0, NRBTS/NRDRB.nsaDrbParam.inactPeriodX2PdcpDuplication - DDDS transmission time)

[CB008490-D]

tInact (for NSA bearers) = max(0, inactPeriodX2PdcpDuplication - DDDS transmission time)

tInact (for NR DC bearers) = max(0, inactPeriodXxPdcpDupNrDc - DDDS transmission time)

[End CB008490-D]

DDDS transmission time = T1 – T0

T1 = time instant when dataOnFlightXx changes from non-zero to zero.

After flow control parameters are initialised (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5451\_replaced([11218932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), T1 value is equal to (flow control parameters initialization time instant).

T0 = time instant of reception of DDDS before “T1”.

After flow control parameters are initialised (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5451\_replaced([11218932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxnL6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), T0 value is equal to (flow control parameters initialization time instant – dddsPeriodX2). Decrementing by dddsPeriodX2 is done for simplifying the implementation, leads to early duplication which is acceptable.

NOTE:

1) The condition is explained with below example:

PDCP PDU with SN 10 is sent to X2-U interface at time instant T10, dataOnFlightXx becomes non-empty.

PDCP PDU with SN 10 is indicated as lost in DDDS received over X2-U interface at time instant T11, dataOnFlightXx becomes empty at time instant T11 from gNB pov.

However from eNB pov, the eNB buffer has been empty even before T10 .

This would mean that gNB would have to track the time before T10 when the buffer became empty at eNB.

To avoid complexity of tracking the buffer empty at eNB, duplication would be allowed immediately when dataOnFlightXx become empty due to lost packet.

2) In case when normal case of data transmission if eNB report that lost packet which cause the dataOnFlightXx to become zero, gNB would immediately allow duplication irrespective of the duplication timer. This is done to ease implementation.

[CB008490-D]

3) Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NR DC Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

---

#### 4.1.2.9.0-3 Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU Criteria for Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU for handling PDCP SN rollover case (ID: 11220520)

**4.1.2.9.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11220534`)

Transmission of Duplicate PDCP PDU
Duplicated transmission of PDCP PDU is allowed over the interface when the following conditions are met

1) NRBTS/NRDRB.nsaDrbParam.dlDataSplitMode is set to dlOverF1UX2U  [CB008490-D]for NSA bearers/ NRBTS.NRDRB.nrDcDrbParam.dlDataSplitModeNrDc is set to dlOverF1UXxU for NR DC bearers[End CB008490-D]

2) The DL COUNT gap between the COUNT of the current PDCP PDU to be sent and the COUNT of the last PDCP PDU sent over the interface (F1-U or X2-U) >= (Window\_Size / 2) (refer 5G\_UP\_IF\_3774\_replaced([11533557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tW4DoPv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

3) The interface (F1-U or X2-U) over which the above condition is satisfied, is marked as available (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5468\_replaced([11219049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxny_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/ 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5526\_replaced([11219461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxqPPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

4) PDCP SDU is the new transmission (no SN assigned)

Rationale:

If the DL COUNT gap between the PDCP PDUs transmitted over the interface is greater than or equal to half window size (SN rollover may also occur), gNB may not be able to identify the exact HFN which may lead to incorrect handling of DDDS. To avoid such an issue, a duplicate PDCP PDU shall be sent over the interface whenever the DL COUNT gap is greater than or equal to half of the PDCP window size.

NOTE:

1) The scenario is explained with below example. gNB will not be able to identify if the DDDS received in step d) is for HFN 0 or 1.

a) PDCP PDU with SN 10 (HFN 0) is sent to X2-U interface.

b) DDDS is received over X2-U with “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” = 10 and "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" = 10

c) PDCP PDU with SN 10 (HFN 1) is sent to X2-U interface => here the DL COUNT gap between the PDCP PDU sent in this step and in step a) is more than half of the PDCP window size.

d) DDDS is received over X2-U with “Highest transmitted NR PDCP Sequence Number” = 10 and "Highest successfully delivered NR PDCP Sequence Number" = 10

[CB008490-D]

2) Retransmissions are supported for Inter-gNB NR DC bearers only. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10519\_replaced([11226009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyR6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for NR DC Glossary.

[End CB008490-D]

---

### 4.1.2.10 DL Discard procedure

#### 4.1.2.10.0-1 DL Discard procedure Sending DL Discard Blocks for the delivered PDCP PDUs (ID: 11220550)

**4.1.2.10.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11220556`)

DL Discard procedure
5G-L2-HI shall perform the following if any of the PDCP PDU(s) discarding is required on given interface due to

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5325\_replaced([11217991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxhsWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* [5GC001354-C] OR 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6517\_replaced([11218123](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxiTbPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End 5GC001354-C]

1) Total number of remaining discard block = number of blocks with "consecutive PDCP PDU SNs" that are marked for discarding over the interface.

2) Execute step 2 until Total number of remaining discard block > 0

a) Number of discard block in NR-U DUD = min(Total number of remaining discard block, Max allowed value for "DL discard Number of blocks")

Max allowed value for "DL discard Number of blocks" is defined in 5G\_UP\_IF\_3953\_replaced([11534903](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tXGGFvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

b) Build NR-U DUD (refer 5G\_UP\_IF\_3866\_replaced([11534245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tW_YZvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with,

* "DL discard blocks" shall be set to '1'
* "DL discard Number of blocks" = Number of discard block in NR-U DUD
* Perform the following "DL discard Number of blocks" times:
* "DL discard NR PDCP PDU SN start" = starting SN of the PDCP PDU block to be discarded.
* "Discarded Block size" = number of consecutive NR PDCP PDUs counted from the starting SN to be discarded.
* Send the NR-U DUD over the interface.
* Total number of remaining discard block = Total number of remaining discard block - Number of discard block in NR-U DUD

Note:

1) PDCP PDU(s) are marked for discarding during DDDS processing. These PDCP PDU(s) will be released during the same DDDS processing. Hence 5G-L2-HI shall remember the PDCP SN of such PDCP PDU to allow sending the PDCP SN in the NR-U DUD for discarding

2) NR-U DUD with "DL discard blocks" is sent without any PDCP PDU. This is done to avoid complexity.

Example 1:

Following PDCP SNs are marked for discarding:

53, 54, 55, 56, 61, 62, 68, 69, 70, 71, 78

Block 1 = 53, 54, 55, 56

Block 2 = 61, 62

Block 3 = 68, 69, 70, 71

Block 4 = 78

DL discard Number of blocks = 4

DL discard NR PDCP PDU SN start (Block 1) = 53

Discarded Block size (Block 1) = 4

DL discard NR PDCP PDU SN start (Block 2) = 61

Discarded Block size (Block 2) = 2

DL discard NR PDCP PDU SN start (Block 3) = 68

Discarded Block size (Block 3) = 4

DL discard NR PDCP PDU SN start (Block 4) = 78

Discarded Block size (Block 4) = 1

Example 2:

number of blocks with "consecutive PDCP PDU SNs" that are marked for discarding over the interface.

= 600

In such case 3 NR-U DUD shall be generated and sent with

1) First DUD with DL discard Number of blocks = 244

2) Second DUD with DL discard Number of blocks = 244

3) Third DUD with DL discard Number of blocks = 112

---

#### 4.1.2.11.2 X2 interface only

##### 4.1.2.11.2.0-2 X2 interface only rdAllowMinDelayLinkXxCalibration (ID: 11220664)

**4.1.2.11.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11220669`)

X2 interface only
[Before CNI-88605]

rdAllowMinDelayLinkXxCalibration

[Before CB008717-B]

Description: The parameter is used to choose F1 interface when the delay on F1 is less than delay limit of F1 and current PDU delay on X2. [End CB008717-B]

[CB008717-B]

Description: The parameter is used to choose MCG F1 interface when the delay on MCG F1 is less than delay limit of MCG F1 and current PDU delay on Secondary link.

[End CB008717-B]

Value range: True, False

Default value: False

Unit: N/A

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: N/A

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5610\_replaced([11220073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxt5m_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB008717-B]

Note:

[End CB008717-B]

[End CNI-88605]

## 4.1.3 Flow control disabled

### 4.1.3.0-1 Flow control disabled 5G-L2-HI shall maintain following variables when Flow control is disabled: f1DataSendSuspended -  Indicates that data sending over F1-U is suspended. 5G-L2-HI shall initialize the variables as follows: f1DataSendSuspended = TRUE. Note: During bearer setup 5G-L2-HI shall not receive the DL F1-U TEID and hence we need to suspend the data transfer over F1-U. (ID: 11221021)

## 4.1.4 Flow control optimization for CPU load

### 4.1.4.0-1 Flow control optimization for CPU load Reduction in frequency of flow control algorithm (ID: 11221033)

**4.1.4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11221056`)

Flow control optimization for CPU load
The frequency of flow control algorithm execution has been optimized such that,

Flow control algorithm is executed (as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7830\_replaced([11219837](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxsrevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only once per a certain number of PDCP SDUs (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21583\_replaced([11221064](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxzZK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for a given DRB if one of the below conditions are met

o If the estimated throughput of the DRB is greater than the configured threshold

AND

If the number of bearers in the bearer group (which the DRB belongs to) are less than or equal to a configured threshold.

o If flow control timer has expired.

If the conditions for flow control execution are not met

– flow control timer [5G\_UP\_ALG\_5293\_replaced([11217660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] is started if not already running.

If the conditions for flow control execution are met

– flow control timer [5G\_UP\_ALG\_5293\_replaced([11217660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxf3KPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))] is stopped if running.

 Upon execution of Flow control algorithm for a PDCP SDU of a given DRB, the flow control decision for the DL data path shall be applied to less than (Rationale 1) or equal to a certain number of PDCP SDUs(Note 1) for a given DRB, and If Duplication is needed for a SDU as per conditions defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8910\_replaced([11220484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxwV0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then SDU should be duplicated to other interface.

The above scheme is not used when,

 The PDCP PDU(s) are marked for retransmission (Rationale 2).

[CNI-97440]

 The IP packet protocol is ICMP.

[End CNI-97440]

Rationale:

1. At the time of flow control timer expiry if there are a smaller number of PDCU SDUs in the radio bearer data buffer than the configured value, the Flow control execution is still triggered to avoid delaying the sending of PDCP SDUs.

2. Retransmission of PDCP PDUs could be due to the PDCP PDU(s) being reported as lost or delayed.

Note:

1. Default value for estimated throughput threshold is defined in EFS.

---

### 4.1.4.0-2 Flow control optimization for CPU load Bundle Size of PDCP SDUs for Flow Control Algorithm (ID: 11221064)

**4.1.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11221079`)

Flow control optimization for CPU load
\* If DL traffic shaping is disabled ([Before CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingX2[CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx[End CB008490-DT] = FALSE), the number of PDCP SDUs bundled for the execution of flow control algorithm shall be based upon an internal configurable parameter defined in EFS.
\* If DL traffic shaping is enabled ([Before CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingX2[CB008490-DT]NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx[End CB008490-DT] = TRUE [CB008490-DT]refer Note[End CB008490-DT]), the number of PDCP SDUs bundled for the execution of flow control algorithm shall be restricted to the minimum of the last calculated estimated throughput for the X2-U [CB008490-DT] and/or Xn-U[End CB008490-DT] interface (if X2-U [CB008490-DT] and/or Xn-U[End CB008490-DT] is available), the available bearer group level burst capacity and the internal configured parameter. Refer Rationale.
\* If the X2-U [CB008490-DT] and/or Xn-U[End CB008490-DT] is unavailable due to the traffic shaping, the number of PDCP SDUs for bundling will be based on the internal configurable parameter defined in EFS.

Rationale:

* The bundling of the PDCP SDUs for Flow Control Optimization shall not exceed the estimated throughput at X2-U [CB008490-DT] and/or Xn-U[End CB008490-DT] so that the bearer level traffic shaping (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17806\_replaced([11224568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIJR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and bearer group level traffic shaping (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17850\_replaced([11224659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIwVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) restrictions are always met.

[CB008490-DT]

Note:

* NRBTS/actL2TrafficShapingXx is the L2 traffic shaping activation parameter. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17794\_replaced([11224548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kyIJRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details.

[End CB008490-DT]
